# Dashboard UI/UX Audit — 2026-06-25

> Generated by a multi-agent audit workflow (`dashboard-ux-audit`): 28 pages reviewed section-by-section in parallel (Sonnet reviewers), then synthesized. **617 recommendations** (106 high · 297 med · 214 low).
>
> Reviewed against the current branch `feat/dashboard-overhaul-phase0-2026-06-25` (after PRs A–K), so it does not re-flag already-fixed items.

## Contents
1. [Cross-cutting themes](#cross-cutting-themes) — fixes that land on many pages at once
2. [Prioritized roadmap](#prioritized-roadmap)
3. [Quick wins](#quick-wins)
4. [Per-page detail](#per-page-detail)

---

## Cross-cutting themes

### 1. Decorative serif '.accent' taglines in the h1 bury the functional page signal (count/status) behind editorial prose, hurting scannability, screen-reader page titles, and heading hierarchy. The globals.css comment at line 2374 already flags these spans for removal.

**Affected:** Overview (welcome), Inbox, Recipes list, Approvals queue, Suggestions, Knowledge (Decisions), Activity (Live), Sessions, Transactions, Approval Insights, Connections, Settings

**Recommendation:** Do one sweep across every page-head: strip the <span class='accent'> tagline from the h1 so it reads as a bare noun ('Suggestions', 'Activity', 'Connections', 'Transactions', etc.), and move the explanatory phrase into the existing .editorial-sub slot (or a dismissible HintCard). Where a count exists (installed recipes, pending approvals, live/idle sessions, unseen inbox), promote it into the subtitle with a .num span so the signal renders first. This is a token/component-pattern fix that lands on ~12 pages at once.

### 2. Missing or bespoke loading states — pages render placeholder dashes / 'Loading…' text / empty-state copy / blank null flashes before data arrives, causing layout shift and a 'broken page' first impression, instead of using the existing Skeleton / SkeletonList / SkeletonStatCard primitives.

**Affected:** Recipe detail hub, Recipe edit, Recipe plan, Approval detail, Run detail, Tasks, Settings, Session detail, Analytics

**Recommendation:** Standardize on the existing Skeleton family. Replace every '.empty-state' loading div, bespoke <p>Loading…</p>, '—' placeholder, and Suspense fallback={null} with the matching primitive (SkeletonStatCard for stat grids, SkeletonList rows/columns for tables, tall Skeleton for editor/code areas), gated on an explicit 'response === undefined' (not-yet-fetched) check rather than an empty-array fallback so the empty state never flickers before data.

### 3. Error and empty states are hand-rolled (raw .alert-err divs, inline paragraphs, bespoke EmptyState copy) instead of the shared ErrorState / EmptyState primitives — so they lack role='alert', icons, a retry affordance, and filter-aware messaging, and they look inconsistent page-to-page.

**Affected:** Recipe plan, Recipe compare, Approvals queue, Approval detail, Traces, Transactions, Session detail, Insights Replay, Knowledge (Decisions), Recipe detail hub

**Recommendation:** Replace every inline error/empty surface with <ErrorState error onRetry .../> and <EmptyState .../> from @/components/patchwork, wiring onRetry to the existing fetch/refetch callback. Make list EmptyStates filter-aware: when any filter/search is active, switch copy to 'No matching results · clear filters' with a Clear-filters action rather than the first-run 'nothing recorded yet' text (Traces, Insights Replay).

### 4. Undefined design tokens (var(--border), --border-default, --border-subtle, --card-bg) silently resolve to no-border / transparent / initial, and dark-theme hex fallbacks (--ok-bg #1b3a1b, --warn-bg #3a2a1b) break contrast in the light 'paper' theme. Borders and surfaces ship invisibly broken.

**Affected:** Run detail, Recipe edit, Approval detail, Marketplace

**Recommendation:** Grep the dashboard for the non-canonical tokens and replace with the real ones: --border/--border-default/--border-subtle → --line-2; --card-bg → --surface (or --bg-2). Define --ok-bg and --warn-bg under :root[data-theme='paper'] using color-mix so the dark-theme hex fallbacks are never reached. Add a lint/CI check that fails on token names outside the documented set to prevent regressions.

### 5. Faint and undersized text fails WCAG AA: chart/section labels at --fs-2xs (10px) in --ink-3, decision/status pills at 10px, and stat sub-labels in --ink-3 are below the small-text contrast and size minimums on both themes.

**Affected:** Activity (Live), Analytics, Approval Insights, Insights Replay, Settings, Login

**Recommendation:** Establish a floor: no informational/label text below --fs-xs (11px), and bump --ink-3 informational labels to --ink-2. Apply to chart card titles ('Events / minute', 'Calls — last 24 hours'), replay/insight pills (raise the primary 'Change' column to --fs-s), the Settings default-model line, and the Login submit button (--fs-s → --fs-base). Codify as a token/utility rule so future labels inherit the safe size.

### 6. window.confirm() native browser dialogs used for destructive actions — unstyleable, untestable, blocked in some embedded contexts, and a jarring break from the design language. The shared Dialog primitive is already imported on these pages.

**Affected:** Inbox, Recipes list, Recipe detail hub

**Recommendation:** Replace all window.confirm() destructive-action gates (Archive, Delete, Disable, Uninstall) with the shared Dialog component, following the existing RunModal pattern — danger variant for Delete/Uninstall, default for Archive — with proper focus trap, Escape-to-cancel, and testable confirm/cancel buttons.

### 7. ARIA role misuse for selection / toggle / tab patterns — aria-pressed used for single-select and tabs, role='link' on <tr>, role='switch' on a duplicate disconnect control, missing aria-expanded on expandable cards, and tablists with no tab semantics — so assistive tech can't convey selection, mutual exclusion, or expand/collapse state.

**Affected:** Inbox, Recipes list, Recipe edit, Run detail, Sessions, Session detail, Connections, Settings, Global chrome (Shell — on every page)

**Recommendation:** Audit interactive widgets against the right ARIA pattern: listbox/option + aria-selected for single-select lists (Inbox sidebar); radiogroup/radio + aria-checked for segmented controls (Recipe edit mode toggle); tablist/tab/tabpanel + aria-selected for tab bars (Run detail); remove role='link' from <tr> and make the inner anchor the focus target (Recipes); add aria-expanded + aria-controls to expandable cards (Sessions, Session detail); role='navigation'/'search' landmarks (Settings nav, Connections filter). Bake correct ARIA into the shared list/tab/segmented-control components so it propagates.

### 8. Touch targets below the 44×44 WCAG minimum — dismiss (✕) buttons and icon-only controls with 0–4px padding, tiny hit areas, and low-contrast --ink-3 icon color.

**Affected:** Inbox, Recipe edit, Suggestions

**Recommendation:** Add a shared icon-button/dismiss-button class enforcing min 44×44 (or 36px minimum with 8px gap from neighbors), flex-centered, with icon color at --ink-1/--ink-0 for contrast. Apply to all ✕ dismiss buttons (Inbox discovery banner, Recipe-edit save-error banner, Suggestion rows) so the fix is one class everywhere.

### 9. Components bypass the shared component system with all-inline styles and hand-rolled status pills / stat cells, diverging from the token contract so future design changes don't reach them.

**Affected:** Inbox, Recipes list, Approvals queue, Session detail, Analytics, Approval Insights, Login

**Recommendation:** Replace bespoke pills/cells with primitives: hand-rolled status pills → StatusPill (RecipeHubCard, RiskMeter dedupe on Approvals); duplicated inline stat cells → StatCard + AnimatedNumber (Session detail's four cells, Insights summary pills, Analytics' local useCountUp → AnimatedNumber which has prefers-reduced-motion built in); wrap the Login form in PatchCard/GlassCard. Delete the per-page STATUS_COLOR maps and useCountUp hooks.

### 10. Mobile / responsive parity gaps — desktop-only data and layouts not ported to small viewports, and sticky bulk-action bars that fall below the fold.

**Affected:** Runs list, Recipes list, Recipe new (create), Approvals queue, Approval Insights, Marketplace

**Recommendation:** Close data-parity gaps (port assertion-failure detail into Runs mobile card; port slug preview into Recipe-new mobile flow where the YAML preview is off-screen), make bulk-action toolbars position:sticky bottom (Approvals BatchActionBar), add ellipsis truncation for long namespaced tool names (Approval Insights), and verify two-column grids actually collapse/expand at breakpoints (Marketplace submit recipe-submit-layout).

---

## Prioritized roadmap

**1. `HIGH` Fix all undefined/wrong design tokens and define light-theme --ok-bg/--warn-bg, then add a CI lint that rejects token names outside the documented set.**

- *Why:* Borders, surfaces, and pill backgrounds currently render invisibly broken or wrong-contrast (especially in the paper/light theme) on Run detail, Recipe edit, Approval detail, and Marketplace. It's a low-effort, zero-regression find-and-replace that quietly improves every affected surface and the CI gate prevents the class from recurring.
- *Scope:* Run detail, Recipe edit, Approval detail, Marketplace; globals.css :root[data-theme='paper'] block; CI

**2. `HIGH` Add a global text-legibility floor: no informational label below --fs-xs (11px); bump --ink-3 labels to --ink-2.**

- *Why:* 10px/--ink-3 chart titles, decision pills, and stat sub-labels fail WCAG AA on both themes across Analytics, Activity, Insights, Insights Replay, Settings, and Login. A token/utility-level rule fixes contrast everywhere at once and is the broadest accessibility win available.
- *Scope:* Activity, Analytics, Approval Insights, Insights Replay, Settings, Login (chart labels, pills, stat sub-labels, submit button)

**3. `HIGH` Standardize loading states on the Skeleton / SkeletonList / SkeletonStatCard primitives, gated on 'response === undefined'.**

- *Why:* Nine pages flash placeholder dashes, 'Unknown' h1s, empty-state copy, or blank null renders before data arrives, reading as broken and causing layout shift on every navigation. The primitives already exist and are unused; this is the highest-frequency first-impression defect.
- *Scope:* Recipe detail hub, Recipe edit, Recipe plan, Approval detail, Run detail, Tasks, Settings, Session detail, Analytics

**4. `HIGH` Replace all hand-rolled error/empty surfaces with ErrorState/EmptyState primitives, wire onRetry, and make list empty states filter-aware.**

- *Why:* Raw .alert-err divs and inline empty paragraphs across ten pages lack role='alert', icons, and any recovery path, and 'nothing recorded yet' copy shows even when filters produced zero results — eroding trust. One primitive swap adds a11y + retry + consistency everywhere.
- *Scope:* Recipe plan, Recipe compare, Approvals queue, Approval detail, Traces, Transactions, Session detail, Insights Replay, Decisions, Recipe detail hub

**5. `HIGH` Strip decorative serif '.accent' h1 taglines across all page-heads; move copy to .editorial-sub/HintCard and promote counts into the subtitle.**

- *Why:* On ~12 pages the page name is buried behind editorial prose, hurting scannability, screen-reader titles, and heading hierarchy; the CSS already flags these spans for removal. Single repeated pattern, broad reach, near-zero risk.
- *Scope:* Overview, Inbox, Recipes, Approvals, Suggestions, Decisions, Activity, Sessions, Transactions, Insights, Connections, Settings

**6. `HIGH` Audit and fix ARIA patterns for lists, tabs, segmented controls, and expandable cards; add missing landmarks; bake correct semantics into shared components.**

- *Why:* Selection, mutual exclusion, tab state, and expand/collapse are invisible to assistive tech on nine pages (aria-pressed misuse, role='link' on <tr>, missing aria-expanded, no tablist). Fixing the shared list/tab/segmented-control components propagates the correct semantics broadly.
- *Scope:* Inbox, Recipes list, Recipe edit, Run detail, Sessions, Session detail, Connections, Settings, Shell

**7. `MED` Replace all window.confirm() destructive-action gates with the shared Dialog primitive (focus trap + Escape), danger/default variants.**

- *Why:* Archive/Delete/Disable/Uninstall on three core operator pages use unstyleable, untestable native dialogs that break the design language; Dialog is already imported. Destructive-action safety + consistency.
- *Scope:* Inbox, Recipes list, Recipe detail hub

**8. `MED` Introduce a shared icon-button/dismiss-button class enforcing ≥44×44 (or 36px + 8px gap) with high-contrast icon color, and apply to all ✕ controls.**

- *Why:* Multiple dismiss buttons are sub-target-size and near-invisible (--ink-3), causing mis-taps on mobile. One class fixes all instances and future-proofs new icon buttons.
- *Scope:* Inbox discovery banner, Recipe-edit save-error banner, Suggestion rows; shared button CSS

**9. `MED` Mount the already-built TopBarBreadcrumb in the Shell header and upgrade BridgeOfflineBanner role from 'status' to 'alert'.**

- *Why:* Breadcrumb is a fully-implemented dead component, leaving every deep page (recipe/run/session detail) with no top-bar wayfinding; the offline banner announces politely despite the dashboard being non-functional offline. Both fix every page at once via the shell.
- *Scope:* Global chrome (Shell) — affects all pages

**10. `MED` Replace remaining bespoke pills/stat cells/animation hooks with primitives (StatusPill, StatCard+AnimatedNumber) and wrap the Login form in a card.**

- *Why:* Inline status pills and duplicated stat cells diverge from the token contract so design changes won't reach them; AnimatedNumber already has the prefers-reduced-motion guard the local useCountUp lacks. Reduces code and unifies behavior.
- *Scope:* Recipes list (RecipeHubCard), Approvals (RiskMeter dedupe), Session detail, Analytics, Approval Insights, Login

**11. `MED` Close mobile/responsive parity gaps and make bulk-action bars sticky.**

- *Why:* Mobile users lose primary failure signal (Runs assertion detail) and creation feedback (Recipe-new slug preview); batch action bars fall below the fold (Approvals). Straight data/interaction parity fixes for primary workflows.
- *Scope:* Runs list, Recipe new, Approvals queue, Approval Insights, Marketplace

**12. `MED` Reorder safety-critical signals above the fold: Marketplace TrustMetadataCard/TrustDivergenceNotice above the YAML preview; Overview LiveWire above Telemetry; Recipe detail-hub top halt-fix hint inline.**

- *Why:* Users make install/run decisions before scrolling past hundreds of lines of YAML or hovering tooltips; surfacing the trust/heartbeat/fix signal where the eye lands prevents silent unsafe actions. Targeted but high-stakes.
- *Scope:* Marketplace, Overview, Recipe detail hub

**13. `LOW` Fill diff/compare data gaps and dual-action conflicts: Recipe compare removed-step rows + in-page recipe selector; Traces flat-view recipe-col expand/navigate conflict; Traces tree-view missing quick actions.**

- *Why:* Core diff/compare workflows are currently broken or undiscoverable (blank removed rows, URL-editing required, overlapping click targets). Per-page but directly defeats the page's purpose.
- *Scope:* Recipe compare, Traces

**14. `LOW` Improve filter discoverability and table semantics: Runs status <select> + halt-pill hover affordance; Analytics/Insights table <thead> + scope='col' + sr-only headers + caption.**

- *Why:* Fundamental filters and column meaning are hidden behind card interactions and glyph-only headers; adds discoverability and screen-reader/keyboard access. Moderate-reach polish.
- *Scope:* Runs list, Analytics, Approval Insights, Activity (table caption/scope)

---

## Quick wins

- Recipes list / Overview leaderboard: wrap recipe names in recipeDisplayName() so 'morning-brief' renders as 'Morning Brief', matching the kanban directly above it.
- Recipe new: add className='btn primary' to the 'Create YAML draft' submit button (line ~1587) so the primary action is visually dominant.
- Login: change the submit button font-size from --fs-s (12px) to --fs-base (14px).
- Activity: add <caption className='sr-only'>Live activity events</caption> and scope='col' on the event-table <th> elements.
- Login error <p>: add role='alert' and aria-live='polite' so failed logins are announced.
- Approval detail: add aria-label to the ✓ Approve / ✗ Reject buttons and aria-hidden='true' on the glyph spans; remove the decorative 'JSON' pill; cap the Parameters <pre> with max-height:320 + overflow-y:auto.
- Recipe new: add aria-expanded={aiOpen} + aria-controls='ai-panel' to the AI-generation toggle and id='ai-panel' on the panel.
- Recipe edit deep-link banner: replace the undefined var(--border-default) with var(--line-2).
- Run detail JudgeVerdictPill: change borderLeft 'var(--border)' to 'var(--line-2)'.
- Settings driver list: enumerate delegation-policy select options human-first ('No gating (off)' not 'off — no gating'); add role='navigation' + aria-label='Settings sections' to the side nav.
- Sessions: replace the <a href> 'Open detail →' with Next.js <Link href> to restore client-side navigation.
- Transactions: add aria-label={`Discard transaction ${tx.id}`} to each Discard button and role='alert' on the stale-data .alert-err banner.
- Overview LiveRunsStrip: replace the redundant 'running · Xm Xs' meta with 'started relTime(r.startedAt)' so it adds info instead of duplicating the LivePill.
- Recipe detail hub: change the disabled Run-now button title to 'Recipe is disabled — enable it first' and add an inline --ink-3 hint below the action bar.
- Recipe plan / lint section: add role='alert' to the lint error container and normalize the prompt cell to --fs-xs.

---

## Per-page detail

### Overview (welcome)  `/`

**Top 3:**
1. Move LiveWire above the Telemetry section (currently buried after the leaderboard where it cannot serve as an always-on page heartbeat) and move the FirstRunChecklist below the hero to stop it blocking the NeedsAttentionBand on every subsequent visit.
2. Apply recipeDisplayName() in the RecipeLeaderboard rows so recipe names are human-readable ('Morning Brief') instead of raw canonical keys ('morning-brief') — the kanban 40px above already uses display names, creating a jarring inconsistency.
3. In LiveRunsStrip, replace the redundant 'running · Xm Xs' meta text on live cards (it duplicates the LivePill's elapsed) with 'started relTime(r.startedAt)' so the meta line adds new information rather than repeating the pill.

**First-run Checklist** — Orange-accented card above the hero, shown until all 4 onboarding steps are complete or dismissed; collapses entirely when done; steps render num badge, label, tip text, and CTA link.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The checklist appears above the hero so on every subsequent visit (bridge connected, recipes running, approvals pending) it still occupies prime real estate above the headline. Once step 1 is done it competes with the far-more-urgent NeedsAttentionBand below the hero.
  - *Fix:* Move the checklist below the QuiltHero and above the NeedsAttentionBand. The hero already handles the 'what needs you now' scan; the checklist is a setup guide, not an alert. Alternatively, collapse it to a single 'Setup incomplete — 2 of 4 steps done →' inline chip above the hero and expand on click.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Completed steps render with opacity: 0.65 and line-through text but still show their doneHint tip. Three done steps with visible tip text inflate the card height significantly and bury the single 'next' step the user actually needs to see.
  - *Fix:* Collapse done steps to show only the check mark and label (hide doneHint). Expand doneHint on click/hover if useful at all. This cuts the card height by ~50% for users who have done 3 of 4 steps.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Get started · N of 4 done' h2 uses .first-run-title (--fs-m, font-weight 600) but the Dismiss button is a .btn.sm.ghost aligned baseline — on narrow viewports the flex-wrap: wrap causes Dismiss to drop to a second line, orphaned right-aligned under the heading.
  - *Fix:* Switch .first-run-heading to align-items: center (not baseline) and ensure the Dismiss button has a min-width so it never wraps. A flex-shrink: 0 on the button is sufficient.

**QuiltHero (greeting + headline + summary + stats meta line + FeaturedRecipeAside)** — Two-column card: left = greeting eyebrow, animated h1 headline, summary paragraph, stats meta-line (uptime · model · IDE); right = FeaturedRecipeAside state-aware slot (running / needs-retry / top / empty). 220px min-height, quilt-pattern SVG background fading in from right.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .quilt-title .accent class applies font-family: var(--font-serif) italic in a utility context (headline copy like 'all clear.' and 'Nothing needs you right now.'). The serif italic signals warmth but at clamp(21px, 2.4vw, 30px) bold weight the font-switch creates a visual jar next to the --font-sans bold numerals — especially when both a .num span and .accent span appear in the same phrase.
  - *Fix:* Remove the serif font-family override from .quilt-title .accent; keep color: var(--orange) and font-style: italic only. The italicised sans is warmer than plain-bold and avoids the mid-sentence font switch.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The FeaturedRecipeAside empty state shows 'Start here' / 'N recipes installed' / 'Run one →' with inline style color: var(--info) for the link, bypassing the shared token. The 'Run one →' link also deep-links to /recipes, but there is no recipe-name context, so it just opens the list — same destination as the 'View all' button in the kanban 40px below.
  - *Fix:* Replace the inline color with a CSS class. Change the 'Run one →' CTA to link to /recipes?action=run-first (or surface the most-recently-installed recipe name and link to its edit page) so it is meaningfully different from the kanban's 'View all' button.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The .quilt-stats meta line (uptime · primary · IDE) renders at 12px with --ink-2 color and font-mono bold values. On the paper (light) theme the --ink-2 token is already light enough that the meta line disappears against the quilt gradient's white wash. There is no aria-label on the stats list; screen readers encounter anonymous bold + text nodes.
  - *Fix:* Wrap .quilt-stats in a <dl> (or a nav with aria-label='Bridge status') and raise the font-size to 12.5px. Add a small contrast boost in the paper theme only: .quilt-stats { color: var(--ink-1); } under [data-theme='paper'] .quilt-stats.

**NeedsAttentionBand** — Full-width card below the hero; three states: 'all clear' (green ring + live-dot + sub-text), 'bridge offline' (red, link to /connections), and actionable (warn/err band with attention chips linking to /approvals, /runs?halt=1, /runs). Severity tints the band and left-border.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'all clear' state renders the .pw-live-dot between 'All clear' and the sub-text — three distinct visual elements (ring icon, bold text, pulsing dot) across a single sentence feels over-engineered for a zero-action state. The live-dot pulse in particular draws the eye toward a non-clickable indicator when there is nothing to act on.
  - *Fix:* In the all-clear state, remove the .pw-live-dot (the green ring icon already communicates health). Simplify to: ring icon + 'All clear — no approvals, halts, or failures.' as a single span. Save the live-dot for states where something is actively happening.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The attention-band-label 'Needs attention' is --ink-3 at --fs-xs. When a warn or err chip is present, the band left-border is already orange or red, giving the severity signal. The label itself adds no actionable information and partially duplicates the chip labels.
  - *Fix:* Replace the static 'Needs attention' label with the highest-severity item's count as a compact badge, e.g. '3 items' or remove the label entirely and let the chips speak. Alternatively, promote the label to --ink-2 so it is readable as a prefix when the label copy is changed to a time reference like 'since last check ·'.

**LiveRunsStrip** — Horizontal scroll row of up to 5 cards for in-flight or recently-finished runs (last 10 min); auto-hides when empty; each card shows StatusPill or LivePill, mono recipe name, elapsed/reltime, halt reason if present, and a rerun button for finished runs.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The strip renders between NeedsAttentionBand and the Telemetry section header with no heading or label. When two or more cards are visible, new users have no immediate framing for what these cards represent — the only identifiers are the StatusPill tone and the recipe name.
  - *Fix:* Add a single-line section label 'Recent runs' as a visually lightweight eyebrow (using the .pg-section-head-label pattern without the full rule) directly above the strip. This requires adding one element, not a full section head, and costs zero height on mobile.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The .lrc-name class uses font-family: var(--font-mono), which is consistent with recipe identifiers elsewhere, but the recipe name displayed is the human-readable recipeDisplayName (spaces, title-case), not a raw YAML key. Mono font on display names with spaces reads like a code string rather than a recipe title.
  - *Fix:* Switch .lrc-name to font-family: var(--font-sans) with font-weight: 600. The StatusPill and LivePill already provide sufficient technical context; the name can read as a label.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** On the live card (data-live='1') the elapsed time appears twice: once inside the LivePill (e.g. '1m 23s') and again in the .lrc-meta span ('running · 1m 23s'). The data is identical, just formatted the same way via fmtElapsed called from the same Date.now() - r.startedAt.
  - *Fix:* In the isLive branch of .lrc-meta, replace 'running · {elapsed}' with 'started {relTime(r.startedAt)}' so the meta line adds new information (absolute start time) instead of repeating the pill's elapsed count.

**Telemetry section (eyebrow + 4 StatCards)** — Section eyebrow with 'Telemetry' label + Sync button; four StatCards: Runs·24h, Pending approvals, Halts·24h, Tools called today; each has an AnimatedNumber value, foot label, optional live-dot, and optional Sparkline; gated — only shown when recipes.length > 0 || runs.length > 0; SkeletonStatCards shown while bridge status is loading.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The four cards are each wrapped in a <div className='stat-card-wrap'> with inline style animation and animationDelay, but stat-card-wrap has no CSS definition in globals.css. The staggered animation works because the inline style is applied directly, but the wrapper div adds a DOM node with no semantic or layout purpose.
  - *Fix:* Move the animation + animationDelay inline styles directly onto the StatCard root element (or pass them as a prop). Remove the stat-card-wrap wrapper divs. This keeps the stagger effect and reduces DOM depth by 4 nodes.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The Sync button in the Telemetry eyebrow (top-right of the section head) is the only manual refresh affordance on the page. Its label is 'Sync' with a reload icon, but the page already auto-polls every 5 seconds. On first encounter users do not know whether clicking Sync is needed or cosmetic.
  - *Fix:* Add a tooltip (title attribute or aria-describedby) 'Refresh now (auto-updates every 5s)' to the Sync button. Alternatively, render the last-updated timestamp in a small --ink-3 span next to the button: 'Updated just now' so users see the auto-poll is already working.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Pending approvals' StatCard foot renders a conditional pw-live-dot--warn only when pendingCount > 0. When pendingCount is 0 the foot shows 'none pending' as plain --ink-3 text without any status indicator — consistent with the other cards. But the StatCard itself links to /approvals unconditionally. A click on a 0-pending approvals tile navigates to an empty approvals page, which may confuse users.
  - *Fix:* When pendingCount === 0, either remove the href from the StatCard (making it non-interactive) or change the href to null and render the tile without a hover state. Only make the tile a link when there is something actionable at the destination.

**Recipes section eyebrow (pg-section-head label row)** — Full-width rule with 'Recipes' mono-uppercase label and a gradient hr; no actions in this row (per code comment, actions are in the kanban card header below).

- 🟡 **[med/S]** There are two consecutive section dividers: the 'Telemetry' pg-section-head and then the 'Recipes' pg-section-head, separated only by the StatCard grid and the LiveWire strip. The LiveWire strip has no section head of its own and appears visually attached to the Telemetry section. This means the page reads: Telemetry → [stat tiles] → [live wire] → Recipes → [kanban]. The LiveWire strip is ambiguously positioned.
  - *Fix:* Move the LiveWire strip to immediately after the Telemetry stat tiles (where it already sits in the code) but remove it from between the stat tiles and the 'Recipes' section head — the current ordering already achieves this. However, per page.tsx line 1237, LiveWire is actually rendered after the RecipeLeaderboard, well below the Recipes section. The comment says 'demoted below the fold.' Ensure the LiveWire sits adjacent to the Telemetry section where it makes contextual sense, not after the leaderboard where it is visually disconnected.

**RecipesAtAGlance (kanban: Active / Draft / Paused)** — Three-column kanban inside a .card: Active | Draft | Paused columns; each column has a color-coded top border, icon, label, count, + add link; each card has avatar initials, name, role text, date chip, ok/total chip, and a tag chip; Active cards get a ▶ run button; mobile collapses to tab strip; shows at most 6 per column with '+N more' link.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The kanban has its own 'Your Recipes' h2 header row with 'View all' and '+ New' buttons. The page also has a 'Recipes' pg-section-head eyebrow immediately above the kanban card. This means the word 'Recipes' appears twice within 30px — once as the page-level section label (mono uppercase) and once as the card-level h2 title.
  - *Fix:* Remove the 'Recipes' pg-section-head eyebrow entirely and let the kanban card's own 'Your Recipes' h2 serve as the section anchor. If the eyebrow rule-line is needed for page rhythm, add class='pg-section-head-rule' as a standalone divider element without a label.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Each kanban column has a '+' link via .rag3-col-add that routes to /recipes/new?status=draft|paused|active. The query param ?status is not a recognized intake param in the recipe-new flow (recipe new scaffolds from a template, not from a status pre-selection). The link effectively goes to the generic new-recipe page in all three cases.
  - *Fix:* Change the Draft and Paused column '+' links to /recipes/new (plain, no useless ?status param). The Active column '+' link could route to /recipes/new?trigger=cron to hint at scheduling if the recipe-new page supports that param; otherwise, also use /recipes/new.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The rag3-empty 'No recipes here' paragraph uses --ink-3 at --fs-xs with 6px top-padding. It is easily missed inside an empty column — particularly the Draft column, which is typically empty on a fresh install with all recipes active. An empty column with no card and a barely-visible placeholder can look like a loading failure.
  - *Fix:* Replace the plain 'No recipes here' text with a minimal EmptyState chip (the shared primitive) or at minimum a centered div at --ink-2 that adds a secondary prompt: 'No recipes here · Add one →' linking to /recipes/new. Use --fs-s (not --fs-xs) for the empty state text so it reads as intentional.

**RecipeLeaderboard** — Card with 'Top recipes' h2, 1h/24h/7d tab strip, ActionPill 'all →' link; each row has SuccessRing, recipe name link, RunSparkBars, run count, optional halts pill, last-status pill, and ▶ Run button; empty state shows inline text link; rows animate in with staggered fade-up.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The leaderboard shows recipe names as raw canonicalRecipeKey strings (e.g. 'morning-brief', 'github-pr-review') in the .lbrd-recipe-link, not the human-readable recipeDisplayName. The kanban directly above uses recipeDisplayName. This creates a visual inconsistency where the same recipe appears as 'Morning Brief' in the kanban and 'morning-brief' in the leaderboard, 40px apart on the same page.
  - *Fix:* Import recipeDisplayName and apply it in the leaderboard row: replace <span>{a.name}</span> with <span>{recipeDisplayName(a.name)}</span>. The existing title attribute already uses a.name for hover context.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** The leaderboard is gated only on agg.length > 0 (empty state shown, else list). There is no loading skeleton. On first load the component flashes from zero-height to the full list when runs data arrives, which creates a layout shift below the kanban.
  - *Fix:* Add a loading prop or read from a shared loading state; when runs is an empty array AND the parent fetch has not yet completed, render a SkeletonList (the shared primitive) with 4 rows instead of an empty div. This matches the SkeletonStatCard pattern used in the telemetry section.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .lbrd-status-pill renders the raw status string ('done', 'error', 'running', 'interrupted') in a colored pill. 'done' as a status label is technically correct but reads awkwardly next to 'running' and 'error' — users expect 'done' to say 'ok' or 'success'. The statusTone function already maps done→ok, but the displayed label is still the raw status string.
  - *Fix:* Add a statusLabel helper alongside statusTone: map 'done'→'ok', 'success'→'ok', 'interrupted'→'halted', keep others as-is. Use statusLabel for the pill text and relTime for the existing title attribute.

**LiveWire heartbeat strip** — Single-row status bar after RecipeLeaderboard: colored dot + text summary ('N running · recipe-names · last finished Xm ago' / 'Quiet · last run recipe-name Xm ago' / 'Bridge offline · check connections →' / 'Idle · run a recipe to begin →'); three dot states: green pulse, amber idle-pulse, muted red static.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The LiveWire is positioned after the RecipeLeaderboard (page.tsx line 1237), which places it at the very bottom of the page content. This contradicts its stated purpose ('constant pulse' / 'always-on heartbeat') — a user who has scrolled down to see the leaderboard will miss the heartbeat on initial page load without scrolling. The QuiltHero summary paragraph already conveys the 'N runs clean in 24h' message.
  - *Fix:* Move the LiveWire immediately above the Telemetry section head (between NeedsAttentionBand and the 'Telemetry' eyebrow). In that position it functions as the transition between the 'attention' zone and the 'numbers' zone, and it is visible without scrolling on any screen size.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** In the 'quiet' state the LiveWire renders the recipe name as a link styled with .live-wire-link inside a run of --ink-3 text: 'Quiet · last run [recipe-name] Xm ago'. The recipe-name link color (var(--accent)) contrasts with the surrounding --ink-3 grey, but there is no visual affordance (no underline by default; underline only on hover) making it non-discoverable as a link on first read.
  - *Fix:* Add text-decoration: underline dotted to .live-wire-link in the quiet/idle state (separate from the hover style), or replace with a full-width clickable treatment consistent with other low-prominence links in the system.


### Inbox  `/inbox`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace window.confirm() for Archive and Delete with the shared Dialog primitive — these destructive actions deserve a styled, cancellable confirmation rather than a browser-native dialog that breaks visual coherence (Reader pane actions)
2. Fix the inbox-item list accessibility: change aria-pressed to aria-selected, wrap items in a role='listbox' or semantic ul/li structure, so screen readers announce selection and item count correctly (Sidebar list)
3. Eliminate the InboxDeliveryCard layout-shift flash (dismissed state seeded asynchronously in useEffect) and refactor its all-inline styles to use PatchCard/GlassCard primitives + design tokens, removing the only component on this page that doesn't use the shared component system (InboxDeliveryCard)

**Header** — h1 editorial serif with accent tagline, editorial-sub path breadcrumb, RelationStrip cross-links, inline pill counts, and a bare icon+text Refresh button — all stacked without visual grouping

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The h1 tagline 'what your agents wrote you.' is decorative copy that buries the actual signal (unseen count, total count) below it; on first glance the eye lands on the tagline before seeing that there are N new messages
  - *Fix:* Move the unseen/total count pills directly into the page-head-title-row next to the h1 (before the HintCard.Toggle), and demote the accent tagline to the editorial-sub line or remove it — the RelationStrip already gives context
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Refresh button uses a custom inbox-refresh-btn class with an icon + text but no visible border or background, making it look like a low-contrast label rather than an interactive control; no aria-label on the button itself (only title='Refresh')
  - *Fix:* Apply .btn.sm.ghost to inbox-refresh-btn for consistent hit-target, hover ring, and border; add aria-label='Refresh inbox' to complement the title attr
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'unread' count pill appears both in the page-head-actions AND again in the sidebar header (inbox-head-pill vs inbox-sidebar-new-pill) — same information rendered twice 50px apart
  - *Fix:* Keep the pill only in the sidebar header where it is adjacent to the list it describes; remove from page-head-actions

**InboxDeliveryCard (discovery banner)** — Full-card variant uses inline gridTemplateColumns layout with all-inline styles; sits between the HintCard and the error banner, above the two-pane layout, visible on every page load until dismissed

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The card uses entirely inline styles (gridTemplateColumns, padding, border, background, fontWeight, all hand-coded color-mix values) instead of the shared GlassCard/PatchCard primitives and design tokens, making it inconsistent with every other banner/card on the dashboard
  - *Fix:* Refactor InboxDeliveryCard to use a PatchCard or a .hint-card wrapper class with CSS variables (--accent-tint, --r-3, --fs-s) rather than inline style props; move the layout to a scoped CSS class in globals.css under the inbox/* namespace
- 🔴 **[high/S]** The dismiss button (✕) has only 4px vertical padding and color: var(--ink-3) — at typical --fs-s sizes this produces a touch target well under 44px and near-invisible contrast against the accent-tinted background
  - *Fix:* Increase dismiss button padding to at least 8px, set minimum width/height to 32px, and use --ink-1 or --ink-0 for the icon color so it passes WCAG AA against the surface
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The card always re-renders on every inbox page visit even after being dismissed — the dismissed state is seeded asynchronously in a useEffect, causing a layout-shift flash where the card appears then vanishes on each load
  - *Fix:* Initialize useState with readDismissed() directly (it guards typeof window already) or use a null initial state + suppress render until mounted, eliminating the flash

**Filter bar (search + category chips)** — Search input with / hotkey hint and four category chip buttons (All / Morning Briefs / Recipe Outputs / Agent Reports) rendered inside the left sidebar pane only when sidebarOpen is true

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Category chip buttons use custom inbox-cat-btn with data-active attribute for active state, rather than the existing cluster tab nav primitives (ActivityTabs pattern with aria-selected); this duplicates styling logic already solved elsewhere
  - *Fix:* Replace the .inbox-cat-chips / .inbox-cat-btn pattern with the shared tab-chip pattern (same className used in ActivityTabs/AnalyticsTabs) which already handles aria-selected, focus ring, and active indicator via CSS [data-active] — the JSX surface stays identical, only the class names change
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The recipe filter banner (inbox-recipe-filter) that appears when ?recipe= is set uses a raw code element for the recipe name, which looks technical and unstyled — no visual affordance that this is a filter in effect
  - *Fix:* Replace the bare code element with a RecipeChip (already imported) in its default pill variant, and apply the same .alert-warn background the error banner uses so the filter-active state is visually distinct from normal content

**Sidebar list (inbox-list-pane)** — Gmail-style message rows: SenderAvatar circle with initial + title row (bold title + relative time) + 2-line preview snippet; unread dot on right edge; collapse/expand chevron in sidebar header

- 🔴 **[high/M]** The inbox-item button uses aria-pressed for selection state, but aria-pressed semantics describe a toggle (on/off), not single-selection from a list — screen readers announce 'button, pressed' for the active item but give no sense that other items exist or that this is a list of messages
  - *Fix:* Wrap the item list in a ul with role='listbox' or role='list', change each inbox-item to an li > button (or role='option' with aria-selected) so VoiceOver/NVDA announce 'list, N items' and 'selected' vs 'unselected' correctly
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The collapse button uses ◀ (Unicode black left-pointing triangle) as its visual indicator — this is a glyph-based arrow with no fallback rendering guarantee and no consistent weight/size versus the SVG icons used everywhere else on the page
  - *Fix:* Replace the ◀ glyph with a ChevronLeft SVG matching the 1.8px stroke weight of RecipeIcon and the other inline SVGs; keeps visual language consistent
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The inbox-list-empty 'No items match' text is a bare div with no icon, no suggestion, and no way to clear the filter — users who type in search or switch a category chip and get zero results have no escape hatch in the sidebar
  - *Fix:* Add a small EmptyState-lite inside inbox-list-scroll for the zero-results case: icon + 'No messages match' + a Clear filters button that resets both search and activeFilter — consistent with the full-page EmptyState pattern

**Reader pane header (sender row + subject)** — h2 subject line, then a sender row with SenderAvatar + provenance chips (RecipeChip/RunChip) + absolute-timestamp date + a ✕ close button top-right

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The close button uses the Unicode ✕ character (inbox-reader-close-desktop class) instead of an SVG — inconsistent with every other icon on the page (all SVG at 1.8–2.2px stroke) and the hit-target is uncontrolled
  - *Fix:* Replace ✕ with a 16×16 X SVG icon using the same stroke style as the mobile back-arrow SVG; wrap in a .btn.ghost.icon class or apply explicit padding:8px to guarantee 32px+ tap target
- ⚪ **[low/S]** When provenance frontmatter is absent, the sender row shows only the avatar + date with no label — the inbox-sender-date div renders a raw toLocaleString() timestamp (e.g. '6/25/2026, 7:03:14 AM') with seconds precision, which is noisier than the relative time shown in the list
  - *Fix:* Add a time element with a dateTime attribute and display only date + hour:minute (drop seconds); optionally pair with the RelativeTime component already imported to show '3h ago' next to the absolute date for context

**Message body (reader content)** — Lazy-loaded MessageMarkdown renders agent-output markdown via react-markdown + rehypeSanitize; h2 headings get H2WithCopy buttons; custom CSS classes inbox-md-* control typography

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The MessageMarkdown loading fallback is div aria-busy='true' with no visible content — while the JS chunk loads, the reader pane shows an empty div with no skeleton or spinner, giving the appearance of a hang rather than a lazy load
  - *Fix:* Change the dynamic() loading fallback to <Spinner size={18} /> (already defined in the file) or a skeleton div matching the content area height, consistent with the SkeletonList used for the list pane
- ⚪ **[low/S]** H2WithCopy's Copy button uses the text 'Copy' / 'Copied ✓' — the ✓ is a Unicode character that may render differently across OS; the button has no visible border or background in its resting state, making it hard to discover unless the user knows to look
  - *Fix:* Give copy-section-btn a .btn.xs.ghost baseline style (border visible on hover) and replace the ✓ glyph with a small checkmark SVG or the system ✓ wrapped in aria-hidden, matching the rest of the design system's interactive affordances

**Reader pane actions (bottom action bar)** — Four buttons in a row: 'Replay recipe' (primary), 'View trace' (ghost link), 'Archive' (ghost muted), 'Delete permanently' (ghost danger) — rendered inside an IIFE at the bottom of the reader body

- 🔴 **[high/M]** 'Delete permanently' uses window.confirm() for destructive confirmation — a native browser dialog that is visually jarring, breaks the design language, and cannot be styled; the existing Dialog primitive is available
  - *Fix:* Replace window.confirm() calls for both Archive and Delete with the shared Dialog component (already in the patchwork primitives), using dialog-level cancel/confirm buttons with appropriate variant styling (danger for delete, default for archive)
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The four actions render in a flat horizontal row with no visual grouping between the primary action ('Replay recipe') and the destructive actions ('Archive', 'Delete permanently') — on narrow viewports they wrap unpredictably
  - *Fix:* Add a flex gap or a visual divider (border-left or margin-left:auto on the Archive button) to group primary/secondary vs destructive actions; on mobile, stack them vertically or move destructive actions behind a '…' overflow menu
- ⚪ **[low/S]** 'View trace' is a Link rendered as .btn.sm.ghost but navigates away from the inbox entirely, losing the current reading context with no warning; the label is ambiguous ('trace' is jargon)
  - *Fix:* Rename to 'View run trace' for clarity; optionally open in a new tab (target='_blank' + rel='noopener') so the message context is preserved — consistent with how cross-entity navigation works on other detail pages

**Loading state (full-page)** — SkeletonList rows={5} columns={2} renders when loading && items.length === 0; no label or context

- 🟡 **[med/M]** SkeletonList with columns=2 does not match the two-pane inbox layout (sidebar list + reader pane) — the skeleton implies a simple table, not the split-panel the user will see after load
  - *Fix:* Replace with a custom skeleton that mirrors the actual two-pane structure: a narrow left column of ~4 inbox-item-shaped skeletons (avatar circle + two text lines) and a wider right empty panel, matching what loads in

**Empty state (no inbox items)** — EmptyState with envelope icon + title + description paragraph + embedded InboxDeliveryCard variant='empty' + 'Run a recipe' CTA link

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The InboxDeliveryCard variant='empty' is embedded inside the EmptyState description prop, creating a nested interactive element (a Link) inside what is structurally descriptive text — the CTA hierarchy becomes unclear (is the primary action 'Run a recipe' or 'Set up delivery'?)
  - *Fix:* Move the InboxDeliveryCard empty variant below the EmptyState component, as a sibling, rather than inside its description prop; this separates the primary CTA (run a recipe) from the secondary discovery CTA (set up delivery)
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The empty state icon is the same envelope SVG used as the page favicon, sidebar collapse button icon, and reader-pane empty-select state — three identical icons at different sizes with no differentiation
  - *Fix:* Use a distinct illustration or a slightly different icon variant (e.g. open envelope or inbox-tray) for the full empty state to create visual hierarchy; reserve the closed-envelope for the sidebar and reader placeholder

**Error state** — ErrorState component used for list load failure and for per-message load failure; inline alert-err banner shown when poll fails but stale items remain

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The inline stale-refresh error uses a raw div.alert-err with no retry affordance — the user sees 'Refresh failed — <error>' with no button to retry immediately
  - *Fix:* Add an inline Retry button inside the .alert-err div (matching the ErrorState onRetry pattern already used below) so users can trigger a re-fetch without waiting for the next 30s poll tick

**Reader pane empty/placeholder (no message selected)** — When items exist but nothing is selected: centered envelope SVG + 'Select a message to read it' + count text; auto-select fires on first load so this is briefly visible

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The placeholder uses a bare p.inbox-reader-empty-title for the headline with no shared primitive (EmptyState) — inconsistent with the full-page empty state that uses EmptyState; the keyboard shortcut to open first item (if any) is not surfaced
  - *Fix:* Wrap in a minimal EmptyState usage (icon + title, no action) to stay consistent with the full-page variant; or at minimum apply the same .empty-state-title class used there so typography matches


### Recipes list  `/recipes`

**Top 3:**
1. Remove role='link' from <tr> elements in the recipe table — invalid ARIA causes screen readers to announce each row as a link then re-announce the inner anchor, and the accessible path should be the recipe-name-link anchor widened to fill the cell (high impact, zero functional regression).
2. Replace window.confirm() for Archive and Delete in RecipeDetailPanel with the shared Dialog component — destructive actions on recipe files need branded, testable confirmation dialogs consistent with the RunModal already on the same page.
3. Replace the hand-rolled status pill in RecipeHubCard with the shared StatusPill primitive and extract all inline layout styles to a CSS class using design tokens — the card is the hub entry point for every recipe and currently diverges completely from the token system.

**Page header** — Two-line header: editorial h1 with decorative serif tagline 'YAML, declarative, yours.' + subtitle showing path + count, plus RelationStrip cross-links and a page-head-actions block with duplicate '+ Add recipe' alongside '↻ Reload'.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Decorative tagline buries the count signal. 'Recipes — YAML, declarative, yours.' followed by a separate subtitle line means the user has to read two lines to find the installed count.
  - *Fix:* Move 'N installed' into the h1 or make it the primary subtitle. Demote or remove the tagline. Example: h1 = 'Recipes', subtitle = '~/.patchwork/recipes · 12 installed'. The editorial tagline can live in an onboarding HintCard instead.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Duplicate CTA: '+ Add recipe' appears in both page-head-actions and the RelationStrip ('New recipe'). Two buttons for the same action fragment attention and reduce the perceived importance of both.
  - *Fix:* Remove '+ Add recipe' from page-head-actions (keep only '↻ Reload' there). RelationStrip's accent-tone 'New recipe' link is sufficient and follows the established pattern on other pages.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The '↻ Reload' button has no aria-label and uses a raw Unicode arrow that screen readers announce as 'clockwise open circle arrow Reload'.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label='Reload recipes' and replace the Unicode ↻ with an inline SVG refresh icon matching the icon system used elsewhere (e.g. the RunSparkBars icon style).

**Toolbar / filter bar** — Search input (with / shortcut hint in placeholder and inline clear button) plus inline enabled/paused count toggle-buttons separated by aria-hidden dots. Connector filter badge renders below the toolbar when ?connector= is active.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The search icon ⌕ is a rare Unicode glyph (U+2315) that may not render in all system fonts, falling back to a box character. Also the placeholder text 'Search recipes by name or description… ( / )' is long and truncates on narrow viewports, hiding the shortcut hint.
  - *Fix:* Replace ⌕ with a standard SVG magnifier icon (12×12, same style as TriggerIcon). Move the '/' shortcut hint into an aria-label or a right-aligned kbd element outside the placeholder text.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The connector filter active badge (recipes-connector-badge) sits below the toolbar but above the table, breaking the visual grouping. It looks like a floating error or status message rather than an active filter.
  - *Fix:* Integrate the connector filter badge inline in the toolbar row as a dismissible chip alongside the enabled/paused toggles, using the same recipes-status-btn pattern. This collapses the vertical space between toolbar and table and signals 'these are the active filters'.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The statusFilter toggle buttons (recipes-status-btn) have aria-pressed but no visible pressed/active style described in JSX. If CSS doesn't supply [aria-pressed=true] styles, users get no visual confirmation that the filter is active.
  - *Fix:* Verify CSS includes `[data-filter][aria-pressed='true']` with a distinct background (e.g. color-mix with --accent-cool) and border to match the active state. If missing, add it. Also add a data-active attribute as a CSS hook since aria-pressed is for AT consumers.

**HintCard slot** — A HintCard id='recipes' renders between the toolbar and the error/loading states, occupying vertical space even when collapsed to a toggle.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** HintCard.Toggle renders unconditionally, so a fresh user sees a toggle icon in the middle of the page flow with no context about what it expands. On pages with 10+ recipes this breaks the visual scan path from toolbar straight to the table.
  - *Fix:* Move HintCard.Toggle into the page-head-title-row (it's already there in the JSX — the standalone HintCard below the toolbar is the redundant copy). Remove the second HintCard render or conditionally show it only when recipes.length === 0.

**Error / loading states** — Three branches: SkeletonList on initial load, ErrorState (uses shared primitive) when no recipes and error present, inline alert-err div when error occurs during a refresh with existing data.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stale-data error branch renders a raw `<div className='alert-err'>Refresh failed — {err}</div>` instead of using the shared ErrorState or Toast primitive, inconsistent with the rest of the error handling.
  - *Fix:* Replace the alert-err div with toast.error() (already wired and imported) or use ErrorState in its compact/inline variant. This matches the pattern used for run failures on the same page and clears automatically.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** SkeletonList rows=4 columns=3 doesn't match the 7-column recipe table (health ring + name + trigger + runs spark + avg + last + actions). The skeleton columns mismatch the real layout, causing a jarring reflow on load completion.
  - *Fix:* Use SkeletonList rows=4 columns=7 or build a purpose-specific skeleton row matching the table column count. Alternatively add a CSS min-height to the .recipes-table-card so the skeleton and table occupy identical vertical space.

**Empty state (no recipes or no filter match)** — Global EmptyState component used when zero recipes installed; in-table inline empty block (raw divs with inline styles) used when filters produce zero results from a non-empty list.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The filtered-empty state inside the <td colSpan=7> uses raw inline styles (fontSize, display, flexDirection, gap, animation, opacity) instead of the shared EmptyState primitive, creating a visual inconsistency between the 'no recipes at all' and 'no match' states.
  - *Fix:* Extract the filtered-empty content into EmptyState with title='No matches' and conditional action buttons for 'Clear search' and 'Show all'. The colSpan td wrapper is still needed but the content should use the primitive.

**Recipe table** — 7-column table (SuccessRing, name+desc+pills, trigger chip+schedule text, RunSparkBars 14-slot, avg duration, last run time, toggle+run button) in a PatchCard with horizontal scroll. Rows are keyboard-navigable with j/k and Enter/Space → router.push to hub.

- 🔴 **[high/M]** Each row has role='link' but is a <tr> element — role=link on a <tr> is not valid ARIA. Screen readers announce the whole row as a link, then encounter an inner <Link> on the recipe name (a genuine anchor), producing duplicate navigation announcements for the same destination.
  - *Fix:* Remove role='link' and tabIndex from the <tr>. Widen the recipe-name-link anchor to cover the full name cell with display:block and ensure it's the primary keyboard focus target. The row's onClick can remain for mouse users but the accessible path should be the anchor, not the tr.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Run' button in the actions cell is disabled when enabled===false, but there is no visual tooltip explaining why it's disabled. A paused recipe shows the button grayed out with no affordance.
  - *Fix:* Add title='Enable recipe to run manually' to the disabled Run button so hovering surfaces the reason. Optionally render the toggle and Run button as a single compound control group with a shared aria-describedby.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Runs column (RunSparkBars) has column header 'Runs' but its tooltip/legend is not accessible — the colored bars carry success/error/halt meaning that is not exposed via aria-label or a legend. The successPct ring (SuccessRing) also has no accessible label.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label to the RunSparkBars wrapper: 'Last 14 runs — N% success'. Pass successPct into SuccessRing's aria-label: e.g. 'Success rate: 82%'. Both values are already computed (pct/successPct) so the wiring is minimal.

**Recipe detail panel (RecipeDetailPanel)** — PatchCard slide-in panel with header (name, LivePill, Run + Diagnose buttons, close), optional RecipeRunInline status strip, Recipe YAML section (CodeBlock with lazy fetch + fallback), Recent runs list (up to 5 RunChip/StatusPill rows), and footer (Archive + Delete permanently).

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The rdp-header mixes semantic roles: rdp-title is a span (not a heading), the close button is an × character, and the Diagnose Link renders next to the primary Run button making both feel equal weight. There is no landmark or focus management when the panel opens.
  - *Fix:* Change rdp-title span to an h2 (or use aria-labelledby on the PatchCard). Set focus to the panel's h2 or first interactive element on open (useEffect + ref). Visually differentiate Diagnose as secondary by giving it ghost style only (it already has className='btn sm ghost' but appears visually equal to Run due to proximity).
- 🔴 **[high/M]** The Archive and Delete buttons in rdp-footer rely solely on browser window.confirm() for destructive action confirmation — not a Dialog primitive, so it can't be styled or tested consistently. Delete permanently is especially dangerous with no secondary confirmation step.
  - *Fix:* Wire Archive and Delete to the shared Dialog component (already imported on the page). This matches the RunModal pattern already used for Run, and allows the dialog to be branded consistently and testable.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Recipe YAML' section label (rdp-section-label) and 'Recent runs' section label are plain divs, not headings, so the panel has no heading hierarchy below the title for screen readers to jump between sections.
  - *Fix:* Change rdp-section-label divs to h3 elements (font-size and style already controlled by the class, so visual impact is zero). This gives AT users a navigation landmark inside the panel.

**RecipeHubCard component** — Card component (used outside /recipes or in hub view) with inline styles for all layout — background, border, borderRadius, padding, gap, minHeight, opacity, transition. Wraps a Link for the name and uses raw span for the status pill rather than the shared StatusPill primitive.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** RecipeHubCard builds its own status pill inline (background/color/border via color-mix, padding, borderRadius 999) instead of using the shared StatusPill component. This diverges from the design token contract and means future pill changes won't apply here.
  - *Fix:* Replace the custom span status pill with <StatusPill tone={tone}>{statusLabel(status)}</StatusPill> where tone maps from statusColor logic using the semantic token names (ok/err/warn/muted). Remove the STATUS_COLOR record and statusColor() helper — StatusPill already encapsulates this.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** All layout is inline style rather than a CSS class, making the card impossible to override via the theme or to inspect consistently in devtools. The minHeight:140 is magic number not tied to a spacing token.
  - *Fix:* Extract layout to a recipe-hub-card CSS class (using --s-* tokens for padding/gap, --r-l for borderRadius). Keep only data-driven values (opacity for enabled state) as inline styles. minHeight should use a spacing token or be replaced by min-content with a padding floor.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The run meta line renders 'N runs · last Xm ago' in --ink-3 (faintest text) at --fs-s. On the dark theme this is likely below 4.5:1 contrast against --bg-1. It is also the only data line in the card with no visual affordance distinguishing it from the disabled-state opacity.
  - *Fix:* Bump the run meta color to --ink-2 for normal state. Reserve --ink-3 only for disabled/secondary labels. Verify contrast ratio in both light and dark themes.

**ConnectorHealthPanel section** — ConnectorHealthPanel renders below the table, conditionally shown only when recipes.length > 0, using a heuristic keyword scan to detect connector usage.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The ConnectorHealthPanel appears unconditionally below the recipe table regardless of whether the panel relates to the current filter view. If the user has filtered to 'paused' recipes, the connector panel still reflects all installed recipes.
  - *Fix:* Pass filteredRecipes (not all recipes) to detectConnectors so the connector panel reflects only the visible subset. Low effort since detectConnectors already accepts Recipe[].

**Mobile / responsive** — MobileRunBar fixed bar appears when a recipe is selected, with close × and Run button. The table is horizontally scrollable. RecipeDetailPanel is visible alongside the table in has-detail grid layout.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The MobileRunBar close button is an × character (recipes-mobile-run-bar-close class) with no visible label text, only an aria-label. On mobile the tap target size should be at least 44×44px — the current styling is unknown from JSX alone, but a bare button with × is typically under 32px.
  - *Fix:* Ensure recipes-mobile-run-bar-close in CSS has min-height:44px and min-width:44px, or use an SVG icon with explicit 44px hit area via padding. Verify the z-index layering comment (z:27 vs nav z:28) is enforced in CSS.

**Run modal (RunModal)** — Dialog wrapper with recipe name in h2 (as <code>), confirm note for no-vars case, var input fields for vars, Cancel + 'Run recipe' (warn-tone) submit. Session-scoped first-run confirmation gate.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Run recipe' submit button uses className='btn warn' (yellow/orange tone), which typically signals caution or warning state. Executing a recipe is the primary positive action and should use 'btn primary' or 'btn accent'. The warn tone makes the CTA look like a destructive action alongside the 'Cancel' ghost button.
  - *Fix:* Change the submit button to className='btn primary' (or 'btn accent' to match the accent-orange brand color used elsewhere). Reserve warn tone for genuinely cautionary or irreversible confirmations.


### Recipe detail hub  `/recipes/[name]`

**Top 3:**
1. Add skeleton loading states to the Summary card, Recent runs card, and layout Header — currently all three flash empty/placeholder content before data arrives, creating a confusing first impression on every navigation.
2. Surface the top halt-category fix hint inline (not only in a tooltip) — operators on touch devices and power users scanning quickly cannot see the actionable fix for the most common failure without hovering each badge.
3. Replace the two `window.confirm()` calls (Disable and Uninstall) with the imported Dialog component — native browser dialogs are unthemeable, blocked in some embedded contexts, and break the design system's interaction contract for destructive actions.

**Header / Hero (layout.tsx)** — Breadcrumb + mono H1 + StatusPill + description + RelationStrip + TabBar stacked vertically with 8–16px gaps; no loading skeleton while recipes list resolves.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** No loading state in the header: H1 renders the raw URL segment before `recipe` resolves, StatusPill shows a placeholder tone but no visual affordance, and description is absent — the header looks broken for ~200–500ms on every navigation.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the H1, StatusPill, and description in a conditional: when `!recipesLoaded`, render a `<SkeletonStatCard />` or two `<Skeleton width='60%' />` lines instead. The Skeleton primitive already exists — use it.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The `recipe-hub-status-pill-enabled` wrapper `<span>` on line 256 of layout.tsx applies `borderRadius: 999` via inline style but the span wraps the StatusPill which already has its own border-radius. The outer span adds no visual — it's dead markup and the class name suggests a custom enabled-state override that isn't defined anywhere visible.
  - *Fix:* Remove the outer `<span>` wrapper and apply any desired enabled-state ring (e.g. a subtle `box-shadow: 0 0 0 2px var(--ok)`) directly as a prop or className on `<StatusPill>` itself.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** TabBar arrow-key navigation focuses the next tab ref but does not navigate (router.push) on ArrowLeft/Right — only on Enter/Space. ARIA tablist pattern requires that arrow keys both focus AND activate tabs (or the tabpanel must be managed separately with tabIndex on panels). The current mix will confuse screen-reader users who expect tab-switching on arrow.
  - *Fix:* Either call `router.push(TABS[next].href(name))` inside the ArrowLeft/Right branch (auto-follow pattern, simpler) or add `tabpanel` roles + `aria-controls` on each tab and only navigate on Enter (manual activation pattern). Auto-follow is consistent with other dashboard tab navs.

**RelationStrip (layout.tsx)** — Horizontal strip of cross-surface link chips (Runs, Halts, Traces, Inbox, Approvals, connector links) rendered below the description and above the TabBar.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The RelationStrip fires on every tab (Overview, Edit, Plan) because it lives in the shared layout, which is correct. However the strip duplicates the 'Runs' and 'Halts' links that already appear as 'View all runs →' and 'View halts →' inline links in the Overview body cards. Three separate entry points to the same /runs page is redundant noise.
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline 'View all runs →' and 'View halts →' anchor links from the Recent runs and Halts PatchCards (page.tsx lines 771–776 and 843–847). The RelationStrip is the canonical cross-surface nav; the inline links are redundant.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** Connector entries in the strip link to `/connections#${c}` — a hash anchor on a different page. If the connections page doesn't have matching id attributes on each connector row, the hash silently does nothing. There is no visual distinction between these 'connector' chips and the page-nav chips (Runs, Traces, etc.).
  - *Fix:* Give connector chips a distinct visual style (e.g. the ConnectorChip pill already exists with a health dot). Replace the plain RelationStrip item with a `ConnectorChip` rendered inline, or add a `kind: 'connector'` variant to RelationStrip that renders the chip style.

**Action bar (page.tsx hub-action-bar)** — Three buttons — Run now (primary), Enable/Disable (ghost), Edit (ghost link) — rendered above the Summary card when recipe is loaded.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** 'Run now' is disabled when `recipe.enabled === false` but there is no tooltip or visible reason explaining why. A disabled button with no explanation is a dead end for the operator.
  - *Fix:* When the recipe is disabled, change `title='Execute this recipe now'` to `title='Recipe is disabled — enable it first'` and add a visible inline hint below the action bar: a `<span style={{color:'var(--ink-3)',fontSize:'var(--fs-xs)'}}>Enable the recipe to run it manually.</span>`.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Enable/Disable button uses `window.confirm()` for the disable confirmation — a browser-native dialog that is unthemeable, blocks the main thread, and is suppressed in some embedded contexts. The shared `Dialog` primitive already exists.
  - *Fix:* Replace the `window.confirm()` call in `handleToggle` with a small `Dialog` confirmation (already imported on this page). Two sentences: action summary + consequence. Cancel + Confirm buttons.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The action bar has no aria-label on the wrapping div, so screen readers encounter three buttons with no landmark context separating them from the page heading.
  - *Fix:* Add `role='toolbar'` and `aria-label='Recipe actions'` to the `.hub-action-bar` div.

**Summary card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card)** — Five stat cells (Trigger, Schedule, Last run, Success rate, Avg duration) in a CSS auto-fit grid inside a PatchCard; labels use --ink-3/--fs-xs, values use --font-mono.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** While `recipes` is undefined (first fetch), `recipe` is null and every stat cell renders its fallback synchronously (`recipe?.trigger ?? 'manual'`, `scheduleString = '—'`, etc.) instead of a skeleton. The card appears instantly with placeholder dashes, giving no indication that real data is loading.
  - *Fix:* When `recipes === undefined` (not yet loaded), render `<SkeletonStatCard count={5} />` in place of the grid. The SkeletonStatCard primitive exists for exactly this pattern.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Success rate' cell appends `over {runs.length}` in --fs-xs --ink-3. When `runs.length` is small (e.g. 1 or 2), this shows e.g. '100% over 1' which overstates confidence. The sample size is not visually de-emphasised enough from the stat value itself.
  - *Fix:* Add a parenthetical sample indicator only when runs.length >= 5, otherwise show a `title` tooltip: `title='Based on only ${runs.length} run(s) — may not be representative'`. Keep the visible copy clean.

**Recent runs card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card)** — RunChip rows with relative timestamps and duration, divided by --line-1 borders; empty state is a centered icon + inline copy; 'View all runs →' link top-right.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The empty state is an ad-hoc centered div (lines 779–791) with a raw `▷` Unicode character as an icon. The shared `EmptyState` primitive (already imported on this page) handles icon, heading, description, and optional action consistently across the dashboard.
  - *Fix:* Replace the inline empty div with `<EmptyState title='No runs yet' description='Use Run now above to start the first run.' />`. Drop the raw `▷` glyph.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** When `runsResp` is undefined (initial fetch), `recentRuns` is `[]` from the `useMemo` fallback, so the empty state immediately renders 'No runs yet' before data has arrived. An operator with 50 runs sees the empty state flicker for ~200ms.
  - *Fix:* Track loading separately: check `runsResp === undefined` (not yet fetched) and render a `<SkeletonList count={5} />` in that branch, showing the real content or empty state only after `runsResp !== undefined`.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The '→ inbox' link in run rows (line 817) uses a raw arrow character and is only `--fs-xs` with `--accent` color — it is too small and contextless. A user who hasn't internalized the inbox concept has no idea what '→ inbox' means.
  - *Fix:* Replace with `<InboxChip name={r.inboxOutputs[0].filename} recipeName={name} />` (the InboxChip is already imported) so it has consistent chip styling. Or at minimum change the text to 'Inbox output →' for clarity.

**Halts card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card — conditional)** — Shown only when haltSummary.total > 0; renders amber pill-badges per category with hint in `title` tooltip; 'View halts →' link top-right.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The fix hints are buried in `title` tooltips (cursor: help) — invisible on touch/mobile and only discoverable by hovering each badge. On a recipe with repeated auth_failure halts, the operator must hover to learn 'Reconnect from /connections.'
  - *Fix:* Below the badge row, conditionally render the top-1 hint inline (the category with the highest count): a single line in --fs-xs --ink-2 `→ {HALT_CATEGORY_HINT[topCat]}`. The tooltip can stay as supplemental detail for other categories.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The card is entirely absent while `haltSummary` is undefined (fetching). This creates a layout shift: cards below jump up while halt data is loading, then the halt card appears and pushes them down.
  - *Fix:* Always render the card slot; when `haltSummary === undefined` show a one-line `<Skeleton width='80%' />` inside the PatchCard. When `total === 0`, render a subtle '✓ No halts in recent window' line in --ink-3 rather than hiding the card entirely.

**Connectors required card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card — conditional)** — Shown only when requiredConnectors.length > 0; renders ConnectorChip per connector with health dot from connectorHealthMap.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Like the halts card, this card is entirely absent when `requiredConnectors` is empty (recipe uses no connectors). But `requiredConnectors` is derived from `recipe` which may be null during load, so the card flickers in/out as data arrives. No loading state.
  - *Fix:* Render the card only when `recipe !== null`. When `recipe === null`, render a `<Skeleton />` placeholder in this slot. This prevents the layout shift.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** When a connector's `healthy` value is `undefined` (bridge doesn't populate it yet — as noted in the comment on ConnectorStatus.healthy), the ConnectorChip presumably renders an ambiguous neutral dot. The user cannot distinguish 'definitely healthy' from 'status unknown'.
  - *Fix:* Pass an explicit `healthy={connectorHealthMap.has(id) ? connectorHealthMap.get(id) : undefined}` and ensure ConnectorChip renders a distinct 'unknown' state (e.g. a grey dot with `title='Status unknown — bridge has not reported health'`) rather than silently omitting the dot.

**Latest inbox output card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card — conditional)** — Shown only when latestInboxOutput is non-null; single row: InboxChip + relative timestamp + 'View in inbox →' link.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Section header reads 'Latest output → Inbox' — the arrow is ambiguous (is it a link? a direction indicator? a breadcrumb separator?). The `→` in a heading signals navigation or a data-flow direction, but this is a static label.
  - *Fix:* Rename to 'Latest inbox output' (remove the arrow from the heading). The 'View in inbox →' link in the row already handles the navigation affordance.

**Controls card (page.tsx PatchCard hub-card)** — Secondary/destructive actions: Plan, Simulate, Compare versions, Uninstall (right-aligned, err-colored). Primary actions (Run, Enable, Edit) live in the action bar above.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Uninstall' button uses `window.confirm()` (line 562–565) — same native-dialog problem as the disable confirm. The SectionHeader 'Controls' is redundant when the card is immediately below the action bar and contains only four buttons — the label adds no scannability.
  - *Fix:* Replace `window.confirm` in `handleUninstall` with the imported `Dialog` component — a destructive action dialog with explicit 'Delete permanently' CTA and secondary warning copy. Consider removing the 'Controls' SectionHeader since the button labels are self-explanatory at this level.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Plan' and 'Simulate' buttons link to sub-tabs/anchors that already exist in the layout's TabBar (Plan) and in this same page (Simulate section below). The Controls card creates a third navigation path to the same destinations already reachable from the tab bar and the RelationStrip.
  - *Fix:* Remove 'Plan' and 'Simulate' from the Controls card. The tab bar handles Plan; the SimulatePanel is already visible on this page. If 'Simulate' needs a shortcut, add it to the action bar row alongside Run/Enable/Edit at a lower visual weight (ghost btn).

**Doctor panel card (page.tsx + DoctorPanel.tsx)** — PatchCard with SectionHeader 'Doctor', then DoctorPanel: a 'Run diagnosis' button, status badge on result, two sub-sections (static checks, runtime halts) rendered as plain ul lists in --fs-xs mono.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'static checks' and 'runtime halts' sub-section labels are plain div spans with className='mono muted' at --fs-2xs. They are visually lighter than the list content they label, inverting the expected label-then-content hierarchy. On a healthy recipe ('✓ lint + policy clean') they read as floating orphan text.
  - *Fix:* Promote the sub-section labels to a SectionHeader-equivalent (font-weight 600, --ink-2, not --ink-3/muted) or at minimum use --fs-xs (not --fs-2xs). Alternatively use a `<dt>`/`<dd>` definition-list structure to make the label-value relationship semantic.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The error display (line 125–129) is a raw `<div>` with `color: var(--err)` at --fs-xs. This diverges from the shared ErrorState primitive and from the Toast pattern used for run errors elsewhere on this page.
  - *Fix:* Replace the inline error div with `<ErrorState message={error} />` using the shared primitive, or if the error is inline/non-blocking, use the Toast pattern already imported (`toast.error(...)`) so it's consistent with how run and toggle errors are surfaced.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The DoctorPanel runtime halt list renders all halt entries with `color: var(--err)` (line 210) regardless of count. A single auth_failure from weeks ago looks as alarming as 20 recent ones. The hint text (→ fix) shares the line with the category, making already-dense rows harder to scan.
  - *Fix:* Apply color semantically: use --err only for the count > threshold (e.g. > 3), --warn for 1–3, --ok for 0. Break the hint onto a second line with `display: block; color: var(--ink-2); margin-left: 16px` rather than inline on the same line, to visually separate the category from the hint.

**What-If Preview panel card (page.tsx + SimulatePanel.tsx)** — PatchCard with SectionHeader 'What-If Preview', then SimulatePanel: 'Run simulation' button, risk summary, dense risk-component breakdown, step list, side effects, approvals, cost, branches, lint — all rendered as mono text at --fs-xs/--fs-2xs.

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The risk component breakdown (line 111–118, SimulatePanel.tsx) is a single compressed mono string: 'high:N · medium:N · writes:N · connector-writes:N · http:N · unresolved:N'. This is machine-log formatting that requires the operator to parse six token-separated numbers with no visual hierarchy or color coding.
  - *Fix:* Render each component as a labeled badge or a small definition grid (two columns: label | count) with semantic color: --err for high, --warn for medium/writes, --ink-2 for the rest. The Sparkline primitive could visualize write-vs-read ratio at a glance.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The SimulatePanel auto-runs on every page view (`autoSimulate = useSearchParams().get('simulate') !== '0'`), but there is no loading skeleton — the panel shows only the 'Run simulation' button (disabled, labeled 'Simulating…') during the fetch. If the simulation takes 2–3 seconds, the large card is mostly empty white space with a disabled button.
  - *Fix:* When `busy === true`, render a `<SkeletonList count={6} />` inside the panel body below the button row to fill the expected content area and reduce perceived wait time.
