  - *Fix:* Add a small section label ('Risk' / 'Pattern') above each chip group (styled as --ink-3, --fs-xs, uppercase) or use a horizontal rule separator between the two groups so users can distinguish policy signals from personal-history signals
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Edit & approve' secondary action button copies a CLI snippet to clipboard but its label gives no indication it is a copy action — users may expect it to open an edit flow inline. The '› Open in terminal' button is similarly ambiguous (opens nothing, just copies)
  - *Fix:* Change labels to 'Copy: edit & approve' and 'Copy CLI command' (or prepend a clipboard icon); add aria-label='Copy patchwork approve --edit command' so screen readers get the full intent
- 🟡 **[med/M]** window.confirm and window.prompt are used for high-risk approve/reject confirmation and rejection-reason collection — these block the main thread, are unstyleable, and cannot be keyboard-navigated on all platforms; on mobile they may be silently suppressed
  - *Fix:* Replace both with the shared Dialog component (already imported in the codebase) for the confirmation gate and a Dialog with a textarea for rejection reason input
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Expired approval cards stay in the list with a red 'Expired' pill and both Approve/Reject buttons disabled, but there is no action to dismiss/clear them and no explanation of why they persist
  - *Fix:* Add a small 'Dismiss' ghost button on expired cards (calling removeWithFade) and update the aria description to note 'This request timed out — the agent has moved on'

**Batch action bar (.approval-batch-bar)** — Appears at bottom of list when items are selected; shows count, Approve selected, Reject selected; uses role='toolbar'; disappears when count=0

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The batch bar appears at the bottom of the card list, which may be below the viewport fold when 5+ cards are showing — users who select via the top checkbox have to scroll down to see the action buttons
  - *Fix:* Make the batch bar position:sticky at the bottom of the viewport (bottom: 0, z-index above cards) so it remains visible regardless of scroll position; this is the standard pattern for bulk-action toolbars
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Batch action buttons have no aria-label beyond button text ('Approve selected (N)') — screen readers won't know what is being approved
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label='Approve N selected tool calls' and aria-label='Reject N selected tool calls' dynamically based on selectedCount

**Pattern suggestions card (.apq-suggestions-card)** — Card with emoji H2 heading, description paragraph, list of tool names with approved count and copy/dismiss buttons, Clear all patterns footer; appears below queue when patterns >= 3 approvals with no rejections

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The card H2 uses a 💡 emoji directly in JSX which violates the project style guide (no emojis unless explicitly requested) and may render inconsistently across platforms
  - *Fix:* Replace 💡 with an SVG icon (e.g. a lightbulb from the existing icon set) or a simple text glyph; add aria-hidden='true' to any decorative icon
- ⚪ **[low/M]** The suggestion card appears below the queue regardless of scroll position — when the queue is long, users never discover the suggestions. When the queue is empty, the EmptyState renders above the suggestion card with nothing in between, making the suggestions feel orphaned
  - *Fix:* When the queue is empty (hasLoaded && filtered.length === 0), render the suggestion card inside or immediately below the EmptyState block; when the queue has items, consider a collapsible panel or a link in the kbd-hint-row instead of a full card below the fold
- ⚪ **[low/S]** 'Copy allow rule' copies raw JSON snippet with no context on where to paste it — a user who just landed on this page has no clear path to act on the suggestion
  - *Fix:* Add a footer link 'Paste into /settings#approvals →' next to 'Clear all patterns' so the copy action has an obvious next step

**Loading state** — Suspense boundary at page level delegates to loading.tsx which renders RouteLoading; within the loaded page, SkeletonList rows=3 columns=3 is shown while hasLoaded is false

- ⚪ **[low/M]** SkeletonList with rows=3 columns=3 renders a generic grid skeleton that doesn't match the tall vertical ApprovalCard layout — the skeleton shape gives no preview of the actual content structure, increasing perceived layout shift when cards appear
  - *Fix:* Replace SkeletonList with a custom skeleton that approximates an ApprovalCard: a full-width block with a short header row skeleton, a code block rectangle, and two button outlines — or use the existing Skeleton primitive with explicit heights matching .apc card dimensions

**Empty state (all caught up)** — EmptyState primitive used correctly with icon, title 'All caught up!', contextual description, optional 'Clear filter' action button; correctly not rendered until hasLoaded is true

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The EmptyState icon is a raw <span> with a checkmark character (✓) styled via .apq-ok-icon class — the icon color and size are CSS-dependent and may not match the EmptyState icon styling used elsewhere in the dashboard (which typically uses SVG at 32px in --ok color)
  - *Fix:* Replace the span/character with an inline SVG checkmark at 32px using color var(--ok), matching the icon style in ErrorState and other EmptyState usages
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The empty state description when riskFilter='all' is a long two-sentence explanation: 'No pending approvals — your recipes are running smoothly. Tool calls are handled by policy or have already been decided.' The second sentence adds noise
  - *Fix:* Trim to 'No pending approvals. Tool calls are handled by policy.' — one concise sentence, signal first


### Approval detail  `/approvals/[callId]`

**Top 3:**
1. Add skeleton loading states (SkeletonList/Skeleton for h1 and cards) — the page currently shows 'Unknown' in h1 and blank card area for the entire first 2-second poll cycle, which reads as broken.
2. Cap the Parameters <pre> with max-height + overflow-y:auto and audit syntaxHighlightJson for XSS escaping of user-controlled string values — large payloads currently bury all subsequent cards, and the highlight path is a potential XSS vector.
3. Replace the three instances of back-navigation (breadcrumb + BackLink in header + ghost link in Decide card) with the single breadcrumb row, and fix both empty/error states to use the shared EmptyState/ErrorState primitives instead of hand-rolled divs.

**Header / page-head** — Dual breadcrumb + BackLink stacked above h1, with callId in full mono below the title; status pills (pending/tier/decision) float right in a flex row.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Redundant navigation: both a breadcrumb row ('Approvals / <callId>') and a BackLink ('Back to queue') appear immediately above h1, doubling the chrome without adding hierarchy. The breadcrumb already provides back navigation.
  - *Fix:* Remove the standalone BackLink component — the breadcrumb row is sufficient. The 'Back to queue' link also appears again in the Decide card, so removing it here eliminates triple repetition.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The full callId is shown twice: once truncated in the breadcrumb (line 229 `callId.slice(0,12)…`) and once in full in `.page-head-sub` code block (line 229). The truncated breadcrumb crumb adds no value over the full ID already on screen.
  - *Fix:* Replace the breadcrumb crumb with a static label 'Detail' or simply omit the truncated ID from the breadcrumb; keep the full callId in `.page-head-sub` only.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** No loading skeleton: while `useBridgeFetch` is in-flight the header renders `toolName = 'Unknown'` and `tier` is undefined, so h1 flashes 'Unknown' and the tier pill disappears. The shared `Skeleton` primitive exists but is not used here.
  - *Fix:* When `loading && !data`, render a `<Skeleton>` in place of h1 text (e.g. `<Skeleton width={200} />`) and a `<SkeletonStatCard />` or pill-width skeleton for the tier pill.

**RelationStrip (cross-links)** — Four contextual links rendered below the header via RelationStrip — Session (conditional), Approval patterns, Knowledge, Approval rules.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Approval rules' item links to '/settings' with a generic label. The Session card further down (line 485) duplicates the Session link. Both point to related resources already described elsewhere on the page.
  - *Fix:* Deduplicate: drop the Session item from RelationStrip when the Session card is rendered below (or vice versa — the card is richer). Keep the three non-session cross-links in RelationStrip.

**Error / empty states** — Raw `<div className='alert-err'>` for fetch errors, and a bespoke `<div className='empty-state'>` for 404, both handrolled without using shared ErrorState/EmptyState primitives.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 404 branch uses a hand-rolled `.empty-state` div with a `<Link>` styled as `.btn sm primary` inline — not the shared `EmptyState` component. Visually inconsistent with other pages that use the primitive.
  - *Fix:* Replace the 404 `div.empty-state` block (lines 294-307) with `<EmptyState title='Unknown approval' body='...' action={{ label: 'Back to queue', href: '/approvals' }} />`.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The fetch error block (`alert-err` on line 291) has no icon, no actionable recovery hint, and no shared ErrorState wrapper. A bridge connectivity failure here gives the user no guidance.
  - *Fix:* Replace the raw `div.alert-err` with `<ErrorState message={error} hint='Check the bridge is running: patchwork status' />` or at minimum add a retry button wired to re-trigger the fetch.

**Delegation policy card** — Card with card-head (h2 + mode pill), then three Row items (Active mode, Risk tier, Matched rule) followed by a prose explanation paragraph.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** 'Active mode' Row and the mode pill in card-head both display the same value (e.g. 'high'). The Row is redundant when the pill already communicates mode at a glance.
  - *Fix:* Remove the 'Active mode' Row — the pill in card-head is sufficient. Retitle it 'Mode: high' for self-sufficiency. Keep 'Risk tier' and 'Matched rule' Rows.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The explanation paragraph uses `color: var(--ink-1)` at `var(--fs-m)` which reads well, but the 'Matched rule' Row value ('yes'/'no') carries low signal — a binary without visual distinction.
  - *Fix:* Replace the 'Matched rule' Row value with a colored pill: `<span class='pill ok'>matched</span>` or `<span class='pill muted'>bypassed</span>`. This makes the policy-match outcome scannable at a glance.

**Decide card (primary action)** — Card with left border colored by tier, h2 'Decide', awaiting-you pill, supporting copy, Approve/Reject buttons with spinner states, and a ghost 'Back to queue' link.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The spinner is implemented via inline `border`/`borderTopColor`/`animation` styles on a `<span>` (lines 381-383 and 397-399) rather than a shared loading indicator. The `animation: 'spin 0.7s linear infinite'` requires a global `@keyframes spin` which may not exist in all theme contexts; if missing, the spinner renders as a static circle.
  - *Fix:* Extract the spinner span into a shared `<Spinner size={14} />` component (or reuse whatever spinner the Toast/Dialog primitives already use), eliminating the inline animation dependency.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Back to queue' ghost link (line 406) is a third instance of the same back navigation after the breadcrumb and BackLink in the header. It adds clutter below the primary CTA and pushes the buttons' visual grouping apart from the `.approval-spacer` element.
  - *Fix:* Remove the 'Back to queue' ghost link from inside the Decide card. After approve/reject the user is already redirected; it is only relevant on cancel, which this workflow does not have.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** Buttons lack `aria-label` attributes — screen readers will announce '✓ Approve' and '✗ Reject' with the raw Unicode characters. The checkmark and cross are decorative but read as literal glyphs.
  - *Fix:* Add `aria-label='Approve this tool call'` and `aria-label='Reject this tool call'` to each button, and mark the icon spans with `aria-hidden='true'`.

**Decision card (resolved state)** — Card showing Decision, Reason, optional Specifier/PermissionMode/Summary as Row components; timestamp pill in card-head.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Decision' Row value (meta.decision) is plain text ('allow'/'deny') at `var(--ink-0)` with no color coding, while the header pill already color-codes the same value. Reading the card provides less visual signal than glancing at the header.
  - *Fix:* Replace the plain `<Row label='Decision' value={meta.decision} />` with an inline colored pill matching the header: `<span class={pill ok|err}>{meta.decision}</span>` inside the Row value slot, or add a `tone` prop to Row.

**Risk signals card** — Card with a flat flex-wrap of severity-colored pills; no explanation of what the signals mean or how they influenced gating.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Pills display only `s.label`; the `s.kind` field is only surfaced in the HTML `title` attribute (tooltip), invisible on mobile and inaccessible to keyboard users.
  - *Fix:* Render pills as `<kind>: <label>` text (e.g. 'pattern: writes outside workspace') so the signal kind is always visible, not hidden in a tooltip.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** Risk signals card and Personal signals card ('Your history with this call') share identical markup (flex-wrap of pills with the same severity mapping) but are split into two separate cards with no visual connective tissue explaining their relationship.
  - *Fix:* Merge both into a single 'Signals' card with two sub-sections ('Risk' and 'Your history') separated by a `<hr style='border-color:var(--line-2)'>` rule. Reduces card count and clarifies that both inform the same gate decision.

**Personal signals card ('Your history with this call')** — Card with flex-wrap of severity pills, identical layout to risk signals; always absent on decided approvals (only reads from pending.personalSignals).

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Card heading 'Your history with this call' is verbose and informal compared to sibling card headings ('Risk signals', 'Decision', 'Session'). Breaks heading rhythm.
  - *Fix:* Rename to 'Personal signals' to match the interface type name and align with sibling heading style.

**Session card** — Card showing session ID in mono code + a link 'All approvals for this session →'. Session is also linked in RelationStrip header.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** This card duplicates the Session entry already in the RelationStrip above. Both link to different targets (/sessions/[id] in RelationStrip vs /approvals?session=id here) which is useful but the duplication of the session ID code block is confusing — user sees the same ID displayed twice.
  - *Fix:* Keep this card but remove the Session item from RelationStrip (or vice versa). If keeping the card, add both links ('View session' and 'All approvals for session') inline inside the single card rather than splitting them.

**Parameters card (JSON block)** — Card with syntax-highlighted JSON via `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` in a `<pre class='detail-json-block'>`. No max-height or scroll constraint visible in JSX.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Large parameter payloads (e.g. file contents passed to write tools) will render an unbounded `<pre>` that pushes all subsequent cards far down the page, burying the Nearby activity section. No `max-height` or collapse control is applied.
  - *Fix:* Add `style={{ maxHeight: 320, overflowY: 'auto' }}` to the `<pre>` element, or wrap in a disclosure `<details><summary>Show parameters ({n} keys)</summary>…</details>` pattern.
- 🔴 **[high/M]** `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` with `syntaxHighlightJson` output introduces XSS risk if the highlighter does not escape all values. The 'JSON' muted pill label adds no value — the `<pre>` and mono font already signal this is code.
  - *Fix:* Audit `syntaxHighlightJson` for HTML-escaping of string values (especially user-controlled tool params like file paths or content strings). Remove the decorative 'JSON' pill — it is noise.

**Nearby activity table** — Horizontally-scrollable table with 5 columns (Time, Kind, Tool/Event, Duration, Status); lifecycle rows show '—' in Tool, Duration, Status columns.

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The 'Kind' column displays lifecycle event names (e.g. 'session_start') as pills alongside tool names as 'tool' pills, making event kinds harder to distinguish. Lifecycle rows always have '—' in 3 of 5 columns, wasting horizontal space.
  - *Fix:* Collapse the Kind and Tool/Event columns into a single 'Activity' column: for tool rows show `<pill>tool</pill> toolName`; for lifecycle rows show `<pill muted>event</pill> eventName`. Drop the now-redundant Kind column entirely.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Timestamp cells use `relTime()` with no `title` attribute fallback visible in JSX (line 537 does have `title={e.timestamp}` — correct). However, the pill count badge in card-head ('±60s · {data.nearby.length}') uses `var(--fs-xs)` implicitly inside `.pill muted` — the window explanation '±60s' is not obviously associated with the time column.
  - *Fix:* Move the '±60s' window description to a `<p class='hint'>` beneath the card-head rather than cramming it into the count pill. A pill should hold a count, not a unit+count hybrid.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** No empty state when `data.nearby` exists but has length 0 — the section is simply absent. But if `data` loaded successfully and nearby is an empty array, the user gets no feedback that the context window was queried and found nothing.
  - *Fix:* Render the Nearby activity card even when `data.nearby.length === 0`, with an `<EmptyState>` or simple `<p class='muted'>No activity in the ±60s window.</p>` inside, so the user knows the lookup ran.

**Loading state (global)** — No explicit loading indicator anywhere on the page; while `loading && !data` the page renders the header with toolName='Unknown' and no cards, silently.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The page has zero loading state — no skeleton, no spinner, no placeholder cards. During the first 2-second poll cycle the user sees a blank section with 'Unknown' in h1, which looks broken.
  - *Fix:* Add `{loading && !data && <SkeletonList count={3} />}` (or individual `<SkeletonStatCard />` blocks) after the page-head, to fill the card area while data is fetching. The primitives exist and are unused here.

**Row helper component (used in multiple cards)** — Local `Row` component uses `var(--border-subtle)` for divider, `var(--ink-2)` for label, `var(--ink-0)` for value. Right-aligned value with `textAlign: right`.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** `var(--border-subtle)` is not a documented design token in the listed token set (which uses `--line-1/2/3`). If the token resolves to undefined, the divider border disappears, leaving rows with no visual separation.
  - *Fix:* Replace `var(--border-subtle)` with `var(--line-2)` (the standard subtle separator token) to guarantee correct rendering in both themes.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Row `value` prop is typed as `string`, so booleans, numbers, or JSX (e.g. a colored pill for the Decision field) cannot be passed — the Decision card has to show plain text. Multiple callsites already work around this by nesting content in `.card` directly.
  - *Fix:* Widen the `value` type to `React.ReactNode` to allow inline pills, links, or code spans, and remove the `textAlign: right` constraint so multi-line values can left-align naturally.


### Suggestions  `/suggestions`

**Top 3:**
1. Remove the editorial-h1 accent tagline ('— patterns mined from your runs.') and keep only 'Suggestions' as the h1 — the subtitle already carries the explanation, and the current merged form hurts scannability, screen reader titles, and heading hierarchy.
2. Increase the dismiss button (✕) touch target to at least 36px minimum dimension and add adequate gap from adjacent CTAs — at ~18x20px computed size it is the most likely source of mis-taps on mobile, particularly on the trust-graduation rows where 'Graduate trust' and ✕ sit in the same flex span.
3. Persist suggestion-dismiss state to localStorage keyed by suggestion identity so dismissals survive page reloads and lookback changes — the current ephemeral state means dismissed items reappear on every visit, eroding user trust in the UI.

**Cluster tab nav (DecisionsTabs)** — Renders the shared DecisionsTabs ('Pending / Suggested / Knowledge') at the very top of the section, before the page-head. No pendingCount prop is passed so the live badge on Pending is always invisible here.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** pendingCount is never passed — the live approval-count badge on the Pending tab is always absent on this page, removing urgency cues that the shared component was designed to surface.
  - *Fix:* Wire useBridgeFetch('/api/bridge/approvals/pending-count') (or derive from existing data fetches) and pass the result as pendingCount to DecisionsTabs, matching how the Approvals page does it.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The active tab label is 'Suggested' in DecisionsTabs but the page title says 'Suggestions'. The mismatch creates a small but unnecessary cognitive gap.
  - *Fix:* Align the tab label to 'Suggestions' (or the page h1 to 'Suggested') so the two always read identically.

**Page header (page-head)** — Flex row: left = editorial-h1 + HintCard.Toggle + editorial-sub + RelationStrip; right = Lookback select + hint-count pill. The h1 embeds an accent span reading '— patterns mined from your runs.'

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The h1 accent '— patterns mined from your runs.' is a serif-italic tagline that buries the functional label. The page name 'Suggestions' must be parsed from 'Suggestions — patterns mined from your runs.' Screen readers and title bars read the whole string.
  - *Fix:* Move the tagline into the editorial-sub (it already exists at line 190–193), leaving the h1 as just 'Suggestions'. Drop the accent span entirely — the subtitle already carries the same explanation.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The editorial-sub has fontFamily: 'inherit' overriding the CSS rule that sets var(--font-sans). The override is a no-op at best and a fragile footgun if the parent font changes.
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline style={{ fontFamily: 'inherit' }} from the editorial-sub div at line 190 — the global .editorial-sub rule already sets font-family correctly.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Lookback select uses inline styles (background, border, borderRadius, color, fontSize, padding, outline: none) that duplicate the system's native select styling and suppress the focus ring entirely (outline: none).
  - *Fix:* Replace inline styles with className="select-sm" (or the project's existing form-select utility if present); if no utility exists, at minimum remove outline: none and add focus-visible styles to restore keyboard accessibility.

**HintCard (contextual onboarding card)** — Renders below the page-head as a dismissable orange-tinted aside with a ✦ icon, title, body, optional tip, and X button. Hidden after first dismissal; re-openable via the ? toggle in the h1 row.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** When HintCard is visible it pushes the suggestion groups down but has no role='status' or aria-live region, so screen readers who land on the page after the hint mounts mid-render get no announcement.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-live='polite' to the aside in HintCard.tsx so assistive tech announces the contextual tip on first visit without interrupting navigation.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The HintCard's r-3 (10px) border-radius is inconsistent with the surrounding card elements that all use --r-l (the design system's large radius token). The mismatch makes it look like a foreign component.
  - *Fix:* Change borderRadius from var(--r-3) to var(--r-l) in HintCard.tsx to align with .card and the rest of the surface.

**Loading state** — Shows <SkeletonList rows={5} columns={3} /> only when loading AND suggestions.length === 0 (i.e. first load only). Correct primitive usage.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** On the initial load, SkeletonList renders three columns but the actual suggestion rows are a single-column list of variable-height rows (pill + label + CTA). The skeleton shape does not match the real layout, creating a jarring layout shift.
  - *Fix:* Pass columns={1} to SkeletonList (or build a dedicated SuggestionSkeletonRow that mimics the 3-part flex row) so the skeleton geometry matches the content it represents.

**Error state** — Two separate error branches: full ErrorState component when no cached data; inline .alert-err div when data exists and a background refetch fails.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .alert-err message 'Refresh failed — {error}' raw-interpolates the error object (which may be an Error instance whose toString() produces 'Error: ...' including a stack fragment on some runtimes) directly into the DOM.
  - *Fix:* Coerce to a human-readable string: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error), and cap at ~120 chars to prevent layout overflow — matching the pattern already used in GraduateButton.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .alert-err div lacks role='alert', so background-refetch failures are invisible to screen readers.
  - *Fix:* Add role='alert' and aria-live='assertive' to the .alert-err div for the stale-data error branch.

**Empty state** — Uses the shared EmptyState primitive with a title and multi-sentence description JSX. No icon prop, no action prop.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The EmptyState description is five sentences long and includes a CLI hint. It buries the primary call to action (widen the lookback) in the middle of prose. Shorter empty states with a direct action convert better.
  - *Fix:* Trim the description to one sentence ('No patterns found in the last {sinceDays} day(s).') and pass an action prop with a button that increments sinceDays to the next option (e.g. from 7 to 30), providing an in-page recovery path instead of just text.

**Suggestion group cards (SuggestionGroup)** — Each group renders a .card with a .card-head (h2 + count pill), subtitle paragraph, and a <ul role='list'> of SuggestionRow items. Up to 3 groups stacked vertically.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** .card has a :hover transform + border-color transition designed for clickable cards. Suggestion groups are not clickable — applying lift-on-hover misleads users into expecting a navigation target.
  - *Fix:* Add a pointer-events: none hover suppression via a modifier class (e.g. className='card card--static') and a CSS rule .card--static:hover { transform: none; box-shadow: var(--card-shadow); border-color: var(--line-1); } to opt out of the interactive hover style.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The subtitle paragraph (the KIND_META.explanation text) renders at var(--fs-s) in var(--ink-2). On the light theme --ink-2 at fs-s (13px) may fail WCAG AA contrast against --card-bg. It also visually competes with the group count pill in the card-head.
  - *Fix:* Bump subtitle to var(--fs-m) (14px/1rem) and optionally move it inline under the h2 using a margin-top: 2px span rather than a separate paragraph to reduce vertical height and keep it clearly subordinate to the heading.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** 'Show N more' button after SUGGESTION_PAGE_SIZE (20) items has no aria-expanded / aria-controls, so assistive tech cannot determine that activating it will reveal more list items.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-expanded={showAll} and aria-controls pointing to the ul's id, and update the button label to 'Show all {items.length} suggestions' for clarity.

**Suggestion rows (SuggestionRow)** — Flex row: kind pill (fs-2xs) | label text (fs-m, flex:1) | action CTA(s) + dismiss button. Animated entrance (sug-fade-up) and dismiss (sug-dismiss). Dismiss is client-state only — reverts on page reload.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The dismiss button uses a Unicode ✕ character at var(--fs-s) as its only visual, with no minimum tap target (computed size is roughly 18x20px via 2px/4px padding). On mobile this violates the 44x44pt WCAG 2.5.5 touch target guideline and is easy to mis-tap next to small action buttons.
  - *Fix:* Set minimum width/height of 36px on the dismiss button (padding: 6px 8px or explicit min-width/min-height) and ensure at least 8px gap between it and the adjacent CTA button.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Dismiss is ephemeral — client state only, resets on page reload or lookback change. Users who dismiss a recurring suggestion will see it return on every visit with no feedback that it will come back.
  - *Fix:* Either (a) persist dismiss state to localStorage keyed by suggestion identity (kind + pair/recipeName) so it survives reloads, or (b) replace 'Dismiss' with 'Not interested' and render a muted 'Hidden — change lookback to reset' inline to set correct expectations. Option (a) is lower effort.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Mouse hover color change on the dismiss button (✕) is handled via inline onMouseEnter/onMouseLeave DOM manipulation rather than CSS :hover. This pattern is inconsistent with the rest of the codebase, doesn't work for keyboard focus, and is not needed given global CSS is available.
  - *Fix:* Remove the onMouseEnter/onMouseLeave handlers; add a scoped rule .suggestion-row .dismiss-btn:hover, .suggestion-row .dismiss-btn:focus-visible { color: var(--ink-1); } to globals.css, and add className='dismiss-btn' to the button.

**Co-occurring pair CTA ('Draft a recipe' link)** — A Link styled as 'btn sm' that navigates to /recipes/new?vars=toolA,toolB. Label is 'Draft a recipe'.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The Link has textDecoration: none as an inline style but uses className='btn sm', which already suppresses underlines. The inline style is redundant noise that will confuse future editors.
  - *Fix:* Remove the style={{ textDecoration: 'none' }} prop from the co-occurring pair Link (and the analogous ghost Links in the installed-but-unused and trust-graduation sections) — the .btn class handles this.

**Trust graduation CTA (GraduateButton)** — Stateful button: idle → loading → done/error. 'done' renders a ✓ span with role='status'. 'error' renders inline error text with role='alert'. Accompanied by a 'View recipe' ghost link.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** After a successful graduation, the row still shows the full suggestion row with pill and label. There is no signal to the surrounding list that this item has been actioned — users must visually parse the ✓ text to know the suggestion is resolved.
  - *Fix:* On state === 'done', set a CSS class (e.g. data-resolved='true') on the li.suggestion-row that applies opacity: 0.5 and a strikethrough or muted style to the label, visually communicating completion without removing the row until the next refetch.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** GraduateButton's error text is capped at 120 chars but has no max-width or text wrapping constraint in the inline flex span. Long server error messages can cause the action column to overflow the row's flex layout on narrow viewports.
  - *Fix:* Add max-width: 260px; overflow-wrap: break-word to the error span's inline style, or wrap the error in a block-level element below the button row.

**Installed-but-unused tool CTAs** — Renders up to 3 ghost Link buttons, each with fontFamily: var(--font-mono) and fs-xs, linking to /activity?tool=toolName&tab=tools.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Up to 3 monospace ghost buttons in a flex row with gap: 6px can overflow the CTA column on mobile when tool names are long (e.g. 'searchWorkspaceSymbols'). The flex row does flexWrap: wrap but the minimum button width is unbounded.
  - *Fix:* Add max-width: 180px; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; white-space: nowrap to each tool link button, with title={toolName} already present as the full-name fallback for truncated labels.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The label (s.label) for installed_but_unused items reads as a generic summary (e.g. '4 unused tools'). The CTA buttons then show specific tool names. This creates redundancy with details.unusedCount already embedded in the label, and users see the count twice.
  - *Fix:* Remove the unusedCount from the s.label for unused suggestions (or move it to the subtitle level) so the row label names the category and the CTA buttons provide the actionable specifics without repeating the number.

**Footer / generatedAt timestamp** — A plain <p> at var(--fs-xs) and var(--ink-2) showing 'Generated at HH:MM:SS AM/PM.' using toLocaleTimeString().

- ⚪ **[low/S]** toLocaleTimeString() without a locale argument renders differently across browsers and OS locales (12h vs 24h, timezone labels). On a local tool this is minor but still causes inconsistency in screenshots and automated tests.
  - *Fix:* Use toLocaleTimeString('en', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' }) to stabilize to HH:MM format, or use a relative time (e.g. 'Generated 2 minutes ago') which is more scannable than an absolute clock time.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The timestamp has no aria-live or role, so it silently updates every 30s (the polling interval) without any screen-reader announcement. The auto-refresh also has no visible indicator, leaving users unsure if the data is current.
  - *Fix:* Add a small animated dot or 'Auto-refreshes every 30s' note next to the timestamp (matching the pattern used on Runs or Activity pages if present), and add aria-live='polite' so assistive tech announces the updated time on each refresh.


### Knowledge (Decisions)  `/decisions`

**Top 3:**
1. Trim the h1 tagline — remove the serif '.accent' clause and move description to .editorial-sub; the current h1 delays reading the page name and the decorative span is called out in the CSS comments as no longer earning emphasis.
2. Replace the bare .alert-err background-refresh failure div with a dismissible Toast or inline ErrorState with retry button — raw error strings are unreadable and there is no recovery path for the user today.
3. Remove the generic 'decision' chip from default info-variant rows — with most entries sharing this chip it adds noise without signal; keep only err/warn/accent chips and let the colored border-left carry the info-variant identity.

**Sub-nav (DecisionsTabs)** — Cluster tab nav rendered as the first child of the section, before the page-head.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** No visible active-tab indicator is visible in this file — DecisionsTabs is a black-box import, but if it uses the shared ActivityTabs/AnalyticsTabs pattern it likely sits above the page-head which breaks the spatial reading order (nav → title → content).
  - *Fix:* Confirm DecisionsTabs renders its active state with the shared tab-underline token. If the tab nav sits inside the section before .page-head, wrap both in a header element so screen readers get landmark order: nav first, then heading.

**Header / page-head** — Two-column .page-head with editorial-h1 left and three filter inputs right; subtitle shows trace count + API method names; RelationStrip cross-links below.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The h1 tagline 'Knowledge — the knowledge base your agents wrote.' buries the noun in a serif italic clause. The decorative accent span delays reading the actual page name and wastes contrast on --ink-2 gray.
  - *Fix:* Trim the h1 to 'Knowledge' or 'Decisions'. Move the descriptive phrase to .editorial-sub (already present below). Drop the <span class='accent'> entirely per the existing CSS comment that calls these out as 'no longer earning emphasis'.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .editorial-sub contains raw API identifiers — 'ctxSaveTrace persists · ctxQueryTraces recalls' — which are developer jargon, not user-facing copy. They mean nothing to a new user and clutter the data line.
  - *Fix:* Replace with 'Agents save decisions here · recalled at next session start'. Keep trace count and LivePill but remove the raw function names.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The visually-hidden label on the search input is doubly declared: both a <span class='visually-hidden'> with inline clip CSS AND an aria-label on the input itself. The span has no semantic purpose since the input already has aria-label, and the position:absolute + clip style is hand-rolled rather than using a .visually-hidden utility class.
  - *Fix:* Remove the <span> and its wrapping <label>. The aria-label on the input is sufficient and correct. Apply the .visually-hidden utility class if a visible label is later needed.

**Filter bar (search + ref + time window)** — Three controls in a flex row right-aligned in page-head: text search (280px), ref filter (180px mono), and a select for time window; focus ring via .decisions-input-focus wrapper.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The two text inputs have no visible label — only aria-label. The ref input's placeholder 'Filter by ref (e.g. PR-42)' disappears on typing, leaving no hint about what the field does. On mobile these reflow to full-width but the select stays auto-width, creating inconsistent heights.
  - *Fix:* Add a small visible label above each input (or an inline prefix chip) using --ink-3 at --fs-2xs. Use .decisions-input-focus already on the wrappers. Set the select width to match a consistent token (e.g. 140px) so all three controls align to the same height in the row.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The active-filter count is not surfaced anywhere. When all three filters are set the only signal is empty results — the header still reads 'N traces'.
  - *Fix:* Add a small badge or parenthetical '(filtered)' next to the trace count in .editorial-sub when any filter is active. This leverages the existing trace count span — just append conditionally.

**Tag cloud / filter pills** — Horizontal flex row of .pill.muted / .pill.info buttons above the list, gated on allTags.length > 0; a 'Show all' overflow button at 20+ tags; 'Tags' label in mono at --ink-3.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Tags' label uses --fs-2xs mono at --ink-3, making it nearly invisible against the row of pills. It reads as a label for the entire section but lacks the visual separation of a proper filter-section heading.
  - *Fix:* Elevate 'Tags' to --ink-2 and add a colon or a thin vertical divider (var(--line-2)) to separate it from the pills. Alternatively apply the existing .filter-chips and .filter-chip CSS that already exists in globals.css instead of the ad-hoc flex+gap+button pattern.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** Clicking a .tag-pill inside a decision row sets the global tag filter but there is no visual confirmation that the tag bar above has updated — the active pill (.pill.info) may be off-screen if the list is long.
  - *Fix:* After clicking an inline tag-pill, scroll the tag cloud into view (scrollIntoView on the tag bar container ref) and/or apply a brief ring pulse on the matching pill so the user knows the filter applied.

**Loading state** — <SkeletonList rows={5} columns={4} /> shown only when loading and traces array is empty.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** SkeletonList with columns={4} implies a table layout but the actual content is a card/row layout with variable-height problem+solution blocks. The skeleton shape misleads the user about what is coming.
  - *Fix:* Replace with a <SkeletonStatCard /> or a custom skeleton that mirrors 1-3 .decision-row tall blocks (two sub-panels side by side, a tag pill strip at bottom). If SkeletonList is the only available variant, use rows={4} columns={1} to approximate the single-column feel.

**Error states** — Full <ErrorState> component when no data + error; a bare .alert-err div when stale data exists alongside a refresh error.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .alert-err div for background-refresh failures is plain text with no retry affordance ('Refresh failed — <raw error string>'). The raw error string is often a URL path fragment, not user-readable.
  - *Fix:* Replace the .alert-err div with a small inline <ErrorState> or a dismissible Toast so users get a retry button. Cap the error display to the first 80 chars and append '…' — raw error strings from fetch can be very long.

**Empty state** — <EmptyState> component with conditional title and description for both 'no data' and 'no matches'; 'Clear filters' ghost button when filters are active.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The filtered empty state description is constructed by concatenating filter values directly into the string (e.g. 'No decisions tagged "foo" with ref matching "bar" containing "baz"'). At three active filters this sentence becomes unwieldy and can overflow on narrow viewports.
  - *Fix:* Show filter chips inline in the empty state body instead of prose — e.g. 'No decisions matching:' followed by the active filter values rendered as small .tag-pill spans. This matches the pill language used elsewhere on the page.

**Decision card list** — Vertical flex column of .decision-row cards; each card has header row (chip + ref + spacer + session link + reltime), optional grid-2 problem/solution blocks, and inline tag pills.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The type chip ('bug' / 'risk' / 'decision' / 'feature') is derived from tag heuristics and defaults to 'decision' for everything that doesn't match. Most entries will show the generic 'decision' chip, adding visual noise without information value.
  - *Fix:* Make the chip optional: only render it when variant !== 'info'. For the common 'info' case, rely solely on the blue border-left color accent. This reduces per-row clutter and makes the err/warn/accent chips actually scannable.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Problem' and 'Solution' label rows use a decorative '✻ ' glyph that is marked aria-hidden but contributes to visual noise. The err-soft / green-soft background pair already distinguishes the two panels — the glyph doesn't add information.
  - *Fix:* Remove the '✻ ' span. The coloured backgrounds and uppercase 'Problem' / 'Solution' labels are sufficient. If iconography is desired, use a single semantic SVG (16px) that is consistently sized with the design token --s-4.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The session link (.pill.muted with truncated sessionId) has no hover label beyond the title attribute. title tooltips are inaccessible on touch devices. A user can't tell what clicking it does from the 8-char hash alone.
  - *Fix:* Add text 'Session' before the 8-char hash — 'Session a1b2c3d4' — inside the pill. This costs ~50px but eliminates the mystery. Alternatively replace with the existing SessionChip primitive if one exists.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The card gap is var(--s-2) (8px) which is very tight for cards that can be 80–120px tall with problem+solution blocks. Vertical rhythm is compressed.
  - *Fix:* Increase gap to var(--s-3) (12px) to give breathing room between cards without wasting space. The existing decision-row padding of 12px 16px stays the same.

**Ref / EntityLink display** — The ref field heuristically matches PR-N or #N and renders an <EntityLink kind='run'> for both patterns, otherwise renders the raw ref string in mono.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Both PR-N and #N refs resolve to kind='run', which may not be semantically correct — #N is typically an issue number, not a run. The EntityLink visual treatment (color, icon) for 'run' applied to an issue ref could mislead users.
  - *Fix:* Map PR-N to kind='run' and #N to kind='recipe' (or whichever kind maps to issues). If the EntityLink component doesn't support issues, fall back to a plain mono span rather than misusing 'run'.


### Runs list  `/runs`

**Top 3:**
1. Add a Status select to the filter bar — status filtering is currently split across non-obvious inline links in editorial-sub and clickable stat cards, making the most fundamental filter (show only errors) undiscoverable without understanding the card interaction model.
2. Port assertion failures to the mobile card detail — users on mobile see zero assertion detail when a run fails assertions, even though it is the primary failure signal shown on desktop; this is a straight data parity gap.
3. Make halt-pill interactivity obvious — the halt category pills in runs-summary-band are the primary entry point for diagnosing failures, but they look identical to the static judge verdict spans beside them; adding a visible hover state would immediately improve the signal-to-noise ratio of the most operationally important section on the page.

**Page header** — h1 'Runs' with conditional editorial tagline in --accent orange, editorial-sub shows count/window/avg, RelationStrip with Recipes and Halts links, LivePill docked top-right

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Editorial tagline '— every patch your agents stitched.' appears only when runs=0 or null, making the h1 visually unstable — it shifts width on load and the serif accent copy is decorative rather than informational
  - *Fix:* Remove the conditional tagline entirely; the editorial-sub line already carries all the context (count, window, avg). The h1 'Runs' stands cleanly without the flourish.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** editorial-sub concatenates count, window label, and avg duration as a single dense string with · separators; 'avg 0ms' appears before data is meaningful and 'any time' is lowercase-jargon that reads as filler
  - *Fix:* Suppress 'avg —' when avgMs===0 (no finished runs). Capitalise the window label fragment to match sentence case. Wrap the inline filter buttons (running/cancelled/interrupted) in a visually distinct wrapper — a small gap or faint --line-2 separator — so they don't bleed into the descriptive text.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** RelationStrip Halts chip uses tone='err' when haltSummary.total>0 but no count is shown on the chip itself, so the red tint gives no quantity signal
  - *Fix:* Change label to 'Halts ({haltSummary.total})' when total>0 so the chip reads '3 Halts' rather than just a colored 'Halts'.

**Halt summary band** — Horizontal band with mono 'halts (window): N' label + clickable category pills; only shown when haltSummary.total>0

- 🔴 **[high/S]** runs-halt-pill buttons all navigate to status='error' filter but give no visible affordance that they are interactive — they look identical to the static judge verdict spans below them
  - *Fix:* Add cursor:pointer and a hover background shift (e.g. data-cat-specific tint at 15% opacity) to runs-halt-pill to distinguish them from the static runs-judge-pill spans; or add a subtle 'click to filter' hint in the title text that is surfaced more visibly (e.g. a small ↗ icon).
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Two separate .runs-summary-band divs (halts + judgments) stack without any visual separator, making them read as one undifferentiated band when both are present
  - *Fix:* Add a 1px --line-2 top border to the second band when both are rendered, or give each band a distinct left-border accent color (--err for halts, --accent-cool for judgments) to create visual grouping.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** Judge verdict spans in the judgment band are non-interactive (just <span>) but sit in an identical layout to the clickable halt pills — sighted users cannot tell which are actionable
  - *Fix:* Either make judge verdict spans filter the list (clicking 'request_changes' filters runs with judge step verdicts) or visually mark them as display-only with a different pill variant (e.g. 'muted' background vs the colored halt pills).

**Filter bar** — Horizontal row: text input for recipe search, two <select> dropdowns (trigger, window), optional attempt/session pills, conditional Clear button

- 🔴 **[high/M]** The status filter is surfaced only through the stat cards below — there is no <select> or tab for status in the filter bar itself, so the status=running/cancelled/interrupted links buried in editorial-sub are the only path to those filters if stat cards are missed
  - *Fix:* Add a Status <select> alongside Trigger and Window in the filter bar (values: all, running, done, error, cancelled, interrupted). The stat cards can remain as visual shortcuts but the filter bar should be complete on its own.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** attempt: and session: active-filter pills (className='pill mono xs') have no dismiss/clear affordance — users must hit the global Clear button which also resets recipe/trigger/window
  - *Fix:* Add an × button inside each pill that clears only that specific filter (setAttemptFilter('') or setSessionFilter('')), consistent with how multi-select filter chips work elsewhere.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Clear button only appears when at least one filter is non-default, but it has no aria-label describing what will be cleared
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label='Clear all filters' to the Clear button.

**Stat cards row** — Three card buttons (All runs, Successful, Errored) each with label, AnimatedNumber, and a footer line; act as toggle filters via aria-pressed; missing Running/Cancelled/Interrupted as direct cards

- 🔴 **[high/M]** Three stat cards do not cover the 'running', 'cancelled', or 'interrupted' statuses — those are relegated to the editorial-sub as inline btn-inline links, which are easily missed and have no visual weight
  - *Fix:* Add a fourth stat card 'Active' showing stats.running with data-variant='running' (pulse animation) that filters status='running'. Running is the most time-sensitive status and deserves card-level prominence. Cancelled and interrupted can remain as inline links since they are less urgent.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** runs-stat-card footer lines show 'Any time' repeated across all three cards when window='any' — redundant since the window is already shown in editorial-sub and the filter bar
  - *Fix:* Show the window label in the footer only on the 'All runs' card; on Successful/Errored cards replace it with the percentage (success/error rate) exclusively, which is more useful.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** Stat cards use custom className='card runs-stat-card' rather than the shared StatCard primitive, which may diverge from the design system over time
  - *Fix:* Migrate to StatCard (if it accepts an onClick/aria-pressed prop) or document the intentional deviation in a code comment so future maintainers don't wonder if StatCard was overlooked.

**Loading state** — SkeletonList with rows=6, columns=6 shown while windowedRuns===null and no error

- 🟡 **[med/S]** SkeletonList renders but the stat cards above it are still empty/zero during load — the three card buttons show '0' via AnimatedNumber before data arrives, which is misleading
  - *Fix:* Wrap the stat card row in the same null check (runs===null) and render SkeletonStatCard placeholders (the primitive already exists) in place of the three cards while loading.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The halt and judge summary bands are absent during load but then pop in after, causing a layout shift that pushes the filter bar and stat cards down
  - *Fix:* Reserve fixed min-height for the summary band area (e.g. min-height: 0 initially, animate height on entry) or use a skeleton placeholder band to avoid CLS.

**Error state** — Two distinct error paths: ErrorState component when runs===null+err (full-page), and a raw <div className='alert-err'> inline banner when err && runs exist (stale refresh failure)

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stale-refresh error path renders a raw <div className='alert-err'> rather than the shared Toast or ErrorState primitive, creating visual inconsistency with other error surfaces
  - *Fix:* Replace the raw alert-err div with a Toast or a small inline AlertBanner component; if neither exists as a primitive, use ErrorState with a compact variant or an inline role='alert' div styled with --err border-left.

**Empty state** — EmptyState component with context-aware title/description/action covering filtered vs unfiltered vs windowed-empty cases; action is either Clear filters button or Go to recipes link

- 🟡 **[med/S]** When empty due to an active time window (e.g. 'Last hour') and no filters, the EmptyState description says 'Try widening the window' but the window select is above the fold and may not be visible without scrolling on a short viewport
  - *Fix:* Add an inline action button 'Widen to 24h' or 'Show all time' alongside or instead of no action, so the user can act without scrolling back up.

**Desktop table** — 6-column table (When, Recipe, Trigger, Status, Duration with progress bar, Task); rows expand inline via <tr> detail row; j/k keyboard nav; aria-keyshortcuts on <table>; stagger animation on rows

- 🟡 **[med/S]** aria-keyshortcuts='j k' is placed on <table> but the interactive rows use role='button' — screen readers will not naturally associate the shortcut hint with the rows; additionally j/k navigation is undiscoverable for all users
  - *Fix:* Move aria-keyshortcuts to a wrapping landmark or add a visually-hidden keyboard hint (e.g. 'j/k to navigate rows') near the table caption or as a <caption> element; add a <caption className='sr-only'> with 'Run history, press j/k to navigate rows'.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Expanded detail row (<tr className='task-row-expand'>) uses inline styles for the error block (borderLeft, paddingLeft, borderRadius, background, padding, marginBottom) mixing ad-hoc values with CSS variables, inconsistent with the design token system
  - *Fix:* Extract the error block styling into a CSS class (e.g. run-expand-error-block) using token variables: border-left: 3px solid var(--err); padding: var(--s-3) var(--s-4); background: color-mix(in oklch, var(--err) 6%, var(--card-bg)); border-radius: 0 var(--r-s) var(--r-s) 0.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Task' column shows taskId.slice(0,8) in mono muted text — the column header 'Task' does not make clear this is a task ID truncation, and there is no link to navigate directly from the table to the run detail page
  - *Fix:* Rename the column header to 'ID' or 'Run ID', and make the truncated ID a <Link href={/runs/${r.seq}}> so the cell itself is navigable, reducing reliance on expanding the row then clicking 'Open full run →'.

**Expanded row detail panel** — Inline <tr> with model, createdAt ISO timestamp, optional errorMessage pre block, optional assertion failures list, optional outputTail pre block, and 'Open full run →' link button

- ⚪ **[low/S]** createdAt is rendered as full ISO timestamp (2026-06-25T07:00:00.000Z) in a small mono span — this is redundant with the 'When' column which already shows the relative time; the absolute ISO string adds noise without utility at this detail level
  - *Fix:* Replace ISO createdAt with a human-readable absolute datetime (e.g. 'Jun 25 07:00') using toLocaleString() with {dateStyle:'medium',timeStyle:'short'}, or omit it entirely and keep only the run-detail page for full timestamp data.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** assertion failures list uses <ul className='run-expand-assertions'> with array index as key and no ARIA role — the failure items have a mono key then em-dash then message, but the em-dash is a literal string '—' which is not a semantic separator
  - *Fix:* Wrap each item as <li> with a <dt>/<dd> or <strong> + <span> pattern; replace ' — ' with a visually styled separator (::before pseudo or a styled <span>) so copy-paste and screen reader output is cleaner.

**Mobile card list** — Stacked run-card divs shown ≤768px, each with head (RecipeChip + status pill), meta row (trigger pill, when, duration, taskId), and expanded detail on tap

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Mobile expanded card (run-card-detail) shows errorMessage and outputTail <pre> blocks without the error block styling (border-left, background tint) that the desktop expanded row uses — error severity is visually equal to normal output on mobile
  - *Fix:* Apply the same error-block styling (--err left border, tinted background) to the errorMessage pre block inside run-card-detail, matching desktop parity.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** run-card-detail on mobile does not show assertionFailures even though the desktop expanded row does — a user on mobile sees no assertion detail
  - *Fix:* Port the assertion failures block (the <ul> render) from the desktop expanded row into the run-card-detail section.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Mobile card has no aria-label (unlike the desktop tr which has a descriptive aria-label), so screen reader users on mobile get only the role='button' announcement with no context
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label={`Run of ${r.recipeName}, ${sLabel}, ${fmtWhen(r.doneAt)}`} to the mobile run-card div.

**Load more / pagination** — Single 'Load more (+100)' button at bottom of table and card list, conditionally shown when runs.length>=limit and windowed count equals total

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The Load more button label '+100' hardcodes RUNS_PAGE_SIZE as a magic number in the UI copy — if the constant changes the label stays wrong
  - *Fix:* Change label to `Load more (+${RUNS_PAGE_SIZE})` which is already done, but also add a small muted line below the button like 'Showing {windowedRuns.length} of {runs.length}+' to give users a sense of pagination progress.


### Run detail  `/runs/[seq]`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the loading state's .empty-state div with SkeletonList to prevent layout shift and provide a proper in-place skeleton — the current blank dashed card with 'Loading run…' causes a jarring full-page reflow when data arrives
2. Add role='tab' + aria-selected + role='tablist' to the Steps/Execution Plan tab bar — the current bespoke tabStyle() buttons have no ARIA tab semantics and keyboard users cannot determine which panel is active
3. Fix JudgeVerdictPill's two silent token bugs: var(--border) is undefined (border never renders) and the --ok-bg/--warn-bg fallbacks are dark-theme hex values that break in the light paper theme — both ship invisibly broken in light mode

**Sticky header** — Card pinned to top=0, zIndex 5; left side has breadcrumb + h1 RecipeChip + RelationStrip; right side packs trigger pill, status pill, duration, model, assertion count, timestamp, and Replay button in a flex-wrap row

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Header has no visible backdrop/blur to separate it from content scrolling beneath it — .card on a white/near-white background renders opaque but on dark theme the card-bg is semi-transparent (rgba 0.94), so body copy bleeds through the sticky header as the user scrolls the step list
  - *Fix:* Add `backdropFilter: 'var(--card-blur)'` and a thin bottom border `borderBottom: '1px solid var(--line-2)'` to the sticky card div so it acts as a true surface stop in both themes
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The flex-wrap right cluster (trigger pill, status, duration, model, assertions, timestamp, Replay button) has no visual grouping — on narrow viewports these all collapse into an undifferentiated blob; the timestamp sits last with only `marginLeft:4` separation and renders in --ink-3 (10px faint) next to the accent-coloured status pill, making it easy to miss
  - *Fix:* Group primary identity signals (status pill + duration) separately from secondary metadata (trigger, model, timestamp) using a `gap: 'var(--s-3)'` divider span or border-right rule; move timestamp to a second line under the h1 breadcrumb instead of the action row
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The Replay button uses raw inline styles (`border: '1px solid var(--line-2)'`, manual padding/radius) rather than the shared button utility class; it also lacks an aria-label, making its purpose opaque to screen-reader users who navigate by tab
  - *Fix:* Apply a shared `.btn` or `.btn-ghost` class (if one exists) or at minimum add `aria-label='Replay this run with mocked outputs'`; reuse the border-radius token `var(--r-m)` instead of `var(--r-1, 4px)`

**Replay status banner + confirm Dialog** — Inline banner (role=status, className alert-err/alert-ok) appears between header and main content when replay completes; Dialog modal uses raw inline-styled h3 + p + ReplayPreflight + action buttons

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The confirm Dialog's primary action button (`Replay (mocked)`) uses raw `background: var(--blue)` and `color: var(--surface)` — --blue is defined as text-only in dark theme (~5.1:1 contrast on canvas) but its contrast against --surface is unverified; no shared `.btn-primary` class is used
  - *Fix:* Use the `--accent` or `--ok` semantic token (both have verified contrast tables in globals) for the confirm CTA, or audit --blue contrast on --surface and document it; apply `.btn .btn-primary` classes to match other Dialog CTAs in the codebase
- ⚪ **[low/S]** ReplayPreflight warning block references `var(--amber)` and `var(--amber-soft)` as direct token names but the canonical semantic alias for amber is `var(--warn)` / `var(--warn-soft)` — raw colour tokens bypass theme switching
  - *Fix:* Replace `var(--amber)` with `var(--warn)` and `var(--amber-soft)` with `var(--warn-soft)` in ReplayPreflight; the border should use `color-mix(in srgb, var(--warn) 25%, transparent)` to match .alert-warn

**Loading / error / invalid-id states** — Three raw branches: invalid seq → plain `<div className='empty-state'>` with h3+p; loading run → `<div className='empty-state' role='status'><p>Loading run…</p></div>`; fetch error → `<div className='alert-err'>Failed to load run: {runErr}</div>`

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The loading branch uses the `.empty-state` CSS class (dashed-border centered card) instead of the `Skeleton` / `SkeletonList` primitives — this creates a layout shift once data loads, since `.empty-state` occupies the full viewport height then is replaced by the multi-card layout; other pages (RouteLoading) use SkeletonList for in-place placeholders
  - *Fix:* Replace the loading `empty-state` div with `<SkeletonList rows={8} />` (already used in RouteLoading) wrapped in a single `.card` so the sticky header stays visible and the layout does not jump
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The error branch uses a raw `<div className='alert-err'>` instead of the shared `ErrorState` component from `@/components/patchwork`; ErrorState provides an icon, retry affordance, and consistent spacing that the raw alert-err div lacks
  - *Fix:* Replace `<div className='alert-err'>Failed to load run: {runErr}</div>` with `<ErrorState title='Could not load run' description={runErr} />` from the patchwork index

**Tab bar (Steps / Execution Plan)** — Two `<button>` elements with fully inlined tabStyle() returning CSSProperties; active tab underlined with 2px solid --accent; tab bar sits in a flex row with borderBottom separator; no ARIA role or aria-selected attributes

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Tab buttons lack `role='tab'`, `aria-selected`, and a wrapping `role='tablist'` — keyboard users and screen readers can tab to the buttons but cannot infer they are tabs or which is active; the `aria-pressed` pattern used on Expand/Collapse buttons elsewhere in the page is the wrong ARIA role for tabs
  - *Fix:* Add `role='tablist'` to the wrapper div, `role='tab'` + `aria-selected={tab === t}` + `aria-controls` to each button, and wrap tab panels in `role='tabpanel'` with matching `id`; this follows the existing lbrd-tabs pattern in globals.css
- ⚪ **[low/M]** The inline tabStyle() function is a custom tab implementation while the codebase already has the cluster tab pattern (ActivityTabs, AnalyticsTabs, DecisionsTabs) and `.lbrd-tabs` / `.lbrd-tab` CSS in globals; this reinvents the wheel and drifts from visual consistency
  - *Fix:* Replace the bespoke tabStyle() buttons with `.rd-tab-btn` class (already defined in globals) that already sets transition; long-term align with the cluster tab components if a shared 2-tab variant exists

**Causal chain card** — Renders when parentSeq or childSeqs present; two-row flex layout with 'triggered by' / 'triggered' labels (--ink-3, fs-xs, minWidth 56px), RunChip, RecipeChip, and duration; card header says 'Causal chain' in ink-2 fs-s

- 🟡 **[med/S]** When the parent or child run data is still loading (async fetch), the row shows only the RunChip with no status or recipeName — nothing communicates the pending state; a user looking at a triggered child run sees an empty label slot with no skeleton or spinner
  - *Fix:* Show a `<Skeleton width='80px' />` inline in the RecipeChip and duration slots while `parent === null` (when parentSeq exists but fetch hasn't resolved); the Skeleton component is already imported in nearby pages
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Label text 'triggered by' and 'triggered' differ in length but share minWidth:56px — 'triggered by' is visually wider than 56px in fs-xs (roughly 70px), so the chip column shifts right and misaligns across rows
  - *Fix:* Set minWidth to 72px or use 'triggered →' / '← triggered by' so both fit the same column width; alternatively use a CSS grid with a fixed first column instead of flexbox so alignment is automatic

**Timeline card** — Card with 'Timeline' header (fs-s, fontWeight 600, ink-2) wrapping EntityTimeline; always rendered when run data is present, even for runs with no step detail; events include trigger, run, steps, inbox outputs

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Timeline' card header label is styled identically (fs-s, fw-600, ink-2) to other card section headers on the page ('Causal chain', 'Steps (N)', 'Execution Plan') — every card section looks the same weight, making it hard to scan which card is which at a glance
  - *Fix:* Differentiate the card header by using the semantic `.card-head` class (defined in globals, applies consistent label treatment) instead of raw inline style; this gives the header a shared look across all cards on the page

**Inbox outputs strip** — Inline flex card below Timeline when inboxOutputs present; 'Delivered to inbox' label in --ink-3 fs-xs fw-500 followed by InboxChip components; separate group also in RelatedPanel aside

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Inbox outputs appear twice: once in the main column strip card and once in the RelatedPanel aside under the 'Inbox outputs' group — this is redundant and causes confusion about which is canonical, especially when the aside is hidden on mobile
  - *Fix:* Remove the RelatedPanel 'Inbox outputs' group when the inline strip is rendered (pass inboxOutputs to the related groups array only when inboxOutputs is empty, so the aside shows a 'none' state); or collapse the inline strip and rely solely on the aside

**Step rows list (Steps card)** — Card with Steps (N) header + Expand all / Collapse all buttons + total duration; each StepRow has a 4-column grid (index, tool+bar, connector/status pill, duration); left border 3px shows running/error/transparent; hover triggers StepDiffHover portal

- 🔴 **[high/M]** The step row click target for expansion only activates when `step.error` is truthy (`onClick={() => step.error && toggleOpen()}`), but successful steps that have VD-2 capture data (resolvedParams/output) are also expandable via hover — keyboard users cannot access the StepDiffHover panel at all since it is mouse-only
  - *Fix:* Add keyboard accessibility: make error rows focusable with `tabIndex={0}` and `onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && step.error && toggleOpen()}`; for the diff hover panel, provide a dedicated 'Show diff' toggle button inside non-error rows so keyboard and touch users can access captured output
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The haltCategory fix hint line (`→ {HALT_CATEGORY_HINT[step.haltCategory]}`) is rendered in --ink-2 (fs-xs) directly below the --err haltReason; the `→` arrow prefix and the identical font-size to the haltReason line makes the two run together visually — users need to re-read to understand which is the problem description and which is the action
  - *Fix:* Visually distinguish the fix hint from the halt reason: use a `pill warn` chip labelled 'Fix hint' before the hint text, or indent + prefix with a wrench icon character; the current HALT_CATEGORY_HINT already provides good copy, it just needs presentation hierarchy
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The duration bar (3px tall, borderRadius 2, --border-subtle background) is extremely thin and indistinguishable at small proportions — for steps that take <1% of total runtime the bar renders at 2px (the min), which is invisible against the subtle background
  - *Fix:* Increase bar height to 4px and background opacity (use `var(--line-2)` instead of `var(--border-subtle)`/`var(--line-1)`) so sub-2% bars are still legible; also consider moving the bar below the step id row rather than nesting it inside the name column where it competes with error text

**Execution Plan tab (PlanView)** — Loaded lazily on tab switch; shows a badge row (triggerType, connectors, has-writes, parallel groups, depth, generated-at) then PlanStepRow list; loading state is a raw `<div style={{ padding:20 }}>Generating…</div>`

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Plan loading state is an unstyled div with text 'Generating…' — no spinner, no skeleton, no role='status'; it is indistinguishable from rendered content at a glance and provides no accessible announcement
  - *Fix:* Replace with `<div role='status' aria-live='polite' style={{padding:20}}><span className='muted'>Generating plan…</span></div>` or use the existing `rd-step-running-indicator` spinner; a SkeletonList with 5 rows would be even better for layout stability
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The plan's 'generated {ISO timestamp}' badge (`marginLeft:'auto'`) pushes to the far right of the badge row — on mobile, the badge row wraps and the generated-at badge no longer aligns right, it just wraps inline after the other pills with no visual separation
  - *Fix:* Move the generated-at timestamp to a separate line below the badge row, or use `flexShrink: 0` + `marginLeft: 'auto'` on a second flex row so it only right-aligns when there is space; alternatively use `.muted` small text below the card header instead of inside the badge strip

**Meta card (task id, timestamps, error message, prior fixes, output tail)** — Single card at bottom of main column; auto-fit grid of label+value pairs (TASK ID, STARTED, FINISHED, MODEL, ATTEMPT); error message in .rd-error-card; prior fixes in recess boxes; outputTail in TruncatablePre

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The `.rd-error-card` div has `borderLeft: '4px solid var(--err) !important'` inline — the `!important` is fighting with `.rd-error-card`'s CSS rule in globals (which also sets border); this pattern is fragile and leaks specificity details into JSX; the error card also has a ⚠ emoji + 'ERROR' label which is redundant with the red border and background
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline `borderLeft` and the `!important`; rely solely on `.rd-error-card` from globals for the visual treatment; replace the ⚠ emoji + 'ERROR' text label with a semantic `aria-label='Error'` on the container and a standard icon character from the design system (or just the pill colour since the red background is already communicating error)
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'PRIOR FIXES FOR {recipeName.toUpperCase()}' label concatenates the recipe name in uppercase inline, but recipe names can be long slugs — this makes the label read as all-caps code (e.g. 'PRIOR FIXES FOR CRYPTO-DAILY-BRIEF') which looks noisy; the 'see all →' link is styled with --info (blue) but shares the same fs-2xs as the label, making it almost invisible
  - *Fix:* Change label to 'Prior fixes' (sentence case, no recipe name repetition — the page is already scoped to this recipe) and increase the 'see all →' link font size to fs-s or give it a dedicated aria-label='See all traces for this recipe'
- 🟡 **[med/M]** The 'OUTPUT TAIL' section label and TruncatablePre appear at the very bottom of the meta card below error message and prior fixes — for long runs with many kb of output tail, the card becomes very tall and the most critical info (STARTED/FINISHED/TASK ID) is visually buried; the outputTail has no role='region' or heading
  - *Fix:* Move OUTPUT TAIL into a separate collapsible card (or a disclosure element `<details><summary>Output tail ({lineCount} lines)</summary>…</details>`) so the meta card stays compact; add `aria-label='Output tail'` to the TruncatablePre container

**Related panel aside (RelatedPanel)** — Sticky aside in .rd-related-aside (200px wide); groups: Recipe, Inbox outputs, Approvals, Traces; each group from RelatedPanel component; collapses to static on mobile

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Approvals group shows raw step IDs that start with 'approval' (e.g. 'approval-1', 'requestApproval') with status as meta — these IDs are meaningless to users and the status string ('ok'/'error') gives no context about what was approved or denied
  - *Fix:* Use `ApprovalChip` from `@/components/patchwork/entity` instead of raw kind:'approval' items in RelatedPanel, or at minimum map the label to something human-readable like the step tool name or the approval outcome label
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The Traces group always shows exactly one item (the recipe name with meta 'decision traces') regardless of whether any traces exist — on error runs this competes with the Prior Fixes section in the meta card, and on success runs it points to a potentially empty traces list
  - *Fix:* Gate the Traces group on `priorFixes.length > 0` (which is already fetched) and show the count in the meta string (e.g. '3 decision traces'); when no traces exist, omit the group entirely so the aside doesn't have stale placeholder links

**JudgeVerdictPill (step-row sub-component)** — Renders inside StepRow when judgeVerdict present; mono span for verdict label + muted first reason; fixList items bullet-listed with a 2px left border; uses hardcoded fallback colours (--ok-bg, --warn-bg) with CSS custom properties with defaults

- 🔴 **[high/S]** JudgeVerdictPill hardcodes fallback colours `--ok-bg: #1b3a1b` and `--warn-bg: #3a2a1b` which are dark-theme values — if --ok-bg is not defined in the light ('paper') theme, the pill renders with a dark green/brown background against a light surface, breaking contrast
  - *Fix:* Define `--ok-bg` and `--warn-bg` in globals.css under the light-theme `:root[data-theme='paper']` block (e.g. `--ok-bg: color-mix(in srgb, var(--ok) 12%, var(--surface))`) so the fallback hex values are never reached in production
- 🔴 **[high/S]** The fixList border uses `var(--border)` which is not a defined token in globals (tokens are --line-1/2/3 and the semantic aliases --border-subtle/default/strong); this silently resolves to `initial` (no border) in browsers, making the indent marker invisible
  - *Fix:* Change `borderLeft: '2px solid var(--border)'` to `borderLeft: '2px solid var(--line-2)'` to use a token that is actually defined

**Assertion failures panel** — Card with red header ('Assertion Failures (N)' + 'expect' pill), each failure in a 2-column grid showing assertion name pill, message in --err, and expected/actual values in mono muted fs-xs

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Expected/actual values are rendered as `JSON.stringify(f.expected)` inline in a `<span>` — for large objects this creates an extremely long unbreakable line (JSON.stringify produces single-line output) that overflows the card on mobile even though word-break is set on parent
  - *Fix:* Replace inline `JSON.stringify()` spans with a `<TruncatablePre>` (already defined in this file) using `text={JSON.stringify(f.expected, null, 2)}` so large objects are pretty-printed, line-wrapped, and collapsible


### Activity (Live)  `/activity`

**Top 3:**
1. Remove the serif italic tagline from the h1 ('every tool, every event, in real time.') — it buries the page title and reduces scannability at first glance; the h1 should read 'Activity' or 'Live Activity' with the tagline demoted to .editorial-sub or dropped.
2. Add <caption className='sr-only'>Live activity events</caption> and scope='col' on all <th> elements in the event table — the table is the primary content of the page and currently has no accessible name or column role annotations.
3. Bump chart card label font-size from var(--fs-2xs) 10px to var(--fs-xs) 11px and color from var(--ink-3) to var(--ink-2) for both 'Events / minute' and 'Top tools' headers — 10px ink-3 text fails WCAG AA contrast on both themes.

**Cluster Sub-nav (ActivityTabs)** — Horizontal cluster-tab nav with 5 links (Live, Runs, Tasks, Sessions, Traces) using shared .cluster-tabs / .cluster-tab primitives; active underline via ::after pseudo-element; aria-label='Activity section' on nav, aria-current='page' on active link.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The ActivityTabs nav aria-label 'Activity section' is generic and duplicates what the visible tab labels already say — screen readers announce 'navigation Activity section' with no useful context about sibling pages.
  - *Fix:* Change aria-label to 'Cluster navigation' or 'Section navigation' (matching the pattern used on /runs and /traces) so it is consistent and distinguishable if multiple navs appear on the same page.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The cluster-tab active indicator uses var(--accent) (orange) per CSS, but the page-level filter tabs use var(--accent-cool) (blue) for their active underline — two different active-state colors on the same page undermine the indicator convention.
  - *Fix:* Align the page-level filter tabs (lines 612–617 in page.tsx) to also use var(--accent) for their borderBottom, or explicitly document and enforce the split-color pattern in styleguide.md so it is intentional.

**Page Header (.page-head)** — Flex row: left side has the h1 with serif italic accent span ('every tool, every event, in real time.'), a subtitle line counting events/errors, a RelationStrip linking to /approvals; right side has a Pause/Resume button and LivePill.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The .editorial-h1 .accent tagline ('every tool, every event, in real time.') renders as serif italic --ink-2 text appended inline to the h1. This buries the page title ('Activity') inside a decorative phrase, reducing scannability — the functional signal is lost after the em-dash.
  - *Fix:* Remove the <span className='accent'> from the h1 and move the tagline into the .editorial-sub slot below, or drop it entirely; the LivePill and stream status already communicate liveness. The h1 should be just 'Activity' or 'Live Activity'.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The subtitle 'N events · last 24h · N errored' only renders when events.length > 0. During the seeded-but-empty state it is absent, leaving a visual gap below the h1 and a layout shift when events arrive.
  - *Fix:* Render the subtitle unconditionally with placeholder text ('Waiting for events…') when seeded and events are empty, so the layout is stable and does not shift on first event.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** The Pause button aria-pressed reflects paused state correctly but has no visible label change animation or visual differentiation beyond the text toggle — easy to miss that streaming is halted, especially when the user has scrolled down.
  - *Fix:* Add a persistent .alert-warn banner or a sticky top strip (like the existing paused banner below) only when paused=true and scroll position > 200px, using position: sticky at top: 0. The button alone is not enough affordance for a state that silently drops events.

**HintCard** — HintCard.Toggle icon sits inline with the h1 via a flex row; HintCard renders immediately below the .page-head. Collapses when dismissed.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** HintCard.Toggle is nested inside the h1 flex row (line 423), making the toggle part of the heading landmark — screen readers will announce the toggle as part of the heading text.
  - *Fix:* Move HintCard.Toggle outside the <h1> element and place it as a sibling in the flex container at the .page-head level, matching the pattern used on other pages (e.g. /runs) where the toggle is outside heading flow.

**Filter Banners (tool / session active filters)** — Two identical inline-styled div banners appear below HintCard when ?tool= or ?session= query params are set. Each has label text, a <code> value, and a 'Clear' ghost button. Inline styles use var(--bg-2), var(--line-2), var(--r-2).

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Both filter banners use var(--r-2) (a non-canonical alias equal to 6px = var(--r-s)) instead of var(--r-m) used across all other similar notification/filter surfaces (alert-warn, StreamStatusBanner uses var(--radius)). Visual inconsistency in corner radius.
  - *Fix:* Replace borderRadius: 'var(--r-2)' with 'var(--r-m)' in both filter banner divs (lines 488 and 510).
- ⚪ **[low/S]** Both filter banner blocks are identically structured inline-styled divs with duplicated style objects — the same pattern appears twice in JSX with no shared component.
  - *Fix:* Extract a small <ActiveFilterBanner label='Filtering by tool:' value={toolFromUrl} onClear={clearToolFilter} /> component (or reuse a generic token-chip pattern) so the two banners share one source and one style definition.

**RecentHaltsPanel** — Rendered unconditionally between filter banners and the charts row. Collapses to nothing when there are zero halts. Provides halt summary matching the sidebar badge promise.
