- ⚪ **[low/S]** When halt data is loading, the panel likely renders a brief empty/loading flash between the filter banners and the charts row that causes a layout shift before settling.
  - *Fix:* Confirm RecentHaltsPanel uses SkeletonList or a fixed-height skeleton during its loading state; if not, add a min-height: 0 guard or a conditional render behind a seeded flag so the layout does not shift on initial paint.

**Charts Row (EventsHistogram + HBarList)** — Two-pane grid (.two-pane-340-rev) collapses to single column at ≤768px. Left pane: EventsHistogram labeled 'Events / minute (last 24h)' at --fs-2xs mono. Right pane: HBarList labeled 'Top tools' at same style. Labels use --ink-3 (faintest text).

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Card labels 'Events / minute (last 24h)' and 'Top tools' are rendered at var(--fs-2xs) = 10px in var(--ink-3) color — below the 4.5:1 AA contrast threshold for small text. At 10px these are unlikely to meet WCAG 2.1 AA.
  - *Fix:* Bump label font-size to var(--fs-xs) = 11px and color to var(--ink-2) for both chart card headers, matching the .act-th pattern used in the table.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The right pane card wraps HBarList in an unconditional render (the JSX has a bare `{ (` with no condition — line 551) but always shows, even when events is empty and stats.topTools is []. The empty chart pane shows a blank card with only a 10px label.
  - *Fix:* Conditionally render the HBarList card: hide it (or replace with a brief 'No tool calls yet' note) when stats.topTools.length === 0, matching the pattern used for the EmptyState below the table.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The .card class applies a translateY(-1px) + border-color hover on both chart cards, implying interactivity. Neither chart card is clickable. Decorative hover lift misleads users.
  - *Fix:* Add pointer-events: none or override the hover transform/border on these non-interactive .card instances (e.g. add a .card--static modifier class), or replace with a flat card that does not have the hover transition.

**Event Type Filter Tabs** — Four toggle buttons (All, Tool calls, Recipe starts, Recipe ends) in a role='group', styled with inline styles using var(--accent-cool) for active state, borderBottom underline, and count badge in --font-mono. Not using the shared cluster-tab primitives.

- 🟡 **[med/M]** These filter tabs are fully custom-styled inline buttons duplicating the visual tab pattern — color, border-bottom underline, font-size, active state — rather than reusing the existing .cluster-tab / .cluster-tabs primitive. Two separate tab conventions exist on one page (cluster-tabs at top, act-tab-btn here).
  - *Fix:* Refactor to use .cluster-tabs + .cluster-tab styling with aria-pressed (or aria-selected with role='tab') rather than the inline style object. The count badge can be a .cluster-tab-badge span matching the established pattern.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** .act-th::after adds a '↕' sort indicator to all column headers but sorting is not implemented (the title attribute says 'not sortable yet'). Users who click column headers expecting sort will get no feedback.
  - *Fix:* Remove the ::after content: ' ↕' from .act-th in globals.css until sort is implemented, and remove the cursor: default to make it clear headers are not interactive. Alternatively add role='columnheader' aria-sort='none' if sort is imminent.

**Stream Status Banner (StreamStatusBanner)** — Inline-styled banner with animated dot, colored by connection state (ok/warn/err). Appears below filter tabs only when err is set AND connection !== 'live'. Uses role='status' and aria-live='polite'.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The StreamStatusBanner uses var(--radius) (10px) for borderRadius — a legacy token alias — while the nearby filter banners use var(--r-2) and alert-warn uses var(--r-m). Three different radius references for equivalent surface types.
  - *Fix:* Standardize to var(--r-m) for all notification/banner surfaces; replace var(--radius) in the bannerStyle object with var(--r-m).

**Paused State Banner** — When paused=true, an .alert-warn div renders above the table with 'Paused — N events buffered' and a Resume button. A duplicate Resume button also exists in the .page-head.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** There are two separate Resume button implementations: one in .page-head (lines 444–471) and one inside the .alert-warn banner (lines 651–671). They share identical flush-and-unpause logic duplicated verbatim. Users also see two Resume affordances simultaneously.
  - *Fix:* Remove the Resume button from inside the .alert-warn banner; the .page-head button (which is always visible) is sufficient. The .alert-warn should be informational only ('Paused — N events buffered. Resume above.') with no second action button.

**Loading State (ActivitySkeletonRows)** — Custom ActivitySkeletonRows renders 6 shimmer rows in a flex layout below the table header while seeded=false. Uses locally-defined .act-skeleton-row and .act-skeleton-cell CSS rather than the shared Skeleton/SkeletonList primitives.

- ⚪ **[low/M]** ActivitySkeletonRows is a local re-implementation of the shimmer skeleton pattern rather than the shared Skeleton/SkeletonList primitive. Diverging animation timing (1.4s linear infinite vs whatever the shared primitive uses) and row structure make the loading state look slightly different from other pages.
  - *Fix:* Replace ActivitySkeletonRows with the shared SkeletonList primitive (or compose Skeleton cells inside the table rows), so the shimmer animation and visual weight are consistent with /runs and /sessions loading states.

**Empty State** — Uses shared EmptyState primitive with 'No activity yet' title and a two-part description. A second EmptyState for 'No events match this filter' includes an action button 'Show all events'. Both cover seeded-and-empty and filtered-to-empty cases correctly.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The first EmptyState description embeds a <span> with display:block and inline styles (color, font-size, marginTop) as a second paragraph inside the description prop. This internal span is not part of the EmptyState component's design contract and will not respect future EmptyState style changes.
  - *Fix:* Pass two separate strings or a structured subtitle to EmptyState (if the primitive supports it) or extract the second line into the EmptyState action slot. Remove the inline-styled span from the description.

**Event Table** — Full-width .table with 5 columns (Time, Kind, Tool/Event, Duration, Status/Decision). Rows use .activity-table-row class for fresh-flash animation; entity chips (ToolChip, ApprovalChip, SessionChip, RecipeChip) render in the Tool/Event cell; Status column uses custom .status-cell with .pill-dot.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The table has no caption or aria-label, so screen readers announce it as an anonymous table. The thead does not have scope='col' on any th elements.
  - *Fix:* Add <caption className='sr-only'>Live activity events</caption> as the first child of <table>, and add scope='col' to each <th> in the thead.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Row keys use `${e.kind}-${e.id ?? i}-${i}` — the index i is always included as a suffix, making every key unique even for duplicates, which defeats React's reconciliation and causes all rows to re-render on every tick (5s interval) instead of only new rows.
  - *Fix:* Key each row as `${e.kind}-${e.id ?? e.at ?? i}` without appending i as a suffix when e.id is defined; the dedup logic upstream already ensures no two displayed rows share id+kind.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Duration cell uses durationCell = meta.summary when no durationMs is present. Summaries can be full sentences ('Committed 3 files to main') that overflow the 100px-wide column, getting clipped with no title attribute to reveal the full text.
  - *Fix:* Add title={typeof durationCell === 'string' ? durationCell : undefined} to the Duration <td> so the full text is accessible on hover, or truncate with text-overflow: ellipsis and an explicit title.

**Activity Ticker (topbar component)** — Compact topbar ticker (ActivityTicker.tsx) shows 3 most-recent events as clickable mono links with a live/offline dot. Dismiss button (✕) writes to localStorage. Uses useBridgeStream, aria-live='off'. The ✕ dismiss button is a raw × character.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The dismiss button uses the literal '✕' Unicode character as its visible label (line 256). This is a decorative character, not a standard × (×), and renders inconsistently across fonts. There is no focus ring defined in activity-ticker-close beyond the browser default.
  - *Fix:* Replace '✕' with '×' (HTML entity &times;) or an SVG icon matching the existing close/dismiss icon used elsewhere in the dashboard, and verify the .activity-ticker-close focus style provides a visible focus ring at ≥3:1 contrast.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** Ticker event links point to /activity?focus=<id> but there is no focus= query param handler in page.tsx — the link navigates to /activity but the focused row is never highlighted or scrolled into view.
  - *Fix:* Either implement the focus= param handler in page.tsx (scroll and briefly highlight the matching row) or change the href to /activity without the focus param until the feature is wired, to avoid the dead-link false affordance.


### Tasks  `/tasks`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace `Suspense fallback={null}` with `fallback={<SkeletonList rows={3} columns={3} />}` to eliminate the blank-page flash on initial load — highest user-facing visibility since every page visit is affected.
2. Remove the redundant status pill from each task row (status is already shown via left-border colour, timeline dot, and in the detail pane) to reduce visual noise and recover horizontal space, especially on narrow viewports where the pill crowds the driver badge and duration.
3. Replace the inline unstyled 'Select a task to see its output.' placeholder with a card-wrapped empty treatment (or minimal EmptyState) to prevent the right pane from collapsing and causing layout shift when no task is selected.

**Page Header** — editorial-h1 with accent tagline, subtitle shows live stats (count/avg/driver), RelationStrip to Approvals, plus a redundant 'N total' pill and a 'Sync' ghost button

- 🟡 **[med/S]** 'N total' pill duplicates the task count already in the h1 subtitle. Two separate count displays within 40px of each other.
  - *Fix:* Remove the `<span className='pill muted'>{tasks.length} total</span>` on the right side. The count is fully represented in the subtitle line.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The editorial-h1 tagline 'Claude subprocess invocations.' uses a decorative serif accent for a definition that buries the primary signal. Users scanning fast see the word Tasks but must parse a clause to understand the count.
  - *Fix:* Move the live stat line (N tasks · avg X · driver: Y) INTO the h1 or elevate it visually. Keep the tagline as a subtitle-only element in muted ink-2, not as an accented h1 fragment.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** 'Sync' button has no aria-label and no loading/spinner state — a user who clicks it during an in-flight poll gets no feedback.
  - *Fix:* Add `aria-label='Refresh task list'` and briefly disable + show a mini spinner on click, consistent with how other pages handle manual refresh (e.g. /runs).

**Activity Tab Nav** — ActivityTabs component rendered at the top of the section, shared with /runs and /sessions

- ⚪ **[low/S]** ActivityTabs is rendered inside `<section>` before the page-head div, meaning the tab bar visually precedes the page title. On /runs and /sessions the tab sits above the h1 too, but here the h1's editorial-sub stats row makes the nav feel displaced from the content it's navigating.
  - *Fix:* No structural change needed — this is consistent with sibling pages. But confirm ActivityTabs has an `aria-label` on its nav element ('Activity sections' or similar) so screen readers don't announce an unlabeled navigation landmark.

**Filter Bar** — Search input + All/Live/Done/Failed toggle buttons + filtered count span, conditionally rendered only when tasks.length > 0

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Filter bar is hidden when tasks.length === 0 but visible during the loading skeleton phase because the skeleton branch only fires when `!hasLoaded`. A user who briefly has 0 tasks mid-session sees the skeleton, then the EmptyState, with no filter bar ever shown — fine. But if tasks exist and then the bridge returns an empty list on a stale poll, the filter bar disappears without warning.
  - *Fix:* Decouple filter-bar visibility from `tasks.length` — show it whenever `hasLoaded` is true and `err` is falsy. This prevents jarring hide/show during brief poll gaps.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Failed' filter label maps to error + interrupted + cancelled statuses, but the pill inside the filter button shows just a count with no semantic colour — pressing 'Failed' with N > 0 gives no pre-click visual urgency.
  - *Fix:* Apply `color: var(--err)` to the count span inside the 'Failed' button when `statusCounts.error > 0`, matching the err pill colour used on the row badges. Keep the button itself ghost until pressed.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Filtered result count `N of M` uses `var(--ink-3)` (faintest text token) and `var(--fs-s)`. At small sizes this will fail WCAG AA contrast against the page background in both themes.
  - *Fix:* Bump to `var(--ink-2)` for the filtered-count readout, or wrap in a `<span className='pill muted'>` for consistent legibility with the same styling used elsewhere for counts.

**Task List (Timeline Rail)** — Vertical timeline with a gradient line, staggered-animation rows as <button> elements with left-border colour coding, inline mini progress bar, DriverBadge, status pill, first output line preview, duration

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Each row carries three distinct visual indicators for status: (1) left border colour, (2) timeline dot colour, (3) status pill. This is triple-redundant. On small viewports the pill and border overlap visually but the dot is hidden by the 44px paddingLeft, making the dot useful only at desktop widths.
  - *Fix:* Drop the status pill from the row (keep it in the detail pane header where it's already present). The left-border colour + timeline dot colour already fully communicate status at a glance. Removing the pill saves ~20px of horizontal space per row.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 32px mini progress-bar (`tasks-progress-bar-track`) represents duration intensity (0–35s mapped to full) but has no accessible label and communicates no discrete value. A 3px bar that maps to an arbitrary 35s ceiling is uninformative to non-visual users and confusing to sighted users who don't know the scale.
  - *Fix:* Replace the intensity bar with nothing for terminal tasks (duration is already shown as text). Keep the indeterminate animation only for live tasks as a loading indicator. Remove the `intensity`/`durSec` computation from row rendering.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The `visibleCount` 'Show N more (M hidden)' button is a plain ghost btn with no role hinting. When searching, resetting visibleCount in the useEffect is correct but the button disappears and reappears without any announcement to screen readers.
  - *Fix:* Add `aria-live='polite'` on a visually-hidden element that announces 'Showing N of M tasks' when visibleCount changes. This is a single-line addition and costs nothing visually.

**Task Row — Inline Output Preview** — First line of task.output (up to 80 chars) shown in monospace font-s with 2-line WebkitLineClamp; falls back to '(running…)' in ink-3

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The first output line preview uses `fontFamily: var(--font-mono)` inline — a duplicated style that bypasses the `.mono` utility class. If the mono token ever changes, this row is the one instance that requires a code hunt.
  - *Fix:* Replace `fontFamily: 'var(--font-mono)'` with `className='mono'` on the preview div, matching the task ID span above it.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** When there is no output and the task is not live, the preview slot renders empty (the `(running…)` fallback only fires when isLive is falsy but output is also falsy — but cancelled/error tasks may have no output and no errorMessage, leaving a blank second line).
  - *Fix:* Add a fallback string for terminal-no-output states: `t.status === 'cancelled' ? '(cancelled)' : t.status === 'error' ? '(no error message)' : '(no output)'` so the row height stays consistent and the state is self-describing.

**Detail Pane** — Right column (sticky-pane class) showing TaskDetail card with status pill, truncated task ID, duration, model, output pre block, files-referenced pills, and action buttons (terminal copy, copy ID, cancel)

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'No task selected' placeholder (`Select a task to see its output.`) is a bare unstyled div with inline padding and ink-3 colour — it doesn't use the shared EmptyState primitive and looks visually disconnected from the card shell that surrounds task details.
  - *Fix:* Wrap in `<div className='card'>` matching the TaskDetail wrapper, or use a minimal `EmptyState` with no action and an icon. This keeps the pane height stable and avoids layout shift when switching between selected/unselected states.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The '> Open in terminal' copy button uses a text prefix `> ` as a pseudo-icon. The emoji 📋 on the 'Copy id' button is wrapped in `aria-hidden` which is correct, but the `> ` prefix on the terminal button is not hidden — screen readers will announce 'greater-than sign Open in terminal'.
  - *Fix:* Replace `> ` text with an `aria-hidden` span or a proper icon. If no icon system is available, simply omit the prefix — the button label is clear without it.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** The output `<pre>` block has `aria-live='polite'` + `aria-atomic='false'` on running tasks, which is correct for streaming output. But when the task transitions from running to done, the aria-live attribute is removed on next render without announcing completion. A screen reader user monitoring a running task gets streaming updates then silence.
  - *Fix:* On transition to terminal status, append a visually-hidden `aria-live='assertive'` announcement ('Task complete — status: done') via a separate span outside the pre. This is already the pattern used in the Toast component.

**Error / Loading / Empty States** — ErrorState component for zero-task bridge failure; inline alert-err div for poll failures when tasks already loaded; SkeletonList(3,3) during initial load; EmptyState with CTA for zero tasks after load

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The `Suspense fallback={null}` at the page root means users see a blank page flash before TasksContent mounts. The SkeletonList inside TasksContent only appears after the Suspense resolves and hasLoaded is false — so there's a brief null render.
  - *Fix:* Replace `fallback={null}` with `fallback={<SkeletonList rows={3} columns={3} />}`. This eliminates the blank-page flash and is the pattern used on other pages.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The inline `alert-err` div for poll failures (when tasks already exist) uses a raw class string with no close/dismiss affordance. A transient network hiccup leaves a permanent error banner above the task list until the next successful poll.
  - *Fix:* Add an onDismiss handler or auto-clear the `err` state when `tasks.length > 0` on the next successful fetch tick. Alternatively use the Toast system already imported — a transient error toast is less disruptive than a persistent banner.


### Sessions  `/sessions`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the hand-rolled chip + sess-live-dot in each session card with the existing LivePill primitive (removes duplicate behavior, dead CSS, and brings aria-live consistency) — session card lines 291-307 and sess-live-dot CSS block.
2. Add aria-expanded={isSelected} + aria-controls='session-panel' to the role=button card div, and id='session-panel' to the sticky-pane container — the expand/collapse interaction is currently invisible to assistive technology.
3. Replace <a href> with <Link href> in SessionSummaryPanel's 'Open detail →' button (line 84) to restore client-side navigation and prevent a full page reload on every detail click.

**Sub-nav (ActivityTabs)** — Shared cluster-tab nav renders above the page header; 'Sessions' tab is active.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** No aria-label on the outer <section> element, so screen readers announce nothing when landing on this page — the ActivityTabs nav provides the only labeled region.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label="Sessions" (or aria-labelledby pointing at the h1) to the root <section> at line 148 of page.tsx.

**Page header (page-head / editorial-h1)** — Large serif-italic tagline 'see what your agents are doing right now.' sits beside the live/idle counts and a RelationStrip.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The '.accent' span renders as faint serif italic (--ink-2, per the CSS comment at line 2374) — the tagline is decorative copy that buries the actionable subtitle ('N live · N idle'), which is the real signal users need first.
  - *Fix:* Remove the .accent tagline span entirely from the h1 and promote 'N live · N idle' into a .editorial-sub span with a .num span for the live count so the live count renders in --orange and draws the eye first.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'editorial-sub' count ('N live · N idle') uses a plain string with no live-region, so a polling update (every 3s) is silently dropped for screen reader users.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the count span with aria-live="polite" aria-atomic="true" so count changes are announced on updates.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** RelationStrip is placed below the live/idle count but above the card list, creating a visual gap that breaks the flow between the h1 group and the content body.
  - *Fix:* Move RelationStrip to the right side of the .page-head flex row (it already has a flex justify-content: space-between container) so it sits flush right at the same vertical level as the h1 group.

**Error state (inline alert-err / ErrorState)** — Two distinct error paths: ErrorState component when sessions is empty, and a bare .alert-err div when sessions are already loaded; both can co-exist.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The .alert-err div at line 182 renders the raw error string directly ('Refresh failed — {error}') with no icon, no dismiss, and no retry action — inconsistent with the full ErrorState used on the empty path.
  - *Fix:* Replace the .alert-err div with a Toast (useToast().show) on polling failure so it doesn't permanently occupy layout space and matches the shared pattern used elsewhere. Keep ErrorState for the initial empty load only.

**Loading state** — <SkeletonList rows={4} columns={3} /> shown on initial load before any sessions arrive.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** SkeletonList renders a table-style skeleton (rows × columns) but the actual sessions UI is a card list with a two-pane layout — the skeleton shape does not match what will replace it, causing a jarring layout shift.
  - *Fix:* Replace SkeletonList with 4 hand-rolled skeleton cards using the same 'glass-card' + 'sess-card' classes and approximate height (~110px each) so the skeleton layout matches the loaded state.

**Empty state** — EmptyState component shown when no sessions and no error; includes a docs link styled with --info color and a Refresh button.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The description is 4 sentences long and leads with an explanation of what sessions are before saying 'No agents are currently connected.' — the key fact is buried last.
  - *Fix:* Reorder: lead with 'No agents are connected to the bridge right now.' then one sentence of context, then the docs link. Cut the explanation of tool call history — that is visible once connected.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The docs link uses style={{ color: 'var(--info)' }} (inline) while all other link colors in the codebase use semantic CSS classes — inconsistent and overrides theme switching for the link color.
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline style; wrap in <a className="link"> or rely on the global a[href] color rule so it respects theme tokens.

**Session card list (left pane)** — Vertical stack of glass-card + sess-card divs with role=button; each shows an ID prefix, activity chip, first-tool ToolChip, 3-stat metrics row, and a footer timestamp.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The activity status chip is a hand-rolled .chip + conditionally chip-accent/chip-amber/chip-muted with an inline sess-live-dot, duplicating the exact visual and behavior already provided by the LivePill primitive (which has connection presets, aria-live, dot-live animation, and themed tone classes).
  - *Fix:* Replace the chip + sess-live-dot combination at lines 291-307 with <LivePill label={act.label} tone={act.label === 'live' ? 'ok' : act.label === 'recent' ? 'accent' : 'muted'} /> and remove the .sess-live-dot CSS + its keyframe (it becomes dead code).
- 🔴 **[high/S]** The card expands an inline detail panel (right pane) when clicked, but the role=button div has no aria-expanded attribute, so assistive technology cannot determine whether the card is collapsed or expanded.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-expanded={isSelected} and aria-controls pointing to the panel id (e.g. 'session-panel') to the div at line 238; add id="session-panel" to the sticky-pane div.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Files' metric cell in the metrics row (lines 369-394) links to /sessions/[id] (the full detail page) rather than to any file-specific view — the link destination is inconsistent with the label and misleading: clicking 'Files' navigates to the session detail, same as clicking the card header's 'Open detail' button.
  - *Fix:* Either remove the Link wrapper from the Files cell and make it non-interactive (it is already visible in the detail panel), or link it to /activity?session=...&type=file if a file-filter exists.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The metrics row stat values use --fs-stat (17px) but the labels use --fs-2xs (10px) — an 8px gap in a 8px vertical space looks cramped and the labels are at the boundary of legibility, especially at --ink-2.
  - *Fix:* Bump stat labels from --fs-2xs to --fs-xs (11px) and increase marginTop from 3 to 4px for breathing room; this matches the sizing used in StatCard-style patterns elsewhere.

**Detail / log panel (right pane — SessionSummaryPanel)** — Sticky card with mono key-value grid showing 8-9 session fields; header shows a 'Open detail →' ghost button; footer has a static hint about the event stream.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** 'Open detail →' at line 84-91 uses an <a href> (hard navigate) rather than Next.js <Link href> — breaks client-side routing, causes a full page reload on click.
  - *Fix:* Replace the <a href> with <Link href={`/sessions/${encodeURIComponent(session.id)}`} className='btn sm ghost'>.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The footer hint 'Live event stream available on the session detail page.' at line 111 is always visible regardless of whether the detail page is actually reachable — it reads as filler copy at --fs-xs / --ink-3 and competes visually with the data rows.
  - *Fix:* Remove the footer hint entirely; the 'Open detail →' button already communicates that more is available on the detail page.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The right-pane placeholder when no card is selected ('Select a session to see its log.' at line 462) sits as a centered faint string with no visual container, creating an invisible dead zone in the right column on desktop.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the placeholder in a glass-card or .card with padding and border (matching the panel when populated) and add an icon or subtle icon from the existing icon set so the pane is visually distinguished from blank space.


### Session detail  `/sessions/[id]`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the four hand-rolled stat cells with StatCard primitives (including href on the pending-approvals card) — eliminates 80+ lines of duplicated inline styles and gives the top of the page proper visual hierarchy with clickable stat cards
2. Use ErrorState and EmptyState shared primitives for all three branches (API error, 404, activity-empty) — they add role=alert, icon, action slot, and animation that the current raw divs lack
3. Fix the decisions card rows — they all link to the generic /decisions list rather than the individual decision, making every row a dead-end navigation link that confuses intent and breaks user trust in the cross-links

**Header / page-head** — BackLink + editorial-h1 wrapping an 8-char code truncation + full UUID subtitle in --font-mono, RelationStrip cross-links, and conditional pills (open-file count + pending-approvals badge) floated right

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The full UUID is repeated twice: once truncated in the h1 and again verbatim in page-head-sub. The h1 truncation adds noise without adding information — the subtitle already shows the full id on hover via title attribute.
  - *Fix:* Remove the editorial-h1 <code>{id.slice(0,8)}</code> and make the page-head-sub the primary title. Apply font-mono + ink-0 weight 600 directly to it. Saves a redundant DOM node and one visual level of hierarchy.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'open' pill in the header (summary.openedFileCount open) duplicates the stat card below and provides no action target. It uses className='pill muted' while the stat card shows the same number in a larger --fs-stat slot.
  - *Fix:* Remove the muted pill from the header. The stat card row already surfaces this value at better visibility. Only keep the 'pending' err-pill (it links to /approvals so it has navigation value).
- ⚪ **[low/S]** RelationStrip includes 'All sessions' — a generic back-link already provided by BackLink above it, creating redundant navigation in a strip meant for cross-entity context links.
  - *Fix:* Remove the 'All sessions' item from the RelationStrip items array. Four cross-links becomes three and the strip reads more purposefully.

**Error / loading / 404 states** — Three separate inline divs: a raw .alert-err string for API/validation errors, a SkeletonList for loading, and a hand-rolled .empty-state div for 404 — none use the shared ErrorState or EmptyState primitives

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The error branch renders a raw .alert-err div with a brittle prefix-check string (error.startsWith('/sessions/:id')). The shared ErrorState component handles layout, icon, detail monospace block, and role='alert' automatically.
  - *Fix:* Replace the .alert-err div with <ErrorState error={error} title='Could not load session' description={error.startsWith('/sessions/:id') ? 'Bridge version mismatch — response shape unexpected.' : undefined} /> imported from @/components/patchwork.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 404 empty state is a hand-rolled div with raw h3 + p, missing the .empty-state animation, icon slot, and action link back to /sessions.
  - *Fix:* Replace with <EmptyState title='Session not found' description='No active session with this id. It may have disconnected.' action={<Link href="/sessions" className="btn sm">Back to sessions</Link>} /> from the shared primitive.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The loading skeleton uses SkeletonList rows=6 columns=4 — appropriate for a table but the first thing the page shows is a stat card row, not a table. The skeleton misleads the user about what is loading.
  - *Fix:* Replace SkeletonList with a SkeletonStatCard row (4 instances) followed by a SkeletonList rows=8 columns=3 to match the stat card + event-stream layout that actually appears on load.

**Stat card row (Connected / Open files / Pending approvals / Events logged)** — A bespoke .card with a CSS grid of four manually styled divs — each with its own inline fontSize/color/fontWeight/marginBottom declarations — approximating what StatCard already provides

- 🔴 **[high/M]** All four stat cells repeat identical inline style objects (fs-2xs label, ink-2, fontWeight 500, marginBottom 4 / fs-stat value, font-mono, fontWeight 700). This is exactly the StatCard + GlassCard primitive's responsibility, duplicated four times.
  - *Fix:* Replace the entire bespoke grid card with four <StatCard> components in a stat-cards grid div. Pass label, value (using AnimatedNumber for the numeric ones), and for pending-approvals pass href={`/approvals?session=${id}`} so the card itself becomes the action link.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Events logged' stat counts stream.length (the post-filter list) rather than total lifecycle+tools length, so toggling 'Hide noise' changes the headline stat without any explanation to the user.
  - *Fix:* Count total events before the hideNoise filter (use lifecycle.length + tools.length) and label the stat 'Total events'. The filtered view count can appear as a footer note inside the StatCard foot prop if desired.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Connected' cell shows relTime which is ambiguous for long-running sessions (e.g. '3 hours ago'). The title tooltip is the only way to get the absolute timestamp but requires hover — inaccessible on mobile/touch.
  - *Fix:* Add a <time datetime={summary.connectedAt}> wrapping the relTime display, and optionally expose the absolute timestamp as a visible secondary line using the StatCard foot prop.

**Pending approvals card** — Conditional card rendered only when approvals.length > 0; each row is a Link styled inline with flex, a tier pill, a truncated tool name (sd-approval-tool), a summary span, and a relTime — no aria-label on the link

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Each approval Link has no accessible label — screen readers announce the concatenated child text as a run-on string (e.g. 'high searchWorkspaceSymbols Read file 2 min ago'), which is confusing with no verb.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label={`Approve ${a.toolName} (${a.tier} tier) — ${a.summary ?? 'no summary'}`} to each Link element.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The card uses inline style background='var(--bg-0)' and border='1px solid var(--border-subtle)' on each row, but --border-subtle is a low-specificity alias that maps to --line-1 only in some themes. Other similar row patterns on the page (decisions card) use the same non-standard token.
  - *Fix:* Replace var(--bg-0) / var(--border-subtle) with var(--recess) / var(--line-1) — the canonical design-token pair used by all other dense-row surfaces in globals.css.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** When approvals exist the stat card already shows the count and the header pill also links to /approvals — three separate surfaces say 'N pending'. The card is the most useful of the three but the others remain.
  - *Fix:* After adding StatCard with href for pending-approvals (see stat card section), remove the redundant header pill. Keep only the dedicated card and the stat card link; that is sufficient entry-point coverage.

**Knowledge saved (decisions) card** — Conditional card shown when decisions.length > 0; rows link to the generic /decisions page (not to the specific decision), show ref in --purple mono, solution text truncated, tags in ink-3 mono, and relTime

- 🔴 **[high/S]** Every decision row links to /decisions (the list page) regardless of which decision was clicked. There is no deep-link to the individual decision by seq/ref, so the link is decorative navigation rather than useful.
  - *Fix:* Change the Link href from '/decisions' to `/decisions?ref=${encodeURIComponent(d.ref)}` (or the appropriate deep-link pattern used by the decisions page). If no per-decision route exists yet, render the row as a non-link div with a copy-ref button instead of a misleading link.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The section heading 'Knowledge saved' is non-standard — the /decisions page and dashboard nav call this 'Decisions'. Inconsistent naming forces users to make a conceptual connection.
  - *Fix:* Rename the card h2 from 'Knowledge saved' to 'Decisions saved this session' to align with the established terminology while keeping the session scope clear.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The problem field (d.problem) is not shown — only d.solution and d.ref are visible in the truncated row, so the user cannot tell what was decided without navigating away.
  - *Fix:* Add d.problem as a de-emphasized subtitle line under d.solution (ink-3, fs-s, truncated at one line) so the row gives problem/solution context at a glance.

**Event stream card** — Merged table of lifecycle events and tool calls, sorted newest-first, with a live-pulse dot, event-count pill, and toggle button to show/hide noise events; tool calls get ok/err pills, lifecycle events get muted/ok/err pills based on type

- 🟡 **[med/S]** Tool name in the Event column uses a full-width pill (className='pill ok/err'), causing long tool names like searchWorkspaceSymbols or batchFindImplementations to overflow the fixed 160px column width and push into the Detail column on narrow viewports.
  - *Fix:* Add .pill.xs className to tool pills in the stream table, or apply max-width: 150px; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis on the pill span. The sd-approval-tool pattern (max-width + ellipsis) already solves this for the approval card — apply the same treatment here.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** The 'live' label and animated dot (sd-live-dot) are shown unconditionally regardless of whether data is actually updating. If the session is disconnected and polling returns stale data, the live indicator misleads the user.
  - *Fix:* Drive live-dot visibility from a freshness signal: show it only when the last fetch was within the polling interval (3000ms). Use a useEffect + Date.now() comparison or derive from the useBridgeFetch response timestamp. Otherwise show a 'stale' pill in ink-3.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** The stream table has no row-count cap or pagination. With a long-running session that generates hundreds of events, the entire table is rendered in DOM at once. There is also no 'load more' affordance, making it unclear whether rows are truncated server-side.
  - *Fix:* Limit initial render to 100 rows and add a 'Show all N events' ghost button below the table if stream.length > 100. This also doubles as an implicit indicator of whether the server is truncating results.

**Activity-empty state (session connected, zero events/approvals/decisions)** — Hand-rolled .empty-state div with h3 'No recorded activity' and a p tag — rendered only when summary exists but all three data arrays are empty

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The empty state text 'hasn't produced any lifecycle events or approvals yet' buries the reassurance ('yet') at the end. The lead sentence should signal status, not process.
  - *Fix:* Change h3 to 'Session active — no events yet' and shorten p to 'Events will appear here as the agent works. Refresh to check for updates.' This leads with the positive status.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The empty state uses the raw .empty-state CSS class but is not rendered via the shared EmptyState primitive, missing the animation, icon slot, and future action-slot upgradability.
  - *Fix:* Replace with <EmptyState title='Session active — no events yet' description='Events will appear here as the agent works.' /> from @/components/patchwork.


### Traces  `/traces`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the filtered-empty EmptyState — 'No decisions recorded yet' shows even when filters are active; add a filter-aware branch ('No matching traces · clear filters') so users understand why the list is empty instead of thinking they have no data.
2. Fix the traces-recipe-col dual-action conflict in flat view rows — the recipe name button (expand trigger) stacks over the RecipeChip navigation link, creating two overlapping click targets with different behaviors; separate expand to the chevron only and make the name purely navigational.
3. Tree view root rows are missing the copy-trace-id button and RecipeChip/ApprovalChip entity links that flat view exposes — users switching to tree view lose all quick-action affordances; mirror the flat-view column set onto traces-root-grid.

**Page Header / Hero** — h1 with editorial-h1 class + italic em tagline, sub-line shows trace counts + LivePill, RelationStrip cross-links below, toolbar (search, By meaning, Export) floated right in same page-head div

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The h1 reads 'Traces — recipe runs and their decision logs.' — the serif em tagline buries the data signal. Users land here to scan runs, not read prose; the tagline competes with the count sub-line directly below it.
  - *Fix:* Drop the em tagline from the h1. Move it into the traces-sub line as a tooltip or HintCard body. h1 becomes just 'Traces' — counts and LivePill carry the context.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** traces-sub count string ('N traces · N done · N errors · last 24h') uses faint editorial-sub styling. After a filter is active the count reflects the filtered set but the 'last 24h' label always shows the since-bucket, not the active filter — misleading when statusFilter is 'errors'.
  - *Fix:* Append the active statusFilter label to the count string when not 'all': '3 errors · last 24h'. Use --ink-1 weight instead of --ink-3 for the counts so they read at a glance.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** toolbar div uses inline style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:8, flexWrap:'wrap' }} rather than a utility class — inconsistent with the design system and breaks on the paper theme if gap tokens differ.
  - *Fix:* Replace inline style with a utility class like 'row gap-2 flex-wrap' (or the project's equivalent). Align with how other page toolbars are structured.

**HintCard** — HintCard.Toggle in the title row, HintCard rendered below the page-head — collapsed by default, content unknown from this file

- ⚪ **[low/S]** HintCard sits between the page header and the recipe-filter banner, which itself sits above the filter bar — three stacked meta-strips before any data. When HintCard is expanded it pushes all content down with no visual anchor.
  - *Fix:* Move HintCard.Toggle into the toolbar row (next to Export), so toggling it doesn't shift the filter bar. Or collapse it into the header sub-line as a '?' icon with a Popover rather than a full-width card.

**Recipe Filter Banner** — Conditional div.traces-recipe-filter showing 'Filtered by recipe: <name>' with a Clear button — appears between HintCard and the filter bar when a ?recipe= deep-link is active

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The banner uses plain span.mono for the recipe name but doesn't use the RecipeChip entity primitive, which exists precisely for this pattern and renders with the correct color/icon.
  - *Fix:* Replace the span.mono + text with <RecipeChip name={recipeFilter} variant='chip' /> inside the banner, matching how the flat-view rows render recipe names.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** 'Filtered by recipe:' banner has no visible close-icon affordance — the 'Clear' text button is the only dismiss. On mobile the label + name + button wrap to multiple lines before Clear is reachable.
  - *Fix:* Add an X icon inside the 'Clear' btn (aria-label='Clear recipe filter') and truncate the recipe name with text-overflow:ellipsis + max-width so the banner stays single-line.

**Filter Bar** — Three groups in one div.traces-filter-bar: status pills (All/Done/Errors/Kill-switch), a since-label + native select, and View toggle (flat/tree) — all on one horizontal row

- 🟡 **[med/M]** Status filter pills (All/Done/Errors) and View pills (flat/tree) are rendered with identical className logic but semantically different roles — status is a filter, view is a layout toggle. They look the same, causing users to treat them as equivalent controls.
  - *Fix:* Give the View toggle a visually distinct treatment: use role='group' with an aria-label='View mode', and style with a segmented-control appearance (border around the pair, selected fills solid) vs the pill chips used for filters.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Kill-switch' pill is visually indistinguishable from 'All/Done/Errors' pills in inactive state (all pill muted). Its toggle behavior (on/off) differs from the status pills (radio). Users may not realize it stacks with other filters.
  - *Fix:* Style the kill-switch pill with a distinct icon prefix (e.g. a lock or warning glyph) and use pill warn (yellow) when active rather than pill info (blue), to signal it is an additive filter, not a radio selection.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** Native <select> for since-filter breaks the design token system — it cannot be styled with --line, --bg, --r tokens consistently across light/paper themes and on mobile defaults to OS chrome.
  - *Fix:* Replace with a segmented pill group matching the existing SINCE_OPTIONS labels (1h · 24h · 7d · 30d · All), same as the status pills. Five options fits in one row at desktop; on mobile wrap is acceptable.

**Type-Color Legend** — div.traces-legend with four inline span items showing a color swatch + type label — rendered between filter bar and the list on every page load

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The legend is always visible even when the trace list is empty or loading — it appears above a SkeletonList or EmptyState, which is jarring and takes space for decorative information when there is nothing to decode yet.
  - *Fix:* Conditionally render the legend only when traces.length > 0 (same guard used for the list). Wrap in a short CSS transition (opacity) so it fades in with the list.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Legend items have no role or aria semantics — screen readers see a run of colored spans with no list structure. The aria-label on the container div ('Trace type colors') is correct but the items should be <li> inside a <ul role='list'>.
  - *Fix:* Change .traces-legend to a <ul role='list' aria-label='Trace type colors'> and each item to <li className='traces-legend-item'>.

**Loading State** — <SkeletonList rows={6} columns={4} /> shown only when loading && traces.length === 0 — stale data stays visible during subsequent refreshes with no loading indicator

- 🟡 **[med/S]** On background refresh (3s interval) with existing data, there is no feedback that a refresh is happening or failed — data could be stale and the user has no way to know until an error banner appears.
  - *Fix:* Show a faint LivePill or spinner in the header sub-line during loading when traces.length > 0 (i.e. a background refetch). The LivePill already exists in the header but has no loading state; add a 'refreshing' prop or use the existing isSearching spinner pattern.

**Error States** — Two branches: (1) ErrorState component when error && traces.length === 0; (2) raw div.alert-err string when error && traces.length > 0

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stale-data error branch (traces.length > 0) uses a raw div.alert-err with an unstyled string including the raw error message — inconsistent with the ErrorState component and potentially exposes internal error text to users.
  - *Fix:* Replace div.alert-err with a shared <Banner tone='err'> or a compact inline ErrorState variant. Truncate the raw error string behind a 'Show details' toggle rather than rendering it inline.

**Empty State** — <EmptyState> with 'No decisions recorded yet' title + description + 'Browse recipes' CTA link — shown when visible.length === 0 && !loading

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The EmptyState title says 'No decisions recorded yet' but shows even when the user has applied filters (statusFilter='errors', ksOnly=true) that produced zero results — the copy reads like a first-run state, not a filtered-empty state.
  - *Fix:* Check whether any filter is active (statusFilter !== 'all' || ksOnly || debouncedSearch) and render a different EmptyState: title='No matching traces' + description 'Try clearing the filters or widening the time window.' + a Clear filters action.

**Flat View — Trace List Rows** — div.card.traces-card containing div.traces-row per trace, each with a 7-col traces-row-grid: expand chevron, type icon, key button, recipe col (name + RecipeChip + ApprovalChip), timestamp, status pill, copy button

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The expand/collapse chevron buttons use raw text '>' and 'v' characters instead of SVG icons or CSS triangles. This is visually inconsistent with the rest of the dashboard and reads poorly in screen readers despite the aria-label.
  - *Fix:* Replace '>' / 'v' with a single <svg> chevron rotated via CSS transform: rotate(0deg/90deg) transition, matching the pattern used in other collapsible rows in the codebase.
- 🔴 **[high/M]** The traces-recipe-col renders two interactive elements stacked: a traces-recipe-btn (expand trigger) that also shows the recipe name, AND a separate RecipeChip link. Two click targets with different actions in the same cell creates confusion — users clicking the name to navigate get expansion instead.
  - *Fix:* Separate the expand trigger from the recipe name display. Make the recipe name a non-interactive <span> or use only RecipeChip as the navigate link. Expand should be triggered only by the chevron button and the traces-key-btn (the trace ID).
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The copy-trace-id button has no visible confirmation state — clicking it silently copies with no feedback. The TraceActions bar has a 'Copied ✓' state for CLI copy, but the row-level copy button does not.
  - *Fix:* Add a local copied state to the row (same setTimeout pattern as TraceActions.handleCopyCli). Replace the SVG icon with a checkmark for 1.5s after copy, or show a Toast.

**Flat View — Expanded Detail Panel** — div.traces-detail-panel containing key text, optional summary text, TraceActions bar (Replay / CLI copy), and TraceDetail (scalar grid + collapsible JSON objects)

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The scalar key/value grid (.traces-detail-scalars) colors keys with theme.fg (the type accent color) via inline style, but --ink-3 faint keys would be more readable — the accent color on small 12–13px text may fail WCAG AA contrast especially for the blue and purple variants.
  - *Fix:* Use --ink-2 for key labels in the scalar grid and reserve theme.fg only for the key name in the summary row (where font is larger). Apply the accent color as a left border on the detail panel instead.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** TraceDetail renders plain <pre> blocks for complex/object fields with no max-height or overflow constraint — a large body (e.g. a full LLM response in a decision trace) will push the panel arbitrarily tall and break page rhythm.
  - *Fix:* Add max-height: 300px; overflow-y: auto to .traces-detail-pre, with a subtle scrollbar style matching the design system's --line-2 border.

**Tree View — Span Groups / Waterfall** — Root rows in traces-root-grid (6-col, no copy button), waterfall SpanBar below each root, children revealed inline on expand with traces-child-grid (5-col) and their own SpanBar rows

- 🔴 **[high/M]** Tree view root rows (traces-root-grid) are missing the copy-trace-id button that flat view rows have. Also missing the RecipeChip / ApprovalChip entity links shown in the flat view recipe col — users lose navigation affordances when switching to tree view.
  - *Fix:* Add the copy button and RecipeChip link to the traces-root-grid, mirroring the flat-view traces-row-grid columns. Both views should expose the same set of quick actions.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** The waterfall .traces-span-track gives no time axis labels — users cannot infer absolute duration without reading the traces-duration span. With a 50-item limit, groups can span seconds to minutes and the bar proportions alone are misleading.
  - *Fix:* Add a two-tick axis above the waterfall area (0ms and groupEndMs - groupStartMs label) using a flex row with justified spans. Keep it subtle (--ink-3, 10px, mono font). Only render when groupEndMs > groupStartMs + 10ms.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** Child rows in .traces-child-grid have no expand/detail affordance — the full body of a child trace (e.g. an approval that was part of a recipe run) is inaccessible without switching to flat view.
  - *Fix:* Add a toggle button to each child row that expands an inline TraceDetail panel (same component reuse as root rows and flat-view rows). aria-label='Expand child trace details'.

**Export Panel (popover)** — ExportButton renders a custom popover div.traces-export-panel with password input, Cancel/Download buttons, and an inline CLI hint when passphrase is set — click-outside + Escape closes it

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The export popover is a custom-built popover (div, mousedown listener, ref) rather than the shared Dialog primitive. It has no role='dialog', no aria-modal, and no focus trap — keyboard users tab past it into the page behind.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the panel contents in the shared Dialog component (or at minimum add role='dialog' aria-modal='true' aria-label='Export traces' and call wrapRef.current?.querySelector('input')?.focus() on open). Use the existing Dialog primitive if it supports inline/anchored mode.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The 'Export' button has no aria-label and its aria-haspopup='dialog' is correct, but aria-expanded toggles on the trigger while the panel appears below it with no aria-controls link — screen readers cannot find the controlled region.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-controls='traces-export-panel' to the button and id='traces-export-panel' to the panel div. Ensures AT announces the panel as the expanded region.


### Transactions  `/transactions`

**Top 3:**
1. Remove the per-card repeated 'Commit happens from the agent' helper sentence — it appears once per transaction card and drowns the discard action in repeated boilerplate; move it to the HintCard body once.
2. Add aria-label to each Discard button naming the transaction ID, and add role='alert' (or switch to ErrorState with onRetry) on the stale-data .alert-err banner — both are P0 accessibility gaps.
3. Replace the SkeletonList loading placeholder with skeleton cards that match the actual tx-card layout, eliminating the jarring table-to-card layout shift on data load.

**Page Header** — editorial-h1 with serif italic accent span + HintCard.Toggle inline, editorial-sub with external doc link, RelationStrip below, and a right-side slot holding the count pill + discard-expired button

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The .accent span text ('staged edits, awaiting your nod.') is decorative serif copy that buries the page identity. The h1 reads as 'Transactions — staged edits, awaiting your nod.' before the user sees what the page actually does. CLAUDE.md / globals.css comment at line 2374 explicitly flags these taglines for removal ('P2-8-B removes the spans that no longer earn emphasis').
  - *Fix:* Trim the h1 to just 'Transactions' and move any educational copy down into the editorial-sub or HintCard body. The sub already handles the functional description.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The editorial-sub overrides fontFamily to 'inherit' via inline style (line 188), redundantly fighting the globals rule that already sets --font-sans. More critically, the sub is rendered as a single paragraph that overflows to ellipsis on desktop (white-space: nowrap in .editorial-sub) — the external doc link may be hidden at moderate viewport widths.
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline fontFamily override. Wrap the external doc link in a second line or a HintCard body instead of embedding it in an ellipsis-clipped sub.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The right-side header slot shows a plain 'N active' muted pill but no live-update indicator. The page polls every 3 s; users have no signal that the count is fresh vs stale.
  - *Fix:* Replace the static pill with a StatusPill or add a small pulsing dot (already in globals as .pill.running style) when loading=true to signal active polling.

**Bulk Discard Expired — Confirm Flow** — Two-step confirm rendered inline in the page-head right slot: first a 'Discard expired (N)' btn.sm, then on click it swaps to a text label + danger Confirm + ghost Cancel trio

- 🟡 **[med/M]** The confirm state renders as a raw flex span with no visual container — it appears as floating text + two buttons with no background or border, visually indistinct from the h1 area. It can be missed, especially on first encounter.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the confirm row in a small alert-warn panel or use the existing Dialog primitive for destructive-action confirmation, consistent with how other bulk actions (e.g. recipe delete) handle it.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The confirmation label ('Discard N expired?') is styled at --fs-s / --ink-2 (12 px, faint) next to a full-height danger button. This violates the visual hierarchy rule that destructive prompts should be the most readable element in their context.
  - *Fix:* Promote the label to --fs-base / --ink-0 or --ink-1 so it reads before the button is clicked.

**Loading State** — SkeletonList rows={6} columns={5} shown when loading && transactions.length === 0

- 🟡 **[med/M]** SkeletonList is a generic table skeleton. The actual page renders cards, not a flat table. The loading skeleton does not match the card-per-transaction layout, causing a jarring layout shift when real data loads.
  - *Fix:* Replace SkeletonList with 2–3 skeleton cards that mirror the .tx-card structure (a card-head bar + a narrow table-area bar). A simple div with a Skeleton height block per card is enough.

**Error States** — ErrorState component used when error && no data; raw .alert-err div used when error && stale data still showing

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The stale-data error banner (line 261) is a raw .alert-err div with a concatenated string 'Refresh failed — {error}'. It lacks an aria role='alert' and does not offer a retry action, making it passive and inaccessible.
  - *Fix:* Use ErrorState with onRetry={refetch} for both error branches, or at minimum add role='alert' to the .alert-err div and wire a small 'Retry' btn.sm inside it.

**Empty State** — EmptyState component with title 'No active transactions' and a code-heavy JSX description explaining beginTransaction / stageEdit / commitTransaction

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The EmptyState description is three sentences of inline JSX with three code tags. EmptyState.description renders inside a <p> with maxWidth 420; the multi-code-tag prose is dense for a passive empty state and the code tokens (beginTransaction, stageEdit, commitTransaction) are tool names unfamiliar to first-time users.
  - *Fix:* Shorten to one sentence ('Nothing staged yet. When an agent stages edits, they appear here for review.') and move the MCP tool names into the HintCard body, which is purpose-built for contextual docs.

**Transaction Card — Header Row (card-head)** — h2 with <code> transaction ID, then a flex row of four pills: staged time, TtlPill, file count, total line delta

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The h2 renders the full transaction ID as <code style='fontSize: var(--fs-base)'> — a long UUID-style string that dominates the card header with no truncation or copy affordance. On narrow viewports the ID and the four pills must share one row (before the media query wraps them) causing overflow.
  - *Fix:* Truncate the ID to the first 8 characters with a title attribute showing the full value, or add a copy-to-clipboard icon. Apply font-size: --fs-s on the code element so the pills share visual weight with the ID.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The left-border status stripe (borderLeft: 3px solid var(--ok/--err)) is set via inline style, diverging from how approval cards use a recess background + inset box-shadow for state. Inline style also overrides on hover because .tx-card:hover does not restore the border-left color explicitly.
  - *Fix:* Move the expired/active stripe to a CSS class (e.g. .tx-card--expired) defined in globals near the .tx-card block. Use a data-expired attribute or conditional class on the card div so the stripe is theme-aware and can transition with the card hover state.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The line-delta pill uses color var(--ok) for positive deltas and var(--err) for negative. Deleting lines (negative delta) is not inherently an error — it is semantically neutral. Using --err here misleads users into thinking line-reduction is a problem.
  - *Fix:* Use a muted pill for negative deltas (e.g. a subtle blue or neutral) and reserve --err for genuinely bad states like expired status. Consider an arrow icon (up/down) instead of color alone for accessibility.

**Transaction Card — Edits Table** — Standard .table inside .table-wrap with four columns: File (mono), Before (bytes), After (bytes), Delta lines (colored mono)

- ⚪ **[low/S]** The 'Before' cell applies both className='mono muted' AND an inline style with fontFamily and fontSize (line 319), duplicating the .table .mono and .table .muted CSS rules. The inline style also sets font-size: --fs-s, making Before smaller than After (.tx-amount = --fs-base), creating an asymmetric column pair that is hard to scan.
  - *Fix:* Remove the inline style from the 'Before' td. Apply a single className='mono muted' and let the table rules handle sizing. Ensure Before and After cells share the same font-size by also applying .tx-amount to the Before td.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** Long file paths (e.g. src/tools/handlers/something/deep/file.ts) overflow the File column with no truncation rule. The table-wrap has horizontal scroll, but the overflow is uncontrolled — the path pushes other columns out of their fixed widths.
  - *Fix:* Add max-width: 0; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; white-space: nowrap on the File td, or clamp it to the leftmost portion of the path (showing the filename + one parent) with a title attribute for the full path.

**Transaction Card — Footer / Discard Action** — A flex row with a .btn.danger 'Discard' button, an inline help sentence with a <code> tag, and an optional state pill shown at margin-left: auto

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The helper sentence ('Commit happens from the agent — call commitTransaction with this ID. Discard is safe; nothing has touched disk.') is repeated verbatim for every card. When there are 5 transactions, this text appears 5 times, adding cognitive noise without adding value after the first read.
  - *Fix:* Move this copy to the HintCard body (already present on the page) or show it once as a page-level note below the page-head. Remove it from the card footer entirely.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The state feedback pill (line 361) shows raw strings like 'discarded', 'error: {message}', 'rolling-back' in a muted pill with margin-left: auto. The error case ('error: network timeout') is plain text in a muted pill — the same visual weight as the 'discarded' success state, with no color differentiation.
  - *Fix:* Use a conditional pill variant: .pill.ok for 'discarded', .pill.err for error states. Trim the error prefix so the pill shows 'Failed: {msg}' in --err-text rather than the raw 'error: ' prefix.
- 🔴 **[high/S]** The Discard button lacks an aria-label that identifies which transaction it targets. A screen reader user navigating a list of three cards hears three identical 'Discard' buttons with no disambiguation.
  - *Fix:* Add aria-label={`Discard transaction ${tx.id}`} (or the truncated ID) to each Discard button.


### Analytics  `/analytics`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the custom useCountUp hook with the existing AnimatedNumber primitive (which already has prefers-reduced-motion support) and swap the '—' loading placeholders for SkeletonStatCard — these two changes kill two bugs and align loading/animation behavior with the rest of the app in under an hour of work.
2. Add a <thead> with visible column headers to the Top tools table — without them the p50/p95 latency columns are discoverable only via hover tooltip, which fails touch users and screen readers entirely.
3. Fix the chart title contrast: 'Calls — last 24 hours' at --fs-2xs (10px) in --ink-3 falls below WCAG AA for informational text — bump to --fs-xs/--ink-2 and replace the 3px color-only legend swatches with labeled shapes for color-vision accessibility.

**Sub-nav (AnalyticsTabs)** — Two-item cluster-tabs nav (Overview / Insights) rendered via layout.tsx above the page content; correct aria-label and aria-current in place.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Tab descriptions (e.g. 'Tool usage & error rates') are only surfaced as native title tooltips, invisible on touch and missed by screen readers unless they hover.
  - *Fix:* Add a visually-hidden <span className='sr-only'> inside each cluster-tab with the description text, or promote the description to a visible subtitle beneath the tab labels using --ink-3 at --fs-xs.

**Page header / hero** — editorial-h1 with decorative serif accent span ('what your agents actually do.'), editorial-sub tagline listing three topics, and a RelationStrip with four cross-links.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The editorial-h1 accent span ('what your agents actually do.') buries the page identity behind decorative copy. Users scanning quickly see 'Analytics —' and then a sentence fragment instead of a concise descriptor.
  - *Fix:* Replace the accent span with a brief, noun-phrase subtitle such as 'Tool Usage & Activity' inline, or move the decorative sentence to the editorial-sub and lead the h1 with 'Analytics' alone — matching the pattern used on the Runs and Recipes pages.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The editorial-sub lists 'tool usage · hook activity · recipe history' — these three topics are exactly what the three stat sections below cover, so the tagline duplicates rather than adds context.
  - *Fix:* Replace with a single actionable context string like 'Last 24 hours — auto-refreshes every 30s' so users understand the data window without scrolling to the stat card footers.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The RelationStrip has four links (Recipes, Runs, Activity, Insights) but 'Insights' is already reachable via the AnalyticsTabs sub-nav immediately above — the link is redundant and adds visual noise.
  - *Fix:* Remove 'Insights' from the RelationStrip; it is already the sibling tab. Keep Recipes, Runs, and Activity.

**Error / partial-error banner** — Full ErrorState shown when error && !data; a raw <div className='alert-err'> shown when error && data (stale-data refresh failure).

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stale-refresh banner at line 206 renders the raw error string with 'Refresh failed — {error}' but the error is typed as unknown — on a network failure it might be '[object Object]' rather than a readable message.
  - *Fix:* Coerce to string: `error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)` before interpolation, matching how ErrorState already does it internally.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The alert-err div has no role='alert' or aria-live region, so screen readers do not announce the refresh failure when it appears mid-session while the user is already on the page.
  - *Fix:* Add role='alert' aria-live='polite' to the alert-err div.

**Stat row (KPI cards)** — Four StatCards (Total tool calls, Unique tools, Hooks fired, Error rate) in a stat-grid; count-up animation via custom useCountUp hook; icon slots filled with inline-style div wrappers housing raw SVGs.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The page re-implements its own useCountUp hook (lines 65-88) with a 600ms cubic ease, while the reusable AnimatedNumber component already exists in /components/patchwork/AnimatedNumber.tsx with prefers-reduced-motion support, flash-on-change, and a 1200ms default. The local hook lacks the reduced-motion guard present in the shared primitive.
  - *Fix:* Replace useCountUp + animatedCalls/animatedTools/animatedHooks with <AnimatedNumber value={totalCalls} /> etc. inside each StatCard's value prop. Remove the local hook entirely.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** StatCard loading state renders a literal '—' string (e.g. value={loading ? '—' : animatedCalls.toLocaleString()}). The SkeletonStatCard primitive already exists and gives a proper shimmer placeholder.
  - *Fix:* When loading and !data, render four <SkeletonStatCard /> in a stat-grid instead of StatCards with '—' placeholders.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The icon slot for each StatCard uses a verbose inline-style div (width, height, borderRadius, background, display, alignItems, justifyContent, color all as inline styles) repeated four times. If this pattern is already used elsewhere, it should be a shared IconBubble helper; if not, the redundancy makes theming harder.
  - *Fix:* Extract a tiny IconBubble component (or a CSS class like .stat-icon-bubble) that accepts a color token and children, cutting each icon slot from 5 style props to 1-2. Light-theme contrast of the orange icon bubble (rgba(--orange-rgb, 0.12) background) should also be verified — it may wash out on --bg-1.

**Area chart (Calls — last 24 hours)** — AreaChart in a plain .card div with an inline chart legend (orange=runs, red=errors) and a gradient-skeleton placeholder while clientNow===0.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The chart title 'Calls — last 24 hours' at line 274 uses --fs-2xs (10px) in --ink-3, which is below WCAG AA minimum for informational text. At this size the label is effectively invisible on dark-theme surfaces.
  - *Fix:* Bump the chart title to --fs-xs (11px) minimum and use --ink-2 instead of --ink-3 for the label. Consider promoting it to --fs-s (12px) to match other section headers.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The legend swatch is a 3px-tall colored bar (height:3), making it nearly invisible and indistinguishable for users with color-vision deficiencies. There is no textual or shape differentiation between the 'runs' and 'errors' series beyond color alone.
  - *Fix:* Replace the 3px bar swatch with an 8x8px rounded square or use different dash patterns. Add a screen-reader label: <span className='sr-only'>runs series in orange, errors series in red</span> next to the legend.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The skeleton placeholder for the chart (lines 286-294) is a gradient div with opacity:0.3 that renders while clientNow===0 on first mount. The standard Skeleton primitive would match the site's shimmer style. The 150ms chartVisible delay also adds a visible pop-in for users with fast devices.
  - *Fix:* Replace the custom gradient div with <Skeleton height={140} /> from the Skeleton component. Consider whether the 150ms stagger delay is worth the jarring entrance — reduce to 0ms or remove it.

**Top tools table** — Headerless <tbody>-only table of up to 15 tools showing ToolChip, an inline bar, call count, error count, p50, and p95; cells sized and spaced via inline styles throughout.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The table has no <thead> and no visible column headers. Users cannot tell whether the last two numeric columns are latency percentiles without hovering to see the title tooltip ('p50 latency', 'p95 latency'). Tooltips are not accessible on touch or for keyboard users.
  - *Fix:* Add a <thead><tr> with column headers: Tool, Usage, Calls, Errors, p50, p95 — styled with the same .table thead th pattern used by the Recent recipe tasks table directly below. The header row can be visually lighter (--ink-3, --fs-xs uppercase) so it doesn't compete with data.
- 🟡 **[med/M]** All cell sizing is done with inline styles (padding, fontSize, fontFamily, color, whiteSpace, textAlign repeated per-td across 15 rows * 6 cells). This bypasses the .table CSS class used by the tasks table immediately below, making future theming changes require touching JSX instead of CSS.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the top-tools table in className='table' and move repeated per-cell styles to CSS under a .anl-tools-table selector. At minimum share the .mono and .muted className conventions already used in the tasks table.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The error count cell renders '{t.errors} err' for every row including 0-error tools, creating visual clutter ('0 err' in --ink-3 across most rows). The 'err' label suffix is redundant given column context once a header is added.
  - *Fix:* Render '—' when t.errors === 0 (matching the fmtDuration pattern) and drop the 'err' suffix from the non-zero case once a column header names the field.

**Top tools loading / empty state** — SkeletonList rows=5 columns=3 shown while loading; EmptyState shown when topTools.length===0 with context-sensitive description.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** SkeletonList renders 3 columns but the actual table has 6 columns (tool name, bar, calls, errors, p50, p95). The skeleton proportions do not match the real layout, causing a jarring layout shift when data arrives.
  - *Fix:* Pass columns={6} to SkeletonList, or better, render skeleton rows inside a matching table structure so column widths match.

**Section headers ('Top tools', 'Recent recipe tasks')** — Both use a <div className='page-head'> wrapper around a bare <h2>, matching top-of-page heading treatment with the same heavy structural element used for the page title.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Wrapping a mid-page <h2> in page-head (which has its own margin, border, and flex layout) adds visual weight and spacing that the top-level h1 uses appropriately but which is excessive for in-page section dividers. It creates the impression of a new page starting rather than a new section.
  - *Fix:* Replace the page-head wrapper on the h2 section dividers with a lighter pattern: plain <h2 style={{ marginTop: 'var(--s-8)', marginBottom: 'var(--s-3)' }}> or a shared .section-heading class, consistent with how other data pages handle sub-section breaks.

**Recent recipe tasks table** — Standard .table with thead (Time, Name/ID, Status, Duration); taskStatusPill() renders inline <span className='pill ok|err|muted'>; shows only when recentTasks.length > 0 (conditionally absent).

- 🟡 **[med/S]** taskStatusPill() at lines 54-62 reimplements StatusPill logic inline using raw className='pill ok|err|muted' spans. The shared StatusPill component already handles these exact three tones (ok, err, muted) with consistent chip styling and deriveRunStatus() for the done/completed/error/failed mapping.
  - *Fix:* Replace the taskStatusPill function with <StatusPill tone={status === 'done' || status === 'completed' ? 'ok' : status === 'error' || status === 'failed' ? 'err' : 'muted'}>{status}</StatusPill> or call deriveRunStatus() to normalize status strings before rendering.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** When the section is empty (recentTasks.length === 0) there is no empty state rendered — the entire section disappears silently. A user who expects to see automation task history gets no feedback about whether tasks exist but are loading, or genuinely absent.
  - *Fix:* Always render the 'Recent recipe tasks' section header and, when empty, show an <EmptyState title='No automation tasks yet' description='Tasks appear here when automation hooks trigger recipe runs.' />.
- ⚪ **[low/M]** The Name/ID column shows task.id.slice(0,8) as a dimmed aside when task.name is present, but neither name nor ID is a link. Users cannot navigate from a task row to its full run detail.
  - *Fix:* Wrap the task name/id in a link to /runs?task={task.id} or the appropriate run detail route, using the existing RunChip entity chip if applicable.


### Approval Insights  `/insights`

**Top 3:**
1. Replace the three floating summary pill-links (decisions/trusted/rejected) in the page-head with StatCard components — eliminates the empty-column layout shift during load and gives the counts proper label context and visual weight.
2. Add a numeric approval-rate percentage beside the visual bar in the Rate column — the 80px bar at current width is too narrow to read relative differences and the column header 'Rate' has no numeric anchor for users sorting by it.
3. Add sr-only text labels and scope='col' to the ✓ and ✗ column headers, and a table caption — the single-glyph headers are inaccessible to screen readers, and namespaced tool names in the Tool column need ellipsis truncation to prevent horizontal overflow on sub-900px viewports.

**Cluster sub-nav (DecisionsTabs)** — DecisionsTabs rendered at the top of the section with no visual separation from the page-head below it.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** No bottom margin between DecisionsTabs and the page-head block, so the tab strip and the h1 read as a single undifferentiated column with no breathing room.
  - *Fix:* Add `marginBottom: 'var(--s-4)'` on the DecisionsTabs wrapper (or a wrapping div) to create a clear visual break before the editorial-h1 — consistent with how ActivityTabs is spaced on /activity.

**Page header (editorial-h1, subtitle, RelationStrip, summary pills)** — Left column has editorial h1 with italic serif accent + plain-text subtitle + RelationStrip cross-links; right column has three summary pill-links (decisions/trusted/rejected) and a Replay button.

- 🔴 **[high/S]** The editorial-h1 accent span reads 'how the bridge reads your decisions.' — a decorative italic tagline that buries the page's actual signal. Users scanning for '97 rejections' have to parse sentence prose to find the three stat pills on the right.
  - *Fix:* Replace the italic accent with a short keyword phrase (e.g. 'Tool approval history') and move it to a plain span with --ink-2. The three summary pills already carry the aggregate signal — the h1 should orient, not narrate.
- 🔴 **[high/M]** The three summary pills (decisions / trusted / rejected) are bare pill-links floating in a flex row with no label context. 'trusted' and 'rejected' refer to tool counts, but a user landing here for the first time cannot distinguish them from call counts.
  - *Fix:* Replace the three ad-hoc pill-links with StatCard components (or SkeletonStatCard during load) — label: 'Decisions', 'Trusted tools', 'Rejected tools', value: the count. This also eliminates the loading gap where data is null and the right column is empty.
- ⚪ **[low/S]** The .editorial-sub override `fontFamily: 'inherit'` is redundant — globals.css (line 2390) already sets .editorial-sub to --font-sans after the theme redesign. The inline override is dead code that will confuse future editors.
  - *Fix:* Remove the `style={{ fontFamily: 'inherit' }}` prop from the editorial-sub div.

**Tool filter banner (active when ?tool= param is set)** — A manually-styled info banner with inline styles: bg-2 background, line-2 border, r-2 radius, shows filtered tool name with a Clear button.

- ⚪ **[low/S]** Uses `--r-2` (aliased to 6px) which is the same as `--r-s` but references a non-canonical alias not used anywhere else in the design system. Also, the entire banner is hand-styled rather than using a system class.
  - *Fix:* Replace `var(--r-2)` with `var(--r-s)` to use the canonical small-radius token. Consider wrapping in the existing `.alert-err`-style pattern or a `.filter-banner` utility class to avoid inline styles accumulating.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The banner has no dismiss icon (only a 'Clear' text button with no visible affordance), and no aria-live announcement when it appears or disappears. Screen-reader users get no feedback when the filter changes.
  - *Fix:* Add `role='status'` and `aria-live='polite'` to the banner div so filter state changes are announced. Optionally add a × icon to the Clear button for visual clarity.

**Loading state** — SkeletonList with rows=6 and columns=5 is shown inside the Suspense boundary and also inline when loading and tools.length === 0.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The Suspense fallback and the inline `loading && tools.length === 0` guard both render SkeletonList — two independent render paths for the same visual. If both trigger simultaneously, two skeleton lists stack.
  - *Fix:* Remove the duplicate `{loading && tools.length === 0 && <SkeletonList ... />}` conditional (line 341) and rely solely on the Suspense fallback, or move the loading check inside InsightsContent above the data-dependent render and remove the Suspense fallback.
- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stat pills in the page-head are hidden (data is null) during load, leaving the right column of the page-head empty — a jarring layout shift when data arrives.
  - *Fix:* Render SkeletonStatCard placeholders in the right column header during load so the layout is stable. This is especially visible since the page-head uses align-items: flex-end and an empty right column collapses.

**Error state (stale-data inline alert)** — Full error (no data): uses ErrorState component correctly. Refresh-failed (has stale data): bare .alert-err div with string interpolation of the error value.

- 🟡 **[med/S]** The stale-refresh error `<div className='alert-err'>Refresh failed — {error}</div>` exposes the raw error string directly inline. If the bridge returns a verbose stack trace, it overflows the card and leaks internal details to the user.
  - *Fix:* Cap the error display: render a fixed message ('Refresh failed — retrying') and log the full error only to console. Optionally add a manual retry button using the existing `refetch` callback, which is already threaded through but not surfaced here.

**Empty state** — EmptyState component with title and a long backtick-quoted description mentioning `patchwork suggest`.
